# Trailing Stop Order | Aster

A **Trailing Stop Order** is a type of stop order that automatically adjusts with the market when the price moves in your favor. It helps you lock in gains without having to manually update your stop.

Instead of setting a fixed stop price, you set a **callback rate** — a percentage that tells the system how far the market must reverse before your order is triggered.

When the price moves in your favor, the stop price follows it. If the price reverses by the callback rate, a **market order** is triggered to close your position.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/order-types/trailing-stop-order#how-it-works)

How it works

*   **Callback rate**: The percentage used to trail the current market price.
    
    *   Example: A 2% callback rate means the stop price stays 2% behind the highest (or lowest) price reached after the order is placed.
        
    
*   **For long positions**:
    
    *   The stop price moves up as the market rises.
        
    *   If the price falls by the callback rate, a **market sell** is triggered.
        
    
*   **For short positions**:
    
    *   The stop price moves down as the market falls.
        
    *   If the price rises by the callback rate, a **market buy** is triggered.
        
    

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/order-types/trailing-stop-order#example-1-long-position-on-btc)

Example 1 (long position on BTC)

*   **Entry price**: $95,000
    
*   **Callback rate**: 2%
    

If BTC rises to **$100,000**, the trailing stop price moves up to **$98,000** (2% below the peak).

If the price then falls to **$98,000**, your stop triggers a **market sell**, closing the position and locking in profit.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/order-types/trailing-stop-order#example-2-short-position-on-btc)

Example 2 (short position on BTC)

*   **Entry price**: $105,000
    
*   **Callback rate**: 2%
    

If BTC falls to **$100,000**, the trailing stop moves down with it, staying 2% above — now at **$102,000**.

If the price then rebounds to **$102,000**, your stop triggers a **market buy**, closing the short position to secure profit before the price climbs further.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/order-types/trailing-stop-order#when-to-use-it)

When to use it

*   To automatically **protect profits** when the market moves in your favor
    
*   To **let your trade run** while still having a dynamic exit
    
*   As a smarter alternative to fixed stop-losses
    

[PreviousHidden Order](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/order-types/hidden-order)
[NextGrid trading](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/grid-trading)

# How to create an API | Aster

1\. Go to [API management](https://www.asterdex.com/en/api-management)
 and connect your wallet. Then, click \[Create API\].

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252Fowf1h0db8limUqi4sV29%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-04-02%252014.45.27.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8c490f4f-c3ff-436b-b012-63c146d98270&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ce7435bc&sv=2)

2\. Enter your preferred label for the API key you want to create, then click \[Create API\].

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FsBgfWDruopgoKdBpVouV%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-04-02%252014.46.44.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8cf8b99b-017a-438c-80f1-363984f421e3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f8c9d886&sv=2)

3\. After creation, you’ll receive the API key and secret key. Click the “copy” icon to copy them and store them in a secure location.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F5UbZBpB5XDJWn57qK74i%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-04-02%252014.47.31.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D031b2882-7e87-4fdf-944f-d459f8e6a318&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=61b8294e&sv=2)

**Note:**

*   The secret key is only visible when the API key is first created. After that, it will be masked and cannot be viewed again.
    
*   Be sure to copy and store the secret key securely right after creating it.
    
*   If you lose your secret key, you’ll need to delete the API key and create a new one.
    
*   Do not share your API key or secret key with anyone to avoid potential losses.
    
*   It’s recommended to bind your API key to a fixed IP address to enhance account security.
    
*   You can view and manage your API keys in [API management](https://www.asterdex.com/en/api-management)
    .
    
*   Each account can create up to 30 API keys.
    

[PreviousAPI](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/api)
[NextAPI documentation](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/api/api-documentation)

# Deposit & Withdrawal Guide | Aster

**Supported Assets on Aster DEX**

Aster DEX currently supports these spot assets on Binance Smart Chain (BSC):

*   ASTER: Aster’s native token
    
*   APX: Legacy token, exchangeable for ASTER
    
*   USDT, USD1, BTC, ETH, FORM, CDL
    

Switch networks and click the ticker icon to view the full list of supported assets.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FINCkQv4aEjrCYVV2D1lj%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-19%252009.02.02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1f2bd753-ee0f-4cc6-a801-ebf3bbf03603&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b082ae99&sv=2)

**Deposit & Withdrawal Guide (from/to CEX and Wallets)**

**Deposit**

Option A: Deposit from CEX

1\. Log in to your CEX account (e.g. Binance, OKX).

2\. Go to Withdraw, select your token, and choose the correct network (e.g. USDT on BEP-20).

3\. Copy your Aster Spot USDT deposit address (found in Aster Web/App under Account → Deposit).

4\. Paste the address in the CEX withdrawal page.

5\. Enter the amount and confirm the withdrawal.

6\. Your USDT should arrive in your Aster Spot account within a few minutes.

Option B: Deposit from an on-chain wallet (MetaMask, Trust Wallet, etc.)

1\. Open your wallet and connect it to the BSC network.

2\. Go to Send → select your token and network, such as USDT (BEP-20).

3\. Copy your Aster Spot USDT deposit address (found in Aster Spot Web/App under Account → Deposit).

4\. Paste the address, enter the amount, and confirm the transaction.

5\. After the transaction is confirmed on the blockchain, your funds will appear in your Aster Spot account.

⚠️ Always double-check that both the network and the address are correct before confirming any transfer.

* * *

**Withdrawals**

From Aster Spot back to CEX or Wallet

1\. On Aster App, go to Assets → Withdraw. On Aster Web, go to Perpetuals or Spot and click Withdraw under Account (bottom-right).

2\. Select your token.

3\. Enter the destination address (your CEX or on-chain wallet deposit address).

4\. Enter the withdrawal amount.

5\. Confirm the transaction.

6\. Your funds will be sent on BSC and should arrive within minutes, depending on network speed.

⚠️ Always double-check that both the network and the address are correct before confirming any transfer.

[PreviousAster Spot](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-spot)
[NextTrading $CDL on Aster](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-spot/trading-usdcdl-on-aster)

# Support Center | Aster

Sometimes you may encounter problems with your orders on Aster. These generally fall into two categories:

**Order not executing**

*   Check the order price in the Open Orders section and confirm whether it has matched a counterparty’s bid or ask at that price and volume.
    
*   If the order is not filled, you can:
    
*   Cancel it from the Open Orders section and place a new order at a more competitive price.
    
*   Use a market order for faster settlement.
    

**Other order-related issues**

For issues such as being unable to cancel an order or coins not being credited to your account, please [submit a ticket in Discord](https://discord.gg/invite/asterdefi)
 with the following information:

*   Screenshot of the order
    
*   Screenshot of the error message or issue
    

[PreviousPost Only & TIF](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-spot/post-only-and-tif)
[NextVIP Program](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/vip-program)

Apply here: [https://forms.gle/7iwxjFw38ojiyVJu6](https://t.co/D5pP0aImqm)

\*Requests that meet the criteria will be reviewed and approved within a few days. The rate will be adjusted automatically after approval, without further notice. **After adjustment for affiliates:**

*   You’ll receive 20% commission from referred users who are VIP 1.
    
*   You’ll receive 10% commission from referred users who are VIP 2 or above.
    

Invite your friends to join Aster and start earning together. Our referral program rewards you when they trade on [Aster Perpetual](https://www.asterdex.com/en/futures/v1/ASTERUSDT)
.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/referral-program#how-it-works)

**How it works**

*   Generate your referral link on the [Referral page](https://www.asterdex.com/en/referral)
    .
    
*   Share your link with friends.
    
*   Earn with our special **10%** commission link! Customize your sharing strategy. For example:
    
    *   **Invite Friends and Earn**: Get 5% commission for each trade your referred friends make.
        
    *   **Give Back to Your Friends**: Your friends also earn 5% from their trades!

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/referral-program#terms)

Terms

*   Rebate rates are calculated daily at 00:00 (UTC) and updated at 09:00 (UTC).
    
*   Referral reward relationships last for **365 days** by default.
    
*   **Liquidation fees** are excluded from referral commissions.
    
*   **Self-trade and zero fee trade volumes** are excluded from the calculation of referral commissions .
    
*   There is no limit to the number of people you can invite.
    
*   Only new users who sign up using your referral link are eligible.
    
*   Self-referrals (creating multiple accounts to invite yourself) are not allowed. If detected, all referral rewards will be revoked and commissions canceled.
    
*   Offensive, misleading, or harmful custom referral codes may result in removal from the program and cancellation of commissions.
    
*   The referrer acts independently and is responsible for understanding the risks and legal implications of promoting leveraged or futures trading in their region.
    
*   Aster may extend the validity period of referrals at its discretion.
    
*   Aster reserves the right to modify rebate rates, program rules, or cancel the referral program at any time.
    
*   Aster also reserves the right to interpret the terms of the program.
    

[PreviousMarket Maker Program](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/market-maker-program)
[NextAPI](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/api)

# Order types | Aster

In 1001x, the following order types are available:

**Market order**

A market order is a buy or sell order that is executed immediately at the best available price in the market.

**Limit order**

A limit order allows you to set a specific price at which you want to buy or sell. The order will only be executed if the market price reaches your specified limit price.

*   **Limit buy order:** Executed when the market price reaches or falls below your specified price.
    
*   **Limit sell order:** Executed when the market price reaches or rises above your specified price.
    

Note: There is no guarantee that a limit order will be filled.

**Take profit order**

A take profit order is a type of limit order that closes an open position at a specified price to secure profits.

**Stop loss order**

A stop loss order is designed to limit potential losses by closing an open position at a specified price.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple/order-types#important-considerations)

Important considerations

*   **Fees:** Both an opening fee and an execution fee are charged when a position is opened. These fees are factored into the leverage amount.
    
*   **Order execution:** Trade orders may not be executed even if the target price is reached due to the following reasons:
    
    1.  **Mark price discrepancy:** The mark price, which is an aggregated price from various exchanges, did not reach the target price.
        
    2.  **Insufficient time at target price:** The target price was reached but did not remain at that level long enough for the order to be executed.
        
    3.  **Order size exceeds available open interest** (the total size of all open positions in that direction): your order may not be filled if it’s larger than what the market can support.
        
    

[PreviousManage your positions](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple/manage-your-positions)
[NextInteract with the contract directly](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple/interact-with-the-contract-directly)

Last updated 3 months ago

# AFEE & BonusUSD | Aster

Aster has launched a new fee discount token called AFEE, allowing users to offset their trading fees on Pro Mode. AFEE is applied automatically and does not require any manual activation. Please note that AFEE cannot be used as margin to open positions; users are required to deposit USDT or other collateral assets to trade.

1 AFEE is equivalent to 1 USDT, and the total supply is 100,000 AFEE tokens.

**Note**

*   When users use AFEE to offset trading fees, both market makers and referrers will receive AFEE tokens as rebates.
    
*   AFEE can only be used to offset trading fees; it cannot be used to deduct funding rates, liquidation fees, or other costs.
    
*   Users do not need to enable multi-asset mode to utilize AFEE.
    

Aster has launched a futures bonus token (BONUSUSD) for users who trade on [Aster Pro Mode](https://www.asterdex.com/en/futures/v1/BTCUSDT)
. BONUSUSD is a futures bonus token issued by Aster. BONUSUSD is a unique USD-pegged token which traders can use as collateral to trade crypto futures on [Aster Pro Mode](https://www.asterdex.com/en/futures/v1/BTCUSDT)
!

_Note: BONUSUSD is a futures bonus token and cannot be withdrawn._ [_Multi-assets mode_](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/asterex-pro-mode/muti-single-asset-margin)
 _has to be activated to use BONUSUSD as collateral._

# Pre-launch contracts | Aster

Pre-launch markets allow users to trade token pairs before they are officially listed on major exchanges. They are based on an expiry futures contracts, but can also take the form of a perpetual futures contract. Once the token is launched and starts trading on cryptocurrency exchanges, the pre-market symbol on Aster Perpetual will convert to a regular perpetual futures contract.

Aster has the right to proceed with the delivery process of the token automatically when the token is launched on an external exchange, or when tokenomics about the token are released. The pre-market mode will be switched to a perpetual contract automatically.

_**Aster has the final right to interpret the delivery price or delist the contract.**_

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/pre-launch-contracts#mark-price-pre-launch-market-usdt-margined-futures-contracts)

Mark Price (pre-launch market USDT-margined futures contracts)

We use Mark Price to avoid unnecessary liquidations for traders and to prevent market manipulation. The “Price Index,” which is the primary component of the Mark Price, is an average of the prices on major mainstream markets. The calculation of Pre-Launch Market Index price is different from regular perpetual futures contracts.

The Mark Price formula for Pre-Launch Market USDT-M Futures Contracts is as follows:

(1) Mark Price = Median × (Price 1 , Price 2 , Contract Price)

(2) Price 1 = ( Bid 1 + Ask 1) / 2 × (1 + Funding Rate × (Time to Next Funding Rate (h)/8 ))

(3) Price 2 = ( Bid 1 + Ask 1) / 2

\*Bid 1 & Ask 1 price are from the Pre-Market order book.

\*Price 2: We will update the logic of Price 2 according to the market situation.

\*Median: The middle price out of Price 1, Price 2, and the Contract Price is taken as the median. For example, if Price 1 < Price 2 < Contract Price, then Price 2 is taken as the Mark Price.

\*Bid 1 & Ask 1 price are from the Pre-Market order book.

\*Price 2: We will update the logic of Price 2 according to the market situation

After the Pre-Market Symbol changes to a regular perpetual futures contract, the index price will be switched to the perpetual future’s index calculation as well.

**Mark Price (USD-margined perpetual futures contracts)**

[![Logo](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1746456893-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Forganizations%252F4RpBC0lt3dm006b0Rt67%252Fsites%252Fsite_kfV5r%252Ficon%252FNT0NjiB0Torv57PEjTso%252Fblack-color.svg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29011997-dc1f-4c3f-a9bd-d6f76d321ff4&width=48&height=48&sign=fe4130d2&sv=2)Mark price | Asterdocs.asterdex.com](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/asterex-pro/mark-price)

Aster Pro **liquidation** protocol:

[![Logo](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1746456893-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Forganizations%252F4RpBC0lt3dm006b0Rt67%252Fsites%252Fsite_kfV5r%252Ficon%252FNT0NjiB0Torv57PEjTso%252Fblack-color.svg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29011997-dc1f-4c3f-a9bd-d6f76d321ff4&width=48&height=48&sign=fe4130d2&sv=2)Liquidations | Asterdocs.asterdex.com](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/asterex-pro/liquidations)

# Auto grid trading guide | Aster

1.  Navigate to the right sidebar of the Futures Grid trading interface. On the \[Auto\] tab, verify the recommended parameters and set up your \[Initial Margin\].
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FKmCqWttJsjbvHYZA0z7O%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-05-15%252017.26.38.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc7877ff5-9bb7-4e0d-85da-183a3e4231c2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9b3adf58&sv=2)

2\. Once you have decided the amount of margin that you want to allocate to your grid trading strategy, click \[Create\], and confirm your grid order so the system automatically places buy or sell orders at the preset prices.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FjMSpalWPHjBK2Dzt31E6%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-05-15%252017.27.03.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5f5a659a-04b9-4165-b618-7c5d1c0b8027&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8647ba47&sv=2)

Please be aware that the auto parameters function will not work when there is not enough trading history on a given asset. Under such circumstances, you will have to set the parameters manually or click \[Copy parameters to Manual settings\] to modify the lower price, upper price, and grid number.

How are auto parameters calculated?

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/grid-trading/auto-grid-trading-guide#a398)

Upper & Lower Price

*   Upper Band = MA + bbm \* Standard Deviation
    
*   Lower Band = MA — bbm \* Standard Deviation
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/grid-trading/auto-grid-trading-guide#id-5684)

Grid Number

Grid Number = (grid\_upper\_limit — grid\_lower\_limit)/ATR

\*Average True Range (ATR) for the past pre-defined hours of the selected symbol

**Risk Reminder:** Grid trading as a strategic trading tool should not be regarded as financial or investment advice from Aster. If the grid setting is unreasonable, you will not be able to get the relevant grid revenue when the market enters the one-sided market and is not inside the grid interval you set. You can adjust the grid strategy according to the current market conditions. Grid trading is used at your discretion and at your own risk. Aster will not be liable to you for any loss that might arise from your use of the feature. It is recommended that users should read and fully understand the Grid Trading Tutorial and make risk control and rational trading within your financial ability.

[PreviousManual grid trading guide](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/grid-trading/manual-grid-trading-guide)
[NextLong/short grid trading](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/grid-trading/long-short-grid-trading)

Last updated 6 months ago

# Manual grid trading guide | Aster

1.  After onnecting your wallet, hover over **More** in the top menu and click on \[[Grid Trade](https://www.asterdex.com/en/strategy/futures/grid/BTCUSDT)\
    \].
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FUoldNNVcZUg8h3lFm8Ut%252FScreenshot%25202025-08-26%2520at%252013.03.11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D103f44ae-1828-431d-a0a2-5085c2366773&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2c4ef4a2&sv=2)

1.  Grid Trading Mechanism
    

The grid trading life cycle:

1.  Grid Trigger (optional)
    
2.  Initial structure
    
3.  Open position
    
4.  Grid Update
    
5.  Stop Trigger (optional)
    
6.  Cancellation
    

Grid Trading life cycle

Description

Grid Trigger (optional)

Users can choose to start grid limit orders immediately or choose to trigger when the market price reaches a certain value. The grid orders will be triggered when the chosen trigger price (Last price or Mark price) rises above or falls below the trigger price you enter.

Initial structure

The initial structure is to determine a series of price levels, according to the latest market price (buy, sell, mid-price), place sell limit orders at a price higher than the market price, and a buy limit order at a price lower than the market price, and wait for the price to be triggered.Note that the number of limit orders is the number of grids +1 at the time of initial construction because no positions are held. One of them (the one near the latest market price) is the initial opening order waiting to be executed

Open position

For neutral grids, the strategy will begin with no initial position. The initial position will be triggered when the market trades beyond the nearest price point after the initial construction.

Grid Update

Initial sell orders for the neutral grid will be placed above the current market price. Meanwhile, the buy orders will be populated below the current market price. Do note that the price nearest to the market price would be excluded

Setting a Stop Trigger (optional）

Users can choose to manually terminate grid operation or to set Stop Trigger.Stop Trigger means that when the market price rises above Stop\_upper\_limit or falls below Stop\_lower\_limit i.e. the market is no longer following a swinging trend, the grid will stop its operation.

Order Cancellation

Users can choose whether to cancel all orders and close all positions manually or automatically after the grid is stopped.When 'cancel all orders' on stop is enabled, the system will automatically cancel all the unfilled orders for the symbol when the grid is stopped; When close all positions on stop is enabled, the system will automatically close all the open positions at the market price for the symbol when the grid is stopped

Grid creation may fail in the following situations:

*   You are already running a grid strategy on the selected trading pair.
    
*   You have open orders or positions on the selected symbol.
    
*   You are in hedge mode; please switch to one-way mode in trading settings.
    
*   You have exceeded the limit of 10 active or pending grid strategies.
    

A grid will terminate if any of the following occur:

*   You manually stop the grid.
    
*   Insufficient margin causes positions to be liquidated or prevents orders from being placed.
    
*   You manually cancel some or all grid limit orders.
    
*   You manually close some or all grid positions.
    

[PreviousGrid trading](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/grid-trading)
[NextAuto grid trading guide](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/grid-trading/auto-grid-trading-guide)

Last updated 3 months ago

# Spot Fee Structure | Aster

In appreciation of our users' support, Aster is introducing a VIP program on Aster spot and Aster perpetual. Fees are based on your rolling 14 day volume and are assessed at the end of each day in UTC.

**Spot VIP Tiers**

Tier

**14-days volume in spot or perp (USD)**

**Taker Fee (bps)**

**Maker Fee (bps)**

VIP 1

< 5M

4.0

0.5

VIP 2

\>= $5M

3.5

0.45

VIP 3

\>= $25M

3.3

0.4

VIP 4

\>= $100M

3.0

0

VIP 5

\>= $500M

2.7

0

VIP 6

\>= $1B

2.3

0

**Maker fee**: 0.005%

Example: Buying 0.1 BTC at 100,000 with a maker order → 100,000 × 0.1 × 0.005% = 0.5 USDT

**Taker fee**: 0.04%

Example: Buying 0.1 BTC at 100,000 with a taker order → 100,000 × 0.1 × 0.04% = 4 USDT

The fee structure for current trading pairs, please visit our [Spot Trading](https://www.asterdex.com/en/spot/CDLUSD1)
 page.

**What are maker and taker?**

**Maker:** When you place an order with a set price and quantity that goes into the order book and waits to be filled, you are a maker. Maker orders add liquidity to the market.

**Taker:** When you place an order that matches and executes immediately against an existing order in the book, you are a taker. Taker orders remove liquidity from the market.

**How to use $ASTER to pay spot trading fees and get a 5% discount?**

You can save 5% on spot trading fees when you pay with $ASTER. Simply deposit $ASTER into your spot wallet, and toggle on 'Pay fee in ASTER'. As long as you have $ASTER in your spot wallet and settings toggled on, your $ASTER will be deducted to pay fees first with 5% discount.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FO4ave1hu4zg9CKA6sNpi%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-10-24%252011.07.48.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D990a9914-1561-4eea-835e-8577d4b1997d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7861736a&sv=2)

# Rocket Launch | Aster

Aster is proud to introduce Rocket Launch, the ultimate hub for discovering the latest alpha launches across multiple ecosystems. Rocket Launch aims to transform token launches from one-time market events into a continuous journey that includes early stage user exposure, trading activation with bootstrap liquidity that translates into long term sustainable growth. Participants can earn rewards by trading designated tokens pairs and share the prize pool based on their trading volume.

**How does Rocket Launch work?**

*   Each Rocket Launch campaign features a reward pool composed of both $ASTER tokens and the participating project’s native tokens.
    
*   Projects joining Rocket Launch contribute funds and project tokens, which Aster uses to buy back $ASTER. The repurchased tokens, together with the contributed project tokens, form the campaign reward pool that is distributed to the Aster users through activities.
    

Rocket Launch further showcases Aster’s unique position as one of the few DEXs that offer both Spot and Perpetual markets. By combining token listings and trading competitions across both markets, Aster creates a mutually beneficial ecosystem for projects, traders, and token holders. Projects gain visibility and trading activity; traders gain early access to on-chain opportunities and rewards; Aster strengthens its platform through high-potential listings and trading volume, while ASTER holders benefit from continuous buybacks and long-term value growth.

**How to participate in Rocket Launch?**

*   To qualify for Rocket Launch rewards, participants must meet both trading and holding requirements.
    
*   Users need to reach the minimum required trading volume in the designated Spot or Perpetual pairs and maintain a combined holding of $ASTER across both wallets throughout the campaign. Eligible participants will receive rewards proportionally based on their trading volume share.
    

**From Trading Depth to Ecosystem Growth**

Aster believes that the next phase of growth in DeFi will not be defined solely by fees, liquidity depth, or leverage, but by the ability to discover and capture early on-chain investment opportunities.

The introduction of Rocket Launch reflects this vision, enabling professional traders to access emerging projects at the earliest stage, allowing high-quality teams to be discovered, traded, and validated by the market.

[PreviousTrade & Earn](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/trade-and-earn)
[NextAT/USDT campaign](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/rocket-launch/at-usdt-campaign)

# Order types | Aster

[Aster Pro](https://www.asterdex.com/en/futures/v1/BTCUSDT)
 supports several order types to give traders more control over how and when their trades are executed.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FvpjHVBqEQq789QtzopND%252FOrder%2520panel.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D897d8063-6be4-4a9e-ae01-af60ac9efa41&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9c15dd3c&sv=2)

Aster Pro's order tab

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/order-types#order-types)

Order types

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/order-types#market-order)

Market Order

Executes immediately at the best available price. Used when speed is more important than exact price.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/order-types#limit-order)

Limit Order

Lets you choose the price you want to buy or sell at. The order will only be filled if the market reaches that price or better.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/order-types#stop-limit-order)

Stop Limit Order

Becomes a limit order once a stop price is reached. It will only be filled at the limit price or better. Useful for precise control, but may not fill in fast-moving markets.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/order-types#stop-market-order)

Stop Market Order

Becomes a market order once your stop price is hit. Guarantees execution, but not price — often used to exit quickly during high volatility.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/order-types#trailing-stop-order)

[Trailing Stop Order](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/asterex-pro/trailing-stop-order)

Sets a stop price that follows the market as it moves in your favor. If the price reverses by a set percentage, it triggers a market order.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/order-types#post-only-order)

Post Only Order

Places a limit order that is **only** added to the order book if it doesn't match immediately. If it would execute right away, it's canceled. This is often used to avoid taker fees and ensure maker rebates.

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/order-types#order-modifiers)

Order modifiers

Order modifiers appear just below the fields where you enter your order size and price.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/order-types#tp-sl-take-profit-stop-loss)

TP/SL (Take Profit/Stop Loss)

Optional settings when opening a position:

*   **Take Profit (TP)**: Closes your trade once a target price is reached, securing gains.
    
*   **Stop Loss (SL)**: Closes your trade if the price moves against you, limiting potential losses.
    

You can set TP/SL based on either the [mark price](https://docs.asterdex.com/astherusex-orderbook-perp-guide/mark-price-oracle)
 (**Mark**) or the last traded price (**Last**).

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/order-types#reduce-only)

Reduce-Only

Ensures the order can only decrease or close your position. It won’t open or add to a position. Prevents your position from increasing unintentionally.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/order-types#time-in-force-tif-options)

Time-in-Force (TIF) Options

*   **GTC (Good 'Til Cancelled)**: Order remains open until it is filled or manually cancelled.
    
*   **IOC (Immediate or Cancel)**: Fills as much as possible immediately; cancels any unfilled portion.
    
*   **FOK (Fill or Kill)**: Must be filled completely right away or it is cancelled entirely.
    

[PreviousSingle asset mode & Multi-asset mode](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/single-asset-mode-and-multi-asset-mode)
[NextHidden Order](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/order-types/hidden-order)

Last updated 7 months ago

**How to get trading pair information**

*   **Contract address**: 0x1b6f2d3844c6ae7d56ceb3c3643b9060ba28feb0
    
*   **Method**: ParisV3
    

**Response**:

*   **Parameters**: data (tuple) Tuple: A tuple is an array of values e.g. \[ "0x4sd…","100","100"..\]. It can contain strings, integers, and boolean values. The structure for this tuple is:
    

Copy

    struct OpenDataInput {
            // Pair.base
            address pairBase;
            bool isLong;
            // BUSD/USDT address
            address tokenIn;
            uint256 amountIn;   // tokenIn decimals
            uint256 qty;        // 1e10

            // Market Trade: worst price acceptable
            uint256 price;      // 1e8
            uint256 stopLoss;   // 1e8
            uint256 takeProfit; // 1e8
            uint256 broker;
        }

# Aster app | Aster

Download Aster Mobile by [tapping "Download beta" on the Aster website](https://www.asterdex.com/en)

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-app#how-to-get-started-on-aster-app)

How to get started on Aster app

1.  Tap **Connect wallet** at the top right. Then tap **Connect** again.
    
2.  Select your preferred network.
    
3.  Choose your wallet. If you don’t have one, we recommend creating a [**Trust Wallet**](https://trustwallet.com/?utm_source=cryptwerk)
    .
    
4.  In your wallet app, **approve** the connection request for Aster.
    
5.  Next, **approve** the signature request to complete the connection.
    
6.  You’re connected! You can now start using Aster Mobile.

# Grid trading | Aster

Grid trading on Aster Pro lets you automate your strategy and capture market swings without constant monitoring. By placing buy and sell orders at preset price intervals, you can profit from volatility whether the market is moving up, down, or sideways.

Aster Pro supports three grid strategies: neutral, long, and short. This gives you the flexibility to match your approach to different market conditions. Whether you use auto-generated parameters or set your own, Grid Trading makes it simple to set up, manage, and earn Rh points while trading.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/grid-trading#in-this-section)

In this section

*   [**Set up your grid strategy**](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-pro/grid-trading/set-up-your-grid-trading-strategy)
    
*   [**Auto grid trading guide**](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-pro/grid-trading/futures-grid-trading-auto-parameters-guide)
    
*   [**Long/short grid trading**](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-pro/grid-trading/long-short-grid-trading-introduction)

# Long/short grid trading | Aster

What is long/short Grid Trading?

Long/Short Grid is a trend-following strategy that allows users to trade with the market trend within a grid trading system. This means you can open an initial position (long or short) according to your analysis, while simultaneously placing buy-limit and sell-limit orders at predetermined intervals to capitalize on market volatility and ranging conditions.

For example:

A trader could open an initial long position in BTCUSDT to express his bullish view on Bitcoin and simultaneously placing buy-orders at every $1,000 below the market price of BTCUSDT, while also placing sell-orders at every $1,000 above BTCUSDT contract’s market price. This allows him to trade with the underlying trend within a grid trading system.

A critical difference between a long/short grid and a neutral grid is the initial opening position. For a long grid strategy, users will have an initial long position opened. Conversely, an initial short position will be opened for a short grid strategy.

How to place a Long/Short Grid?

In this example, we will be using BTCUSDT perpetual contract.

1.  Enter the parameters of your long/short grid strategy on the grid trading panel. The key parameters that you must include are:
    

*   The upper and lower boundaries of the price range;
    
*   The number of orders to be placed within the configured price range;
    
*   The width between each grid order;
    
*   Initial margin.
    

If the current market price is greater than the grid trading range, the grid strategy will start with zero position.

1.  Assign the initial margin of the position. The system will calculate your Initial Margin value based on the number of grids, leverage, and the strategy’s price range. Note that the denser the grid, the greater the corresponding initial margin.
    

Please note:

*   Note that the denser the grid, the greater the corresponding initial margin.
    
*   Please note that the notional value for each grid order must be greater than the minimum requirement. Reduce the number of grids or increase the initial margin to ensure that each grid’s minimum notional value is met.
    
*   Insufficient Initial Margin Reminder
    
*   When the initial margin is less than the minimum requirement, a notification will indicate the minimum initial margin required to activate the grid strategy.
    
*   Please ensure that your available balance and maintenance margin is higher than the initial margin to avoid liquidation.
    

1.  Click \[Create\] to place your grid order.
    

Long/Short Grid Profit and Loss Calculation

The profit and loss calculations for a long/short grid strategy consider both the total matched profits and the unmatched profit and loss. In this case, completed transactions are recorded as matched transactions, while partially completed transactions are recorded as unmatched transactions. A matched transaction means that every short position (or long position) in the grid strategy is matched by a corresponding buy order (or sell order).

Index

Definition

Methodology

Unmatched P&L

The profit and loss of unmatched grid transactions

(The latest contract price - unmatched grid pair’s average price) \* Unmatched volume

Total Realized P&L

Total realized Profit & Loss since inception

matched grid income + unmatched grid profit and loss

Yield

Total return ROI

ROI = total profit / initial\_margin \* 100%

Annualized Rate of Return

Annualized Total Return APR

APR = ROI \* year/T, T is the running time of the strategy

Advanced Settings

The Grid trading bot has advanced functions that enable you to better manage positions and risks. One of which is the trigger price. The trigger price is a predetermined price level at which the grid trading bot is activated. This allows you to dictate when the system will be active when market conditions meet your criteria.

When the grid trading bot is triggered, the system will divide the asset price range into several grid pending orders based on your parameters. When the price of an asset falls, the buy-order will be executed, and at the same time, a sell-order will be placed immediately at a higher price level. When the asset price rises, the order will be placed at the lower price level immediately when the sell order is executed. This strategy allows you to buy low, sell high and profit from market fluctuations.

In addition, you can set stop losses for grid positions.Once the price of the asset is below or above the stop loss range, your entire grid position will be closed. This function guarantees that your positions will be protected from huge losses when the market behaves unfavorably.

To monitor trading activity, click the \[Active Grid\] tab to find grid trading details.

To end the grid trading system, click \[Terminate\].

[PreviousAuto grid trading guide](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/grid-trading/auto-grid-trading-guide)
[NextHedge Mode](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/hedge-mode)

Last updated 5 months ago

# FAQs | Aster

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-3-dawn/faqs#q-what-are-rh-points)

Q: What are Rh points?

Rh points are Aster Stage 3 airdrop points for trading on Aster Perpetual and Spot (1001x still does not earn Rh points).

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-3-dawn/faqs#q-how-are-points-calculated)

Q: How are points calculated?

Points = (Trade points +Position points + USDF/asBNB points + Profit points + Loss points) × Team boost + Referral points

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-3-dawn/faqs#q-does-a-higher-score-always-mean-a-bigger-airdrop)

Q: Does a higher score always mean a bigger airdrop?

Aster does not encourage hedging or wash trading to farm points. To ensure fairness, adjustments are applied to farmed points; points shown may not reflect final allocation.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-3-dawn/faqs#q-how-are-trade-points-calculated)

Q: How are trade points calculated?

In Season 3, both spot and perpetuals trading are counted.

Trade Points are now calculated based on your trading fee contribution, liquidity (maker order) contribution and symbol boost factor.Updated hourly.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-3-dawn/faqs#q-what-is-symbol-boost-on-trade-points)

Q:What is Symbol Boost on Trade Points?

It’s a limited-time boost on **Trade Points** for ASTER-designated symbols.

Trade the eligible symbols to receive an extra multiplier on your **Trade Points**

Your **final Trade Points** will be equal to your **previous Trade Points** multiplied by the symbol’s boost factor. Only the Trade Points generated from trading the boosted symbol will receive this multiplier — others will remain unchanged.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-3-dawn/faqs#q-how-are-position-points-calculated)

Q: How are position points calculated?

Based on both the duration and size of your positions. Aster does not encourage long-term hedging positions to farm points. To ensure fairness, adjustments are applied to farmed points; points shown may not reflect final allocation.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-3-dawn/faqs#q-how-are-usdf-asbnb-points-calculated)

Q: How are USDF/asBNB points calculated?

Based on the margin size (only in cross-margin mode) when opening positions each day, and on the proportion of asBNB or USDF in your portfolio. The larger your margin and the higher your share of Aster assets, the more points you earn.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-3-dawn/faqs#q-how-are-profit-and-loss-points-calculated)

Q: How are profit and loss points calculated?

Points are based on your net profit or loss each hour. The timing follows the schedule shown on this page. Do not attempt to game the system by closing offsetting positions right before and after the hourly cutoff to double-count profit and loss points. Doing so may delay your points from being added.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-3-dawn/faqs#q-how-does-the-referral-bonus-work)

Q: How does the referral bonus work?

Earn a share of your invitees’ based on the total points of your invitees and their invitees. Points earned from first-level invitees are higher than those from second-level invitees. Updated daily.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-3-dawn/faqs#q-how-does-team-boost-work)

Q: How does team boost work?

When a team’s cumulative points reach a certain threshold, the team unlocks a boost multiplier. The boost takes effect a few hours after joining a team. In Stage 3, team boosts accumulate throughout the campaign and _**do not reset**_.

[PreviousTeam boosts](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-3-dawn/team-boosts)
[NextAster Harvest :Stage 4](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-4-harvest/aster-harvest-stage-4)

Last updated 7 days ago

# Aster Dawn: Stage 3 | Aster

The new Aster Dawn: Stage 3 introduces new enhancements to reward your trading commitment across both Perpetual and Spot markets.

Building on Stage 2’s emphasis on high quality trading activity, Stage 3 adds Spot trading rewards, symbol-specific boost multipliers, and revised team boost mechanics to maximize your earning potential.

With continuous team boosts and faster activation for new members, collaboration is more rewarding than ever.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-3-dawn/aster-dawn-stage-3#why-trade-on-aster-perpetual-and-spot)

Why Trade on Aster Perpetual and Spot?

Aster Perpetual (Pro mode) offers professional-grade trading with deep liquidity, advanced order types, and leveraged positions up to 100x at competitive fees. Now expanded to include Spot trading rewards, you can earn Rh points from diverse trading strategies on both markets.

Benefits:

*   Low maker (0.005%) and taker (0.04%) fees on Aster Perpetual
    
*   Earn 5% discount by using Aster tokens to pay the trading fee.
    
*   Earn Rh points from Perpetual and Spot trading volumes.
    
*   Rewarding diverse, high-quality trading with Spot inclusion and Symbol-boosters.
    
*   Use of assets like asBNB or USDF for margin increases your rewards.
    
*   Active referral and team programs amplify your earning potential
    
*   Trade like an expert with a full suite of tools and incentives.

# How do Rh points work in Aster Dawn: Stage 3? | Aster

Like in previous stages, Aster continues using Rh points as the core rewards mechanism for Stage 3. Points are calculated on a weekly basis, with each “epoch” running from Monday 00:00 UTC to Sunday 23:59 UTC, unless otherwise stated.

Stage 3 expands the system to reward both Perpetual and Spot trading activity, reflecting a broader range of trading styles and strategies. This updated system continues Aster’s focus on rewarding high quality trading activity, ensuring fairness and encouraging participation throughout the campaign period.

**What are Rh points?**

Rh points are Aster Stage 3 airdrop points for trading on Aster **Perpetual and Spot** (1001x still does not earn Rh points).

**Scoring calculation:**

Final Points = _(Trading points + Position Points + USDF/asBNB points + Profit and Loss Points) x Team boost + Referral points_

_**Note: Weightings are undisclosed.**_

Rh points in Stage 3 are based on a multi-dimensional scoring model, taking into account factors such as:

**Trading Points Score**

*   Trade Points are now calculated based on your trading fee contribution, liquidity (maker order) contribution and symbol boost factor.
    
*   Selected Spot and Perps symbols may boost your trading points.
    
*   Update hourly.
    

**Position Points Score - Only for Perpetual**

*   The larger size and longer time you hold a position, the more Rh points you earn.
    
*   Points caps are not applied anymore on your trading volume.
    
*   Updated on a T+1 basis.
    

**USDF/asBNB Points Score - Only for Perpetual**

*   Earn Rh points by using Aster assets such as asBNB or USDF as margin.
    
*   Points caps are not applied anymore on your used margin value to hold the positions.
    
*   Updated on a T+1 basis.
    

**Profit and Loss Points Points Score - Only for Perpetual**

*   Hourly net profit and loss (excluding fees such as funding fees) contributes to Rh points.
    
*   Updated hourly
    

**Team Boost & Referral Points Score**

*   Team boosts will accumulate throughout Stage 3 and won’t reset during this period.
    
*   Team boosts for new members will take effect in a few hours after joining the team
    
*   Earn a share of your invitees’ based on the total points of your invitees and their invitees.
    
*   Points earned from first-level invitees are higher than those from second-level invitees. Updated daily.
    

Referral score example

*   A invites B, C, and D:
    
*   A earns from B/C/D’s base Rh points (excluding team boosts).
    
*   If B invites C and C invites D (maximum two levels):
    
*   A also earns from C’s base Rh.
    

Base Rh points include trading points score, positions points score, Aster asset holding score, and net PnL score.

_**Note**_

_While the exact formulas and weightings remain undisclosed, all factors above are calculated weekly to determine Rh points. These points accumulate toward your $ASTER airdrop share at the end of Stage 3._

**Terms & Conditions**

*   Market Makers who are participating in the dedicated MM Program cannot earn Rh points.
    
*   After the end of each cycle, Aster may adjust the rules according to user feedback and market conditions. Rh points will be released non-linearly.
    
*   Only participants who meet all the requirements will be considered as a qualified user.
    
*   The Rh points are limited to only one entry per user; bot registered accounts will not be eligible for rewards
    
*   Aster reserves the right to disqualify trades that are deemed to be wash trades, displaying attributes of market manipulation, bulk-account registrations to farm additional bonuses, or any other attempts at fraud.
    
*   Aster reserves the right to cancel or amend any Activity or Activity Rules at our sole discretion.
    
*   Aster reserves the right of final interpretation of this activity.
    

Risk warning: Crypto futures trading carries a substantial risk. All trading activities are done at your discretion and at your own risk. The information here should not be regarded as financial or investment advice from Aster. Aster will not be liable for any loss that might arise from your use of Aster.

[NextRh Points Calculation Scenarios](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-3-dawn/rh-points-calculation-scenarios)

# Delistings | Aster

To maintain a healthy trading environment, Aster Pro may delist certain perpetual futures contracts based on factors like low liquidity or low trading volume. The delisting process is designed to be transparent and timely.

This article outlines the delisting process, including timelines, restrictions, and settlement behavior.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/delistings#reasons-for-delisting)

Reasons for delisting

A futures contract may be delisted due to one or more of the following:

*   Low liquidity or trading volume
    
*   Project operations cease
    
*   Major changes to the underlying blockchain (e.g. hard fork)
    
*   Other factors that negatively affect the trading experience
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/delistings#delisting-process)

Delisting process

1.  Announcement
    
    A delisting notice will be issued on [Twitter](https://x.com/Aster_DEX)
    , [Medium](https://medium.com/asterdex)
    , [Telegram](https://t.me/AsterDEX)
    , and [Discord](https://discord.gg/invite/asterdefi)
     at least 24 hours in advance. The announcement will include the cessation of trading date and any relevant instructions for users.
    
2.  Reduce-only window
    
    Starting 10 minutes before the cessation of trading, users can only place reduce-only orders for the affected contract. New positions cannot be opened during this time.
    
3.  Final mark price calculation
    
    During the last hour before trading stops, the _mark price_ of the delisted contract is calculated as the average of the price index every second over that hour — a total of 3,600 data points.
    
4.  Trading halt and settlement
    
    At the time of delisting:
    
    *   All remaining open positions will be automatically closed at the final mark price.
        
    *   Trading fees will be charged for the automatic settlement.
        
    *   All unrealized PnL will be settled and converted into realized PnL at that time.
        
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/delistings#after-delisting)

After delisting

*   The delisted contract will no longer be available for trading.
    
*   Historical data may remain available for reference.
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/delistings#recommendations)

Recommendations

To avoid automatic settlement and additional fees, traders are strongly advised to manually close all positions before the cessation of trading.

[PreviousAFEE & BonusUSD](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/afee-and-bonususd)
[Next1001x (Simple)](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple)

# Aster ALP | Aster

**The Au Points Program will officially sunset and a snapshot of Au Points balances will be taken at 00:00:00 UTC on Friday, June 13, 2025. No further Au Points will be granted after this point.** [**Read more**](https://x.com/Aster_DEX/status/1932367398872760416)
**.** _**Last updated: June 10, 2025**_

* * *

The ALP pool provides liquidity for all trading pairs on Aster Simple Mode (ALP mode) to maximize capital efficiency. Those who mint ALP participate in the market-making of on-chain perpetual contracts. ALP net asset value (NAV) is correlated with the profit and loss (PnL) of the ALP pool, which means that ALP price may rise or fall. Platform fees also contribute to boosting ALP NAV.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/aster-alp#alp-yields)

ALP Yields

ALP APY is generated from ALP’s market-making on Aster Simple Mode — that is, ALP’s profit and loss (PnL), income from trading fees, funding fees, and liquidations. Similar to asTokens, APY generated will reflect in the net asset value of ALP.

Minting ALP also earns you 5x Au points, which can be exchanged for the Aster token airdrop, thus presenting an additional layer of gains.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/aster-alp#supported-networks)

Supported networks

ALP can be minted on the BNB Chain or Arbitrum networks. Remember to switch networks as supported assets for minting differ.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F8fUtguA0iUqEppLeWDYZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dac65e61e-d7ad-48b0-ba16-5c82d6528d08&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fe275e0b&sv=2)

# Mint asBTC | Aster

**The Au Points Program will officially sunset and a snapshot of Au Points balances will be taken at 00:00:00 UTC on Friday, June 13, 2025. No further Au Points will be granted after this point.** [**Read more**](https://x.com/Aster_DEX/status/1932367398872760416)
**.** _**Last updated: June 10, 2025**_

* * *

**Page summary**

[How to mint & withdraw asBTC](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asbtc#how-to-mint-and-withdraw-asbtc)

[asBTC FAQs](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asbtc#asbtc-faqs)

asBTC is an innovative liquid staking token of BTC. Stake BTC to mint asBTC on Aster and earn:

*   1x Au Points Multiplier.
    
*   Up to 5% APY by employing stable trading strategies, distributed back to holders and reflected in the net asset value of asBTC.
    

Fund security is prioritized through Ceffu, a trusted third-party custodian, and stringent risk control measures ensure safety. Smart contracts are fully audited to guarantee their reliability.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asbtc#how-to-mint-and-withdraw-asbtc)

**How to mint & withdraw asBTC**

1\. Go to [AsterEarn](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn)
. Click \[Connect Wallet\] and sign the message.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FHVI9iZFM5ft0l7oBf9xy%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-04%252017.55.53.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd8f5ee82-8b2a-4e7b-937a-bd6def981bba&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d2eb7b07&sv=2)

2\. You can deposit BTC with your DeFi wallet. Currently, you can only deposit BTC using BSC chain.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FY117cEQ878oZoq2lMPCG%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-04%252018.04.46.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4668f6e7-1a59-4aec-bb0a-98a6c4187c6d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eeb3bacd&sv=2)

3\. Select BTC from the dropdown menu. Click \[Approve BTC\].

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FmIGZ8ewCo0x6v1aKXESc%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-04%252018.05.40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4e9b1ac7-3eb2-46f7-a9a0-7365cbad4f80&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=997d7ee0&sv=2)

4\. Enter your desired BTC value. Click \[Mint asBTC\]. Then click the confirm button to proceed.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FLMx7hXUrDVYuSlvVSARd%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-04%252018.06.47.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91d9c99c-39df-4cb5-a426-a5f942226bc7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b6b88a57&sv=2)

5\. Once confirmed, you have minted asBTC successfully. If you want to withdraw asBTC and get BTC tokens back, please enter the amount and click \[Request Withdraw\].

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FGSbGv5UnSoKid1PMyNi6%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-26%252009.44.16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6dd71904-88bc-45de-a3d4-0f29e4481496&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4d8ed5f5&sv=2)

6\. Once confirmed, the withdrawal will be processed within 14 days. You can check the status under \[Claim\].

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252Fv3ZL0gN6RJ0pumHU9qzA%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-26%252009.47.09.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D037675d5-017e-464b-8169-4dc141c0c012&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e880c931&sv=2)

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asbtc#asbtc-faqs)

**asBTC FAQs**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**What is asBTC?**

asBTC is an asToken minted by depositing BTC on AsterEarn. Holding asBTC earns you rewards. The token contract address is: 0x184b72289c0992BDf96751354680985a7C4825d6.

**Can I withdraw my asBTC at any time?**

Yes, withdrawals are subject to a 14 day waiting period.

**How is the APY generated?**

Your deposited BTC on AsterEarn will be used to employ stable trading strategies. The returns generated from the strategies are distributed back to you and reflected in the net asset value of asBTC. To see asBTC APY, visit: [https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn)
.

**How do I get the Au Multiplier?**

By minting asBTC, you earn Au points. Hold asBTC and let your Au points stack hourly. Au points give you an allocation of $AST airdrop.

**How is Au calculated?**

This depends on your BTC investment and the market price of BTC. For example, if you stake 0.001 BTC when BTC price is $95,667, and asBTC Au multiplier is 1x, your mint earns 0.001 x 95,667 x 1 = 95 Au.

If there is no change in BTC price, you will continue earning (0.001 x 95,667 x 1) Au per hour.

If BTC price later drops to $95,500 you will earn (0.001 x 95,500 x 1) Au per hour.

**What is Ceffu, and is it secure?**

Ceffu is an institutional digital asset platform that offers comprehensive custody and liquidity solutions. It is designed to securely manage and utilize your crypto assets efficiently. With advanced security protocols and risk management measures in place, Ceffu ensures that your Assets are stored and handled with the highest levels of safety and reliability.

**What are the risks involved?**

We have conducted thorough smart contract audits to ensure the security and reliability of the platform. In addition, we implement robust risk management protocols to protect your funds at all times.

**Are there any fees involved?**

There are no fees to mint or withdraw asBTC. You can manage your assets freely without incurring additional costs.

# Having trouble connecting your wallet? | Aster

If you’re running into issues while connecting your wallet through WalletConnect, try the steps below. Most problems can be resolved with reconnecting your wallet.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-app/having-trouble-connecting-your-wallet#i-receive-the-error-given-link-couldnt-be-opened-after-tapping-on-my-wallet)

I receive the error “Given link couldn’t be opened” after tapping on my wallet

Make sure you have the wallet app installed on your phone. WalletConnect uses app deep linking — if no compatible wallet app is installed, nothing will happen.

Fix:

*   Install a supported wallet and try again
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-app/having-trouble-connecting-your-wallet#wallet-opens-but-theres-no-connection-prompt)

Wallet opens, but there’s no connection prompt

Rarely the wallet opens but doesn’t ask you to approve the connection.

Fix:

*   Force-close both Aster Mobile and your wallet app
    
*   Reopen Aster Mobile and try connecting again
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-app/having-trouble-connecting-your-wallet#wallet-doesnt-open-or-switch-back-to-aster-mobile)

Wallet doesn’t open or switch back to Aster Mobile

Sometimes WalletConnect doesn’t automatically switch between your wallet and Aster Mobile during connection or signature steps.

Fix:

*   Manually return to Aster Mobile or your wallet to complete the step
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-app/having-trouble-connecting-your-wallet#wallet-accounts-arent-switching)

Wallet accounts aren’t switching

WalletConnect sessions are tied to the specific account and network you approved. Changing either inside your wallet doesn’t automatically update the session.

Fix:

*   Disconnect the wallet from Aster Mobile
    
*   Reconnect using the desired account and network
    

[PreviousAster app](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-app)
[NextDelete account](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-app/delete-account)

Last updated 4 months ago

# Fees & slippage | Aster

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FgBl72kb3DQq6Ssu96wFb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D99b7d129-30dc-4b32-943c-842697ed8689&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=916aa8b1&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple/fees-and-slippage#opening-position-fee)

**Opening position fee**

A Opening fee = Number of contracts × Entry price × Opening fee rate0.08% fee is charged when opening a position, calculated as:

> _Opening fee = Number of contracts × Entry price × Opening fee rate_

**Example**

If a trader on BNB Chain opens a 1 ETHUSD long position at $1,500:

> Opening fee = 1 × 1,500 × 0.08% = $1.20

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple/fees-and-slippage#closing-position-fee)

**Closing position fee**

A 0.08% fee is also charged when closing a position, calculated as:

> _Closing fee = Number of contracts × Close price × Closing fee rate_

**Example**

If the same trader closes the 1 ETHUSD position at $1,600:

> _Closing fee = 1 × 1,600 × 0.08% = $1.28_

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple/fees-and-slippage#dynamic-pnl-based-close-fee)

**Dynamic PnL-based close fee**

For positions using 500×, 750×, or 1001× leverage, no opening fee is charged. Instead, a dynamic closing fee is applied, calculated based on the realized PnL.

The minimum closing fee under this model is 0.03%.

![](https://apollox-finance.gitbook.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh5.googleusercontent.com%2Fx-j0hkF1yifTiEfpjNKi9QxklpcglxrspGw_zyq7T_x9jhm4amRlqWuVhID7Vc4g_ZRbTZSvgADb3SdkVDM7URENgpX-VTHzQO_ub3DjZkywItw1DA8WUk-x2_uxGOTrKLGdVRkbuN0Sp0Zwgygmi8c&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=afbf17f3&sv=2)

Where:

*   PnL = Profit or loss on the position
    
*   Share rate = Percentage of notional paid in fees (e.g. 15%)
    
*   Notional = Value used to open the position
    
*   Close min rate = Minimum fee rate applied (e.g. 0.03%)
    

Example

![](https://apollox-finance.gitbook.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh5.googleusercontent.com%2FJBltC7k0bpU6vJBnkwdmtndsWuXaY1ti1OMzqVeMkOmQMuaptZTTy7m2zve9BfsywU12w2Nylz4JVI033tzLicDAvbThaljCFFFxcj1apyL6vqmVBWTJroohNd8ShV6mB0LPrEeOO-sTIq4c6u_nq7Q&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3589ca81&sv=2)

If the position has a $100 profit, share rate is 15%, and notional is $600:

> _Closing fee rate = Max((100 × 15%) / 600, 0.03%) = 0.03%_

**Note**: In the event of liquidation, the 85% liquid loss rate includes this closing fee.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple/fees-and-slippage#execution-fee)

**Execution fee**

This fee covers network costs and ensures smooth order execution. It is charged only when a position is opened.

*   BNB Chain: $0.50
    
*   Arbitrum: $0.20
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple/fees-and-slippage#forex-perpetual-contracts-only-on-bnb-chain)

Forex perpetual contracts (only on BNB Chain)

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FtJfp5G5EQfT4yvPDZ9s1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24e24bbf-f185-44f5-89a0-115ad8a999cd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9a38a383&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple/fees-and-slippage#funding-rate)

Funding rate

The funding rate helps balance long and short positions on 1001x. It protects the ALP from excessive risk exposure and reduces the pool’s exposure to large open positions.

Funding is calculated **every block**. When market conditions change, the accumulated funding fee is automatically updated. This fee is reflected in a position’s **unrealized PnL** and directly affects the **liquidation price**.

*   If the user holds a **long** position, the fee uses the **long funding rate**
    
*   If the user holds a **short** position, the fee uses the **short funding rate**
    

**Funding fee formula**

> _Funding fee per block = (Number of contracts × Price) × Funding rate per block_

**Funding rate per block**

The funding rate per block is determined by the gap between long and short open interest and the platform’s current borrow rate.

**When long positions > short positions:**

*   Long basic funding rate = -abs(funding rate p)
    
*   Short basic funding rate = abs(funding rate p)
    

**When short positions > long positions:**

*   Short basic funding rate = abs(funding rate p)
    
*   Long basic funding rate = -abs(funding rate p)
    

**Final funding rate**

*   Long funding rate = Long basic funding rate − Borrow rate
    
*   Short funding rate = Short basic funding rate − Borrow rate
    

**Borrow rate**

The borrow rate is reviewed and adjusted regularly as part of platform risk management. It is influenced by:

*   The size of the position
    
*   The time the position is held
    

![](https://apollox-finance.gitbook.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F86643275-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FKgTrH6FlpxEZKMS3bN7R%252Fuploads%252FdDz79MnN66rRRSHClfEm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da5ab0f83-828c-477c-96e9-3fcb3f9b7875&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b6d1c5cd&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple/fees-and-slippage#base-interest-rate-per-block)

Base interest rate per block

The base interest rate per block is used to help calculate the borrow rate dynamically, based on recent market volatility.

> _Base interest rate per block = Base interest rate / (365 × 28,800)_

Where:

*   Base interest rate = k × HV
    
*   k = Adjustment factor (default: 1.25, platform adjustable)
    
*   HV = Historical volatility = 2-week average volatility × 365
    

This allows the platform to adjust borrow costs dynamically in response to volatility.

For more, see the historical volatility & base interest rate below:

![](https://apollox-finance.gitbook.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F86643275-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FKgTrH6FlpxEZKMS3bN7R%252Fuploads%252F8knme1A3VfJbsoVcN6d5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D42a46633-36ef-4662-81dd-ffc78d61c474&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cf88dfa1&sv=2)[119KBHV&BaseInterestRate.xlsx](https://86643275-files.gitbook.io/~/files/v0/b/gitbook-x-prod.appspot.com/o/spaces%2FKgTrH6FlpxEZKMS3bN7R%2Fuploads%2FVyhBYUAEUAV7xKbA4Lx6%2FHV%26BaseInterestRate.xlsx?alt=media&token=20619efe-eee9-4793-baf4-33ebdc431f23)

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple/fees-and-slippage#liquidation)

**Liquidation**

Liquidation occurs when a position’s mark price reaches its **liquidation price**. This price is determined by factors like leverage, margin, funding, and the platform’s liquidation loss rate.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple/fees-and-slippage#liquidation-price-distance)

Liquidation price distance

The liquidation price distance is calculated as:

> _Liquidation price distance = Entry price × (Initial margin × Liquidation loss rate + Cum funding fee) / Initial margin / Leverage_

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple/fees-and-slippage#liquidation-price-formulas)

Liquidation price formulas

For long positions:

> _Liquidation price = Entry price − Liquidation price distance_

For short positions:

> _Liquidation price = Entry price + Liquidation price distance_

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple/fees-and-slippage#parameter-definitions)

Parameter definitions

*   Entry price: The price at which the position is opened
    
*   Initial margin: The collateral the trader deposits to open the position
    
*   Liquidation loss rate: The default platform-defined loss factor during forced liquidation (default: 90%)
    
*   Cum funding fee: The total accumulated funding fees since the position was opened
    
*   Leverage: The leverage multiple selected by the user
    

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple/fees-and-slippage#example)

Example

If a trader opens a long ETH/USD position at 10× leverage with:

*   Entry price: $1,500
    
*   Initial margin: $100
    
*   Funding fee: $2
    
*   Liquidation loss rate: 85%
    

Then:

> Liquidation price distance = 1,500 × (100 × 85% + 2) / 100 / 10
> 
> \= 1,500 × (85 + 2) / 1,000
> 
> \= 1,500 × 87 / 1,000
> 
> \= 130.5
> 
> Liquidation price = 1,500 − 130.5 = 1,369.5

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple/fees-and-slippage#liquidation-1)

**Slippage**

Slippage on 1001x can be either **fixed** or **dynamic**, depending on the trading pair. The platform determines the slippage type based on the liquidity of the pair’s underlying assets, as observed from its oracle sources. This mechanism helps prevent price manipulation.

In general:

*   **Slippage increases** when open interest and new position size increase
    
*   **Slippage decreases** when oracle-source liquidity improves
    

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple/fees-and-slippage#fixed-slippage-btc-eth-and-forex-pairs)

Fixed slippage (BTC, ETH, and forex pairs)

Fixed slippage is used for high-liquidity pairs like BTC/USD, ETH/USD, and forex contracts.

**Example:**

If a trader opens a long ETH/USD position when the Pyth oracle price is $1,500 and the slippage is 0.01%:

> _Entry price = 1,500 + (1,500 × 0.01%) = 1,500.15_

Because liquidity differs across trading pairs and source markets, slippage levels also vary by asset. In general, pairs with lower liquidity will experience wider spreads.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple/fees-and-slippage#dynamic-slippage-all-other-trading-pairs)

Dynamic slippage (all other trading pairs)

Dynamic slippage is used for trading pairs that don’t qualify for fixed slippage. It is calculated based on **ALP exposure**, current **open interest**, and the **size of the user’s new position**.

**Formulas:**

> _Long dynamic slippage (%) = (New position + Symbol long open interest) / 1% depth above_

> _Short dynamic slippage (%) = (New position + Symbol short open interest) / 1% depth below_

Where:

*   New position: Size of the user’s order
    
*   Long/short open interest: Current open interest for the symbol in each direction
    
*   1% depth above / below: Aggregated spot market depth within ±1% of the index price, based on major source markets
    

This design ensures that slippage scales with market impact and liquidity — helping maintain fairness and pool stability.

[PreviousPrice oracles](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple/price-oracles)
[NextDegen mode](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/1001x-simple/degen-mode)

# Team boosts | Aster

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-4-harvest/team-boosts#team-boost-in-stage-4)

Team Boost in Stage 4

Everyone in a referral family is a team. Teams can enjoy team boosts. In Stage 4, the team boost mechanism continues to reward cumulative trading activity within your referral team but with important improvements to enhance collaboration and consistency.

A team is composed of the following members:

*   The person who invited you (A)
    
*   Other invitees of the person who invited you (B)
    
*   Yourself (C )
    
*   Your invitees (D)
    

For example: Yuki invited you and Wyn to Aster. You invited Zen, and Zen invited Ben.

*   Yuki = A
    
*   Wyn = B
    
*   You = C
    
*   Zen = D
    
*   Ben is not part of your team because he is a referral of your referral (second level).
    

**How team boosts work**

*   Team boosts are based on the team’s cumulative points earned from trading on Aster Perpetual and Spot.
    
*   Unlike Stage 2 where team boosts reset weekly at the start of each epoch, in Stage 4 the team boost accumulates continuously throughout the entire campaign without resetting.
    
*   This change means your team’s progress is preserved, encouraging long-term collaboration and steady growth.
    
*   When a new member joins a team, the team boost takes effect for them within a few hours, allowing immediate benefit without waiting for the next epoch.
    

Example

Wyn, Yuki, and Zen are a team. On the previous hour, they earned:

*   Wyn: 600,000
    
*   Yuki: 300,000
    
*   Zen: 100,000
    

Team points = 600,000 + 300,000 + 100,000 = 1,000,000

According to the boost table, the team qualifies for a 1.05x boost, applied equally to each member’s:

*   Wyn: 600,000 × 1.05 = 630,000
    
*   Yuki: 300,000 × 1.05 = 315,000
    
*   Zen: 100,000 × 1.05 = 105,000
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-4-harvest/team-boosts#rh-team-boost)

Rh team boost

Team Rh (at hourly snapshot)

Team boost

3,000,000

1.05x

15,000,000

1.1x

45,000,000

1.15x

90,000,000

1.2x

# Referral bonus | Aster

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-4-harvest/referral-bonus#id-1.-how-to-generate-invite-code)

Go to the Aster Harvest: Stage 4 landing page. Connect your wallet. Your invite code will be automatically displayed. Share the code with your invitees. You can also change your name by clicking on the edit button.

2\. How to bind invite code

Go to the Aster Harvest: Stage 4 landing page. A screen will pop up to prompt you to enter your invite code. Click \[Redeem invite code\]. Click \[Skip\] if you don’t have one.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FtwBp4wUWINDeGcIAfjj7%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-11-07%252018.20.40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D61485f36-40b1-4dbd-8a19-634dbcda10a1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d83dee26&sv=2)

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FjOcWa8lqW1PgQWCjtBjR%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-11-10%252016.45.03.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba904f4d-9223-4fb8-bb01-a3d62c7ecd7b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8249850d&sv=2)
