# AT/USDT campaign | Aster

**APRO ($AT): A Trusted Oracle for the Multi-Chain Era**

**What is APRO?**

APRO is a professional oracle delivering verifiable data across cutting-edge ecosystems (RWA, AI & DeFi), purpose-built to be 100% startup-friendly, and validated by proven PMF, a strong team, and sustainable profitability.

*   Campaign symbol: AT/USDT
    
*   Campaign Period: 12:00 UTC 24 Oct – 23:59 UTC 6 Nov 2025
    
*   Total rewards: $200,000 in ASTER + additional prize pool in AT
    

Users who meet the following criteria during the campaign period will be eligible to share a extra $AT prize pool:

*   Achieve 1,000 USD trading volume in $AT/USDT spot trading pair during the campaign period.
    
*   Hold a minimum combined amount of 100 $ASTER (across Spot and Perpetual wallets) throughout the entire event
    

In the Rocket Launch program, users will get eligible trading volume when trading on the AT/USDT spot pair. Eligible trading volume will be updated daily around T+1, 06:00 UTC. Your eligible trading volume determines the final reward allocation for each user.

**FAQs**

**What is Rocket Launch?**

Rocket Launch aims to establish a liquidity-driven platform that supports project growth, while providing users with early access to emerging on-chain opportunities.

Each Rocket Launch campaign features a reward pool jointly funded by $ASTER and the participating project’s native tokens. As part of the initiative, the project team will buy back $ASTER and contribute the repurchased tokens to the reward pool.

**How to qualify for the campaign?**

Each campaign requires a minimum $ASTER holding and a minimum trading volume.

Only wallet login can be eligible for the Rocket launch campaign, **email login users are unable to join the Rocket launch campaign.**

**When can I receive my Rocket Launch program rewards?**

Rewards will be distributed to users’ Aster spot accounts within 14 days after the campaign ends.

**Notes:**

1.  Participants must trade at least $1,000 in total AT Spot trading volume during the campaign period and hold a minimum combined amount of 100 $ASTER (across Spot and Perpetual wallets) throughout the entire event to be eligible for rewards.
    
2.  Rewards will be distributed based on each participant’s AT Spot trading volume relative to the total AT trading volume during the campaign.
    
3.  Each eligible participant can receive a maximum of 3% of the total reward pool.
    
4.  All new and existing Aster users are eligible, excluding market makers.
    

**How to Access Rocket Launch?**

1.  Connect your wallet on Aster and find 「[Rocket Launch](https://www.asterdex.com/en/rocket-launch)
    」 under the 「Rewards」 menu.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F2HWBEZF04tcOuSQWyq0d%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-10-23%252018.02.28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D89ff7ddd-d4ad-40e0-a0d0-1b8496e04bf9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3b1b56e8&sv=2)

2\. Find the Ongoing campaigns, click the 「Trade to Earn」 and find the Specified spot trading pairs.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FFnGmaluSrpq9OAVS2AKn%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-10-23%252018.03.40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D713aa724-11f8-4c16-912d-31ffbe96df51&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9398be78&sv=2)

# How to mint ALP? | Aster

1.  Go to [https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn/alp](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn/alp)
    . Check that you are on the correct network (you can mint ALP on BNB Chain and Arbitrum networks).
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FAouy5Iuzembuh1sgrI99%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-31%252012.39.50.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D342ae6b1-4d55-4e9f-96fa-2ab1bcc21b39&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b0d24a5f&sv=2)

1.  After connecting your wallet, click **\[Mint ALP\]**. Use any of the supported ALP pool assets to mint ALP. After confirming the transaction, you will receive the ALP tokens in your wallet successfully.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FtdNqNoLyOEzphTQh0Wnw%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-31%252012.45.40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De7b552e7-16aa-44b4-8b9b-5ffa5eabd674&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=15cf4ba4&sv=2)

1.  Add ALP token to your wallet to check its balance.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FpQJYDJY9bessk6wbhW7b%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-31%252012.48.07.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D65ccfdcc-8320-4f59-abce-83639281cf4d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1dd5b53b&sv=2)

**Please note:**

*   ALP cannot be burned in the first 48 hours after minting.

# Trade & Earn | Aster

**Important Notice:**

*   _**New adjustment for the Trading rewards:**_
    

1) _Starting from_ _**20th Nov**__, weekly trading volume requirement has been adjusted to_ _**50,000 USD**__._

_2) When calculating trade rewards, we will determine the reward amount based on the USDF holdings snapshot for each account. Starting from_ _**September 4th**__, the_ _**maximum USDF holdings**_ _per account that can be considered for trade rewards will be adjusted to_ _**100,000 USDF.**_

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/trade-and-earn#what-is-trade-and-earn)

What Is Trade & Earn?

Trade & Earn is a feature on Aster Pro that rewards you for using Aster’s yield-bearing assets as margin in your perpetual trading.

Instead of just holding your tokens in a wallet or staking vault, you can now deploy them as collateral while continuing to earn passive rewards - turning every trade into a smarter, yield-generating move.

**Supported Assets: asBNB & USDF**

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/trade-and-earn#asbnb)

[asBNB](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asbnb)

asBNB is Aster’s liquid staking token. Mint asBNB by staking BNB or slisBNB, and enjoy both flexible asset utility and strong yield potential. Use asBNB as collateral to trade more efficiently or to earn passive income through staking rewards.

**Sources of asBNB Income** asBNB generates rewards through BNB Launchpools, HODLer airdrops, and Megadrops, making it a versatile asset for both trading and earning.

**Receiving asBNB Rewards**

*   Launchpool rewards are reflected in the asBNB exchange rate directly.
    
*   HODLer airdrops and Megadrops require manual claiming within the platform.
    

**How to Trade with asBNB** Deposit asBNB into your trading account to use it as margin for contracts. Continue earning rewards from asBNB while executing profitable trades.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/trade-and-earn#usdf)

[USDF](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin)

USDF is Aster’s yield-bearing stablecoin, fully backed and redeemable 1:1 with USDT. Designed for passive income generation, USDF lets you earn while holding.

**Sources of USDF income**  USDF earns two types of income: deposit rewards and trading rewards, both funded by platform fees.

**How Can I Receive USDF Rewards?**

*   Deposit Rewards: Earned by depositing and holding over 1 USDF in your trading account. Deposit rewards are calculated based on each account's hourly USDF holdings snapshot and distributed proportionally according to the total holdings performance.
    
*   Trading Rewards: Earned by being active at least 2 days a week with a weekly trading volume of over _**50,000**_ **USDT**.（Active user: At least has one trading transaction like opening position, closing position or liquidation transaction per day)
    
*   _**New adjustment for the Trading rewards:**_ _When calculating trade rewards, we will determine the reward amount based on the USDF holdings snapshot for each account. Starting from_ _**September 4th**__, the_ _**maximum USDF holdings**_ _per account that can be considered for trade rewards will be adjusted to_ _**100,000 USDF.**_
    

**Rewards Distribution** Rewards from the previous week are automatically distributed and transferred in USDF to your trading account every week, enabling continuous earning.

**How to Trade with USDF** Deposit USDF into your trading account to use it as collateral for contracts. Benefit from USDF income streams while actively trading.

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/trade-and-earn#how-to-usdf-or-asbnb-as-collateral-for-aster-pro-trading)

How to USDF or asBNB as collateral for Aster Pro trading?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  You may [deposit](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-perpetual-pro/deposit-and-withdraw-guide)
     USDF or asBNB to your Aster Pro account on our [website](https://www.asterdex.com/en)
    .

# Maintaining the peg | Aster

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/maintaining-the-peg#id-1.-rigid-redemption-and-arbitrage-opportunities)

1\. Rigid redemption & arbitrage opportunities


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

USDF and USDT offer a 1:1 redemption mechanism, ensuring that the stablecoin is always pegged to the value of the US Dollar. This rigid redemption model is crucial to maintaining the stability of the stablecoin.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/maintaining-the-peg#how-does-redemption-work)

**How does redemption work?**

When you hold USDF, you can redeem it at any time for the equivalent value in USDT (or another equivalent value, depending on the platform). The redemption process ensures that there’s always a direct 1:1 correlation between USDF and USDT, which plays an important role in maintaining the price peg.

For example:

*   If you hold 100 USDF, you can redeem it for 100 USDT.
    
*   The value of the USDF token remains stable because the system ensures there is always an equal amount of underlying assets (such as USDT) available for redemption.
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/maintaining-the-peg#arbitrage-opportunities)

**Arbitrage opportunities**

One of the key mechanisms through which holders can profit from market inefficiencies is arbitrage. If the price of USDF deviates from its 1:1 peg (either above or below), users can take advantage of the discrepancy by engaging in arbitrage trading.

Consider the scenario where the USDF-USDT pair in a liquidity pool (e.g., PancakeSwap) becomes imbalanced, and the price of USDF is slightly higher than 1 USDT. Here’s an example of how arbitrage works:

**Example of arbitrage:**

1.  **Arbitrage opportunity:**
    

*   Suppose the USDF token is trading at 1.02 USDT in the PancakeSwap pool (where USDF is temporarily overvalued).
    
*   A holder could then redeem USDF at the fixed 1:1 rate (e.g., 100 USDF = 100 USDT) and then swap the 100 USDT for 102 USDT worth of USDF on PancakeSwap.
    
*   The holder profits from the price difference (2% arbitrage profit in this example).
    

1.  **Actionable arbitrage:**
    

*   If the price of USDF is temporarily undervalued (e.g., 0.98 USDT), a holder can purchase USDF at the discounted rate and redeem it 1:1 for USDT, capturing the arbitrage profit when the price reverts to its proper peg.
    

Aside from helping holders profit from market inefficiencies, arbitrage also helps to stabilize price and minimize further risk of deviation from the peg.

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/maintaining-the-peg#id-2.-delta-neutral-positions)

2\. Delta-neutral positions


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

While rigid redemption plays a significant role in ensuring that USDF and USDT maintain their 1:1 peg, delta-neutral strategies also help further stabilize the price and minimize the risk of deviation.

In the context of USDF, the delta-neutral strategy helps maintain a stable 1:1 peg by balancing long and short positions in the underlying assets that back the stablecoin. This helps to:

1.  **Stabilize the price**: By managing the volatility of the underlying assets (such as USDT), USDF ensures that its value remains close to 1:1 with the US Dollar, even when the price of other assets in the market fluctuates.
    
2.  **Generate consistent yield**: The delta-neutral strategy allows for fee generation through liquidity pools or other decentralized finance mechanisms, while minimizing risk exposure to volatile assets.
    

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/maintaining-the-peg#id-3.-key-takeaways-of-the-usdf-pegging-mechanism)

3\. Key takeaways of the USDF pegging mechanism


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **1:1 redemption**: USDF can always be redeemed at a 1:1 rate for USDT, ensuring price stability and providing holders with a mechanism to maintain their capital in a stable value.
    
*   **Arbitrage opportunities**: Market inefficiencies in liquidity pools or exchanges create arbitrage opportunities where holders can capitalize on price discrepancies between USDF and USDT, further stabilizing the peg.
    
*   **Delta-neutral strategy**: The delta-neutral approach helps hedge against volatility and maintains the 1:1 peg by balancing long and short positions, ensuring that USDF remains stable even in fluctuating markets.
    

[PreviousHow USDF works](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/how-usdf-works)
[NextFund custody & risk management](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/fund-custody-and-risk-management)

# Team boosts | Aster

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-3-dawn/team-boosts#rh-team-boost-in-stage-3)

Rh Team Boost in Stage 3

Everyone in a referral family is a team. Teams can enjoy team boosts. In Stage 3, the team boost mechanism continues to reward cumulative trading activity within your referral team but with important improvements to enhance collaboration and consistency.

A team is composed of the following members:

*   The person who invited you (A)
    
*   Other invitees of the person who invited you (B)
    
*   Yourself (C )
    
*   Your invitees (D)
    

For example: Yuki invited you and Wyn to Aster. You invited Zen, and Zen invited Ben.

*   Yuki = A
    
*   Wyn = B
    
*   You = C
    
*   Zen = D
    
*   Ben is not part of your team because he is a referral of your referral (second level).
    

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-3-dawn/team-boosts#how-team-boosts-work)

How team boosts work

*   Team boosts are based on the team’s cumulative Rh points earned from trading on Aster Perpetual and Spot.
    
*   Unlike Stage 2 where team boosts reset weekly at the start of each epoch, in Stage 3 the team boost accumulates continuously throughout the entire campaign without resetting.
    
*   This change means your team’s progress is preserved, encouraging long-term collaboration and steady growth.
    
*   When a new member joins a team, the team boost takes effect for them within a few hours, allowing immediate benefit without waiting for the next epoch.
    

**Example**

Wyn, Yuki, and Zen are a team. On the previous hour, they earned:

*   Wyn: 600,000 Rh
    
*   Yuki: 300,000 Rh
    
*   Zen: 100,000 Rh
    

Team Rh = 600,000 + 300,000 + 100,000 = 1,000,000 Rh

According to the boost table, the team qualifies for a 1.05x boost, applied equally to each member’s Rh:

*   Wyn: 600,000 × 1.05 = 630,000 Rh
    
*   Yuki: 300,000 × 1.05 = 315,000 Rh
    
*   Zen: 100,000 × 1.05 = 105,000 Rh
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-3-dawn/team-boosts#rh-team-boost)

Rh team boost

# How to burn ALP? | Aster

1.  Go to [https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn/alp](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn/alp)
    . Check that you are on the correct network (you can mint ALP on BNB Chain and Arbitrum networks).
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FBtnudeJCWbOJK2yjf9Gz%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-31%252012.39.50.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De390c3ea-f38f-47ac-807a-758d0279a9cb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=69d9e001&sv=2)

1.  After connecting your wallet, click **\[Burn ALP\]**.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FKZdVt1fUBUrOgXWNPFf5%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-31%252012.52.40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1aab4229-1079-4746-b3e1-85a42b486ef2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2c5a8a4e&sv=2)

**Please note:**

*   ALP cannot be burned in the first 48 hours after minting.
    
*   Amount of ALP tokens that can be burned: min\[(Value of the liquidity pool - Value of user’s positions)\*50%\]/ALP Market Price. For instance, if the value of the liquidity pool is 10,000,000 USDT, the value of user A's position is 5,000,000 USDT and ALP market price is 2 USDT, the maximum amount user A can burn is 1,250,000.
    
*   The amount of assets that holders receive after burning their ALP tokens will not exceed the amount in the ALP liquidity pool. For instance, if the liquidity pool only has 1000 USDT, the maximum amount of USDT that holders can receive will be 1000 USDT. The remaining ALP tokens can be burned for other ALP pool asssets.

[NextALP fees](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/aster-alp/alp-fees)

# ALP fees | Aster

To encourage the use of different assets for minting ALP, fees are adjusted according to the target weights and current weights of assets in the ALP liquidity pool. We aim to encourage asset composition of the pool to reflect the target weights.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/aster-alp/alp-fees#buying-fee)

Mint fee:

*   Basic Rate Parameter 1: FeeBasisPoints, USDT is currently set at 0.25%
    
*   Basic Rate Parameter 2: TaxBasisPoints, USDT is currently set at 0.05%
    
*   The current asset value: InitialValue=AssetValueInPool+AssetUnrealizedpnl\_usd
    
*   The current asset value after minting: AfterMinValue=InitialValue+MinValue
    
*   Calculating the asset value according to the target weight: TargetValue=(Total Value\_usd+totalUnrealizedpnl\_Usd)\*Target weight，Total Value=sum(InitialValue)
    
*   The current asset value and the target value (absolute value): InitialDiff=InitialValue-TargetValue
    
*   After Minting, the asset value and target mechanism (absolute value): AfterDiff=AfterMintValue-TargetValue
    
    *   if AfterDiff<InitialDiffValue
        
    
*   MintFee=Max(FeeBasisPoints-TaxBasisPoints\*InitialDiff/TargetValue，0)
    
    *   if AfterDiff>=InitialDiff
        
    
*   MintFee=FeeBasisPoints+TaxBasisPoints\*Min((InitialDiff+AfterDiff)/2,TargetValue)/TargetValue
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/aster-alp/alp-fees#selling-fee)

Burn fee:

*   Basic Rate Parameter 1: FeeBasisPoints，USDT is currently set at 0.25%
    
*   Max Base Rate Parameter 2: TaxBasisPoints，USDT is currently set at 0.05%
    
*   The current asset value: InitialValue=AssetValueInPool+AssetUnreliazedpnl\_usd
    
*   The current asset value after Burn: AfterMaxValue=InitialValue-MinValue
    
*   Calculating the Asset value according to the target weight: TargetValue=Total Value\*Target weight
    
*   The current asset value and target value (absolute value): InitialDiff=InitialValue-TargetValue
    
*   After Burn, the asset value and target mechanism (absolute value): AfterMaxDiff=AfterBurnValue-TargetValue
    
    *   if AfterDiff<InitialDiffValue
        
    
*   BurnFee=Max(FeeBasisPoints-MTaxBasisPoints\*InitialDiff/TargetValue，0)
    
    *   if AfterDiff>=InitialDiff
        
    
*   BurnFee=FeeBasisPoints+TaxBasisPoints\*Min((InitialDiff+AfterDiff)/2,TargetValue)/TargetValue
    

For example:

If the value of the ALP pool is $10,000,000, the unrealized PnL is $+10,000, the value of BTC in the liquidity pool is $1,000;

The BTC target weight is 2%, and the current weight is 0.01%. The base rate parameter 1 of BTC is 0.25%, and the base rate parameter 2 is 0.45%.

According to the calculation, the rate of minting ALP with 1 BTC at this time is 0% = 0 BTC. The transaction fee for burning ALP to get 1 BTC is 0.7% = 0.007 BTC.

Click [here](https://astherus.com/en/earn/alp)
 to view the composition of the ALP liquidity pool, the tokens’ quantities and values, target weights and current weights, and other information.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FVVnuNsPUi14hf3Yk4hsx%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-31%252013.56.17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df45faaaf-582f-4430-9991-387a6313d16e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2bcb68f0&sv=2)

After selecting the asset, quantity and clicking \[Mint ALP\] or \[Burn ALP\], the webpage will display the transaction fees. Example:

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FgVGmUaLo0IrwHy2lNtAu%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-31%252013.57.17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8fa5a4f8-9666-4184-9ba6-48c617607358&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a677f000&sv=2)

[PreviousHow to burn ALP?](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/aster-alp/how-to-burn-alp)
[NextEcosystem](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem)

# USDF Stablecoin | Aster

**The Au Points Program will officially sunset and a snapshot of Au Points balances will be taken at 00:00:00 UTC on Friday, June 13, 2025. No further Au Points will be granted after this point.** [**Read more**](https://x.com/Aster_DEX/status/1932367398872760416)
**.** _**Last updated: June 10, 2025**_

* * *

USDF is a fully collateralized, yield-bearing stablecoin issued by Aster. It is convertible 1:1 with USDT and designed to generate passive returns.

The underlying USDT is used to create delta-neutral strategies — approaches that aim to earn yield while minimizing exposure to price swings. These strategies help support staked USDF (asUSDF) rewards.

Users who mint and hold USDF are eligible for a **20× Au Points multiplier**, which contributes to $AST airdrop rewards.

👉 [**Mint USDF here**](https://www.asterdex.com/en/usdf)

# How Points Work in Aster Harvest: Stage 4 | Aster

Just like in previous stages, Aster continues to use points as the core rewards mechanism for Stage 4. Points are calculated on a weekly basis, with each “epoch” running from Monday 00:00 UTC to Sunday 23:59 UTC, unless otherwise specified.

**What are points?**

Points are Aster Stage 4 Airdrop points for trading on Aster Perpetual and Spot (Note: 1001x trades are excluded and do not earn points).

**Scoring Formula:**

Final Points = (Trading points + Position Points + Aster Asset points +Liquidation points+ Profit and Loss Points) x Team boost + Referral points

**Note:**

*   Each category carries its own weighting to ensure balanced and fair rewards.
    
*   Adjustments may be applied to farmed points to maintain integrity.
    
*   Specific weightings and formulas remain undisclosed.
    

**Scoring Model Overview**

Points are calculated using a multi-dimensional scoring model, which considers multiple factors :

**Trading Points Score**

*   Trade Points are now calculated based on your trading fee contribution, liquidity (maker order) contribution and symbol boost factor.
    
*   Selected Spot and Perps symbols may boost your trading points.
    
*   Update hourly.
    

**Position Points Score - Only for Perpetual**

*   The larger size and longer time you hold a position, the more points you earn.
    
*   Points caps are not applied anymore on your trading volume.
    
*   Updated on a T+1 basis.
    

**Aster Assets Points Score - Only for Perpetual**

*   Earn points by using Aster assets such as $ASTER/asBNB/USDF as margin.
    
*   Points caps are not applied anymore on your used margin value to hold the positions.
    
*   Updated on a T+1 basis.
    

**Liquidation points - Only for Perpetual**

*   Liquidation points are generated when a position is liquidated.
    
*   The more liquidation fees a user generates, the more Liquidation Points they receive.
    
*   Update hourly.
    

**Profit and Loss Points Points Score - Only for Perpetual**

*   Hourly net profit and loss (excluding fees such as funding fees) contributes to points.
    
*   Updated hourly
    

**Team Boost & Referral Points Score**

*   Team boosts will accumulate throughout Stage 4 and won’t reset during this period.
    
*   Team boosts for new members will take effect in a few hours after joining the team
    
*   Earn a share of your invitees’ based on the total points of your invitees and their invitees.
    
*   Points earned from first-level invitees are higher than those from second-level invitees. Updated daily.
    
*   Referral score example
    
*   A invites B, C, and D:
    
*   A earns from B/C/D’s base points (excluding team boosts).
    
*   If B invites C and C invites D (maximum two levels):
    
*   A also earns from C’s base points.
    

Base points include trading points score, positions points score, Aster asset holding score, and net PnL score.

**Note**

While the exact formulas and weightings remain undisclosed, all factors above are calculated weekly to determine your total points. These points accumulate toward your $ASTER airdrop share at the conclusion of Stage 4.

_**Terms & Conditions**_

*   Market Makers who are participating in the dedicated MM Program cannot earn points.
    
*   For each epoch, Aster may adjust the rules according to user feedback and market conditions.
    
*   Only participants who meet all the requirements will be considered as a qualified user.
    
*   The points are limited to only one entry per user; bulk registered accounts will not be eligible for rewards
    
*   Aster reserves the right to disqualify trades that are deemed to be wash trades, displaying attributes of market manipulation, bulk-account registrations to farm additional bonuses, or any other attempts at fraud.
    
*   Aster reserves the right to cancel or amend any Activity or Activity Rules at our sole discretion.
    
*   Aster reserves the right of final interpretation of this activity.
    

Risk warning: Crypto futures trading carries a substantial risk. All trading activities are done at your discretion and at your own risk. The information here should not be regarded as financial or investment advice from Aster. Aster will not be liable for any loss that might arise from your use of Aster.

# Fund custody & risk management | Aster

Aster works with [Ceffu](https://www.ceffu.com/)
 for the custody of USDF and underlying funds USDT, and to prepare funds for the execution of asUSDF yield strategies.

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/fund-custody-and-risk-management#how-ceffu-ensures-safe-custody-of-funds)

How Ceffu ensures safe custody of funds


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Ceffu provides institutional-grade crypto asset management solutions, focusing on security and efficient technology. They offer a variety of services such as cold storage, off-exchange settlement, and multi-party computation to secure digital assets. Ceffu is designed to meet the needs of institutions by providing custody, liquidity solutions, and compliance with rigorous security standards.

Advanced technologies like multi-party computation (MPC) and multi-signature wallets are utilized. They manage crypto assets using private key encryption, which is stored securely in hardware devices or cryptographic vaults. Ceffu’s custody solutions are compliant with institutional standards, offering features like custom governance controls and robust security measures for managing and protecting digital assets.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/fund-custody-and-risk-management#mirrorx)

MirrorX

Ceffu's MirrorX function plays a crucial role in generating staked USDF (asUSDF) yields. MirrorX is a solution by Ceffu that allows projects to deploy their capital on Binance instantaneously while keeping their assets in Ceffu’s independent custody. This service enables a 1:1 balance delegation from a Ceffu account to a designated Binance sub-account, with assets always remaining in Ceffu’s custody. Trades are settled off-exchange, minimizing counterparty risk. Withdrawals can be made directly from the Binance account, triggering a T+1 settlement. This setup combines deep liquidity with heightened security. [Read more](https://www.ceffu.com/blog/maximize-capital-efficiency-with-mirrorx-for-binance-institutional-users)
.

Through MirrorX, the Aster account on Ceffu supports the execution of a delta-neutral strategy by providing a seamless off-exchange settlement mechanism, optimizing returns while upholding institutional-grade security measures. The account buys spot assets on Binance, then shorts the corresponding perpetual contracts to maintain delta-neutral positions.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/fund-custody-and-risk-management#audit)

Audit

Before deploying any asset, Aster conducts a rigorous evaluation to assess market fit and potential risks.

USDF Audit report

[Audit reports](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/audit-reports)

9MB

[Astherus \_ SSC.pdf](https://4068247257-files.gitbook.io/~/files/v0/b/gitbook-x-prod.appspot.com/o/spaces%2FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%2Fuploads%2FkYEapH4f4Nk3GFHM75ia%2FAstherus%20_%20SSC.pdf?alt=media&token=0e52c180-6a14-4bb3-b213-910b1aa8a10f)

Download[Open](https://4068247257-files.gitbook.io/~/files/v0/b/gitbook-x-prod.appspot.com/o/spaces%2FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%2Fuploads%2FkYEapH4f4Nk3GFHM75ia%2FAstherus%20_%20SSC.pdf?alt=media&token=0e52c180-6a14-4bb3-b213-910b1aa8a10f)

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/fund-custody-and-risk-management#risks)

Risks


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

As with any asset, it is important to consider potential risks and understand what actions can be taken to mitigate risk. There are general risk factors and risks associated with a yield-bearing stablecoin like USDF.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/fund-custody-and-risk-management#smart-contract-risk)

Smart contract risk

Smart contract risk refers to the chance for malicious actors to exploit loopholes in the protocol’s smart contracts. Aster engages reputable security firms to conduct audits on all smart contracts and maintains a robust risk monitoring system. However, as exploiters become more sophisticated, there remains a minimal risk of unexpected exploits. To mitigate this, Aster works with security and blockchain partners to stay abreast of the newest developments in crypto and DeFi security. We also regularly liaise with these partners’ in-house risk monitoring teams.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/fund-custody-and-risk-management#underlying-asset-risk)

Underlying asset risk

When a user stakes USDT, they mint USDF at a 1:1 ratio. USDT is also used as trading collateral to maintain delta-neutral positions. Thus, underlying asset risk refers to the potential risks associated with USDT — the most salient involving the risk of price depegging and ensuring a robust reserve backing for USDT. These risks are disclosed by Tether (the issuer of USDT) in their [Legal Terms](https://tether.to/en/legal/?tab=risk-disclosure-statement)
. To see current USDT balances, reports and reserves, please visit [https://tether.to/en/transparency/?tab=usdt](https://tether.to/en/transparency/?tab=usdt)
.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/fund-custody-and-risk-management#custodial-partner-risk)

Custodial partner risk

Aster relies on Ceffu for the custody of USDF underlying funds. There may be custodial partner risk if operations on Ceffu fail — such as lack of accessibility, availability of asset transactions and the failure of operational duties like frequent PnL settlements for open positions. There is also risk if Ceffu falls short of compliance, security or data privacy standards, leading to a temporary or permanent shutdown. Due to the above, Ceffu solutions are [ISO 27001 and 27701 certified](https://www.ceffu.com/blog/ceffus-solution-receives-iso-27001-and-iso-27701-certification)
 and [SOC 2 Type 1 & 2 compliant](https://www.ceffu.com/blog/upholding-trust-and-safety-ceffu-renews-soc-2-attestation)
. These qualifications mean auditors have analyzed Ceffu’s cybersecurity and privacy controls. [Ceffu is also part of the Global Travel Rule (GTR) Alliance](https://www.ceffu.com/blog/ceffu_joins_global-travel_rule_alliance_digital_asset_compliance)
 to comply with the Travel Rule (officially known as the Financial Action Task Force’s (FATF) Recommendation 16), which is set to become the universal standard in compliance reporting. Aside from these, Aster takes a proactive stance to react quickly in the event of custodial partner risk.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/fund-custody-and-risk-management#exchange-partner-risk)

Exchange partner risk

The Aster-Ceffu account maintains delta-neutral positions to generate asUSDF yields. USDT assets continue to be kept in Ceffu’s independent custody and trades are settled off-exchange. There is exchange partner risk if the Binance exchange becomes insolvent, which will render the delta-neutral positions ineffective. Aster takes a proactive stance in monitoring to react quickly in the event of exchange partner risk.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/fund-custody-and-risk-management#funding-risk)

Funding risk

Perpetual shorts are used in the delta-neutral strategy for hedging. In the process, the Aster-Ceffu account may earn funding fees which reflects in asUSDF’s net asset value. If there are consistently negative funding rates, the Aster account on Ceffu may be required to pay more funding fees, thus affecting asUSDF APY. That said, it is normal for funding rates to fluctuate especially in periods of volatility. Even though negative funding rates directly affect APY, perp markets are usually designed to balance long and short open interest. This means that negative funding rates usually return back to a positive mean.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/fund-custody-and-risk-management#liquidation-risk)

Liquidation risk

When there are perpetual positions involved, there is a risk of liquidation. This risk may arise when the underlying spot asset price changes significantly in a short period of time, causing positions to be automatically liquidated if collateral falls short of margin requirements. This risk is minimal as the Aster account on Ceffu regularly monitors existing positions and frequently settles PnL.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/fund-custody-and-risk-management#prospects)

Prospects

During periods of market downturns, USDF presents a reliable option for those seeking steady returns. A yield-bearing stablecoin, minting and holding USDF earns holders 20x Au points for the Aster token airdrop. Holding USDF also opens additional channels for earning when users stake USDF to get asUSDF, its yield-bearing token. asUSDF currently generates yield through two primary channels: APY from delta-neutral strategies and Au points.

There is huge market potential for USDF and asUSDF. Consider the integration of real-world assets (RWAs) like US Treasury Bonds, thus allowing Aster to develop new avenues for yield. The protocol also continually explores new arbitrage strategies, RWA and onchain strategies to boost capital efficiency and yield generation. Thus, Aster’s aim is always access to safe and productive investment options even in less favorable economic conditions.

# FAQs | Aster

**The Au Points Program will officially sunset and a snapshot of Au Points balances will be taken at 00:00:00 UTC on Friday, June 13, 2025. No further Au Points will be granted after this point.** [**Read more**](https://x.com/Aster_DEX/status/1932367398872760416)
**.** _**Last updated: June 10, 2025**_

* * *

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/faqs#usdf-faq)

USDF FAQ


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**What is USDF?**

USDF is a yield-bearing stablecoin minted with USDT. USDT and USDF are fully convertible at a 1:1 ratio on Aster. The contract address is 0x5A110fC00474038f6c02E89C707D638602EA44B5.

**What yield sources does USDF have?**

Minting USDF earns you Au points. Au points grant an allocation of the $AST airdrop.

**What happens to my USDT?**

USDT funds are sent to Aster’s Ceffu account. Ceffu is Aster’s custodial partner. The funds are then used to create delta-neutral positions which back USDF and which generates asUSDF yields.

**How is Au calculated?**

This depends on your USDT investment. For example, if you stake 100 USDT, USDT price is $1 and USDF Au multiplier is 20x, your mint earns 100 x 20 = 2,000 Au.

Since USDT is a stablecoin, you will continue earning (100 x 20) Au per hour.

**What is Smart Mint USDF?**

Smart Mint USDF is a mechanism to optimize USDT to USDF rates so that you get the best conversion rate. Your mint will be executed via the Aster USDF mint contract, or via PancakeSwap.

Minting USDF with USDT on Aster adheres to a 1:1 ratio. However, USDF/USDT liquidity pools on PancakeSwap may see some price deviation—for example, minting on Aster could potentially result in a lower amount of USDF than if you had bought USDF on PancakeSwap. Smart Mint accounts for this.

**What is the minting fee?**

There is no minting fee if your mint is executed on Aster. For example, if Alice uses 1,000 USDT to mint USDF, she will receive 1,000 USDF.

There is a small fee if your mint is executed via PancakeSwap. Before swapping, you will be able to see the estimated fee.

**How to redeem USDF (USDF to USDT)?**

There are two ways to redeem USDF.

*   [Request to redeem USDF on Aster](https://www.asterdex.com/en/usdf)
    

Go to the _Redeem_ tab, enter the amount, and click \[Redeem\]. Most redemptions are processed within 1–2 days, but larger amounts may take up to 7 days. During this time, you will not earn airdrop points. Once the waiting period ends, go to the Claim tab and click \[Claim\] to receive your USDT.

*   Swap USDF via PancakeSwap
    

Input a USDF amount. You will see a note: "Via Pancake Swap, you will receive \_\_\_\_ USDT instantly." Click \[Swap\]. You will be redirected to the PancakeSwap page with the quoted USDT amount.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FetwNFmUk9MdOxqrnng9W%252FUSDF%2520pcs%2520swap.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b888c86-4636-4827-8a2f-2ff5af957d39&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eedac52c&sv=2)

**What is the redemption fee?**

The redemption fee is 0.1% if your redemption is executed on Aster. For example, if Alice redeems 1,000 USDF, she will receive 999 USDT in return.

There is a swap fee if you swap USDF for USDT on PancakeSwap. Before swapping, you will be able to see the estimated fee.

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/faqs#asusdf-faq)

asUSDF FAQ


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**What is asUSDF?**

asUSDF is an asToken on AsterEarn and the innovative yield-bearing token of stablecoin USDF. To mint asUSDF, stake USDF on AsterEarn. Holding asUSDF allows you to earn additional rewards. The token contract is: 0x917AF46B3C3c6e1Bb7286B9F59637Fb7C65851Fb.

**How is asUSDF APY generated?**

asUSDF APY is generated from delta-neutral strategies which also involve the collection of funding fees. APY is reflected in the net asset value of asUSDF.

**What other yield sources does asUSDF have?**

Minting asUSDF earns you Au points. Au points grant an allocation of the $AST airdrop.

**How is Au calculated?**

This depends on your USDF investment. For example, if you stake 100 USDF, USDF price is $1 and asUSDF Au multiplier is 10x, your mint earns 100 x 1 x 10 = 1,000 Au.

Since USDF is a stablecoin, you will continue earning (100 x 1 x 10) Au per hour.

**Can I withdraw my asUSDF (asUSDF to USDF) at any time?**

Withdrawals will be subject to a T+1 hour waiting period (2 hours). Check your processing withdrawals in the \[Claim\] section. Please note that you will not continue earning Au points and yield during the waiting period. Remember to click \[Claim\] after the waiting period ends.

**Are there any fees involved?**

There are no fees to mint or withdraw asUSDF.

# How USDF works | Aster

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/how-usdf-works#delta-neutral-strategy-and-capital-flows)

Delta-neutral strategy and capital flows


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

USDF offers a decentralized and yield-bearing alternative to traditional stablecoins. Innovative mechanisms ensure stability, risk management, and revenue generation for holders. A critical component of USDF's operation is its integration of a low-risk delta-neutral strategy. Below, we’ll explain how USDF works, the flow of funds, and the delta-neutral positions used to generate revenue.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/how-usdf-works#id-1.-capital-flow-process-for-usdf)

1\. Capital flow process for USDF

The process of minting and using USDF is simple and transparent.

**Step 1: Minting USDF**

Mint USDF with USDT (Tether) at a 1:1 ratio. For example, 100 USDT mints 100 USDF. Once the USDF is minted, the capital moves into a managed process to generate yield.

**Step 2: Transfer to Ceffu Wallet**

After the mint, corresponding USDT funds are transferred to a Ceffu wallet. The Ceffu wallet is a custodial wallet, keeping the USDT secure on behalf of Aster and to prepare for deployment in a yield-generating strategy. This wallet plays a critical role in the management of the funds.

**Step 3: Opening a position on Binance**

The funds in the Ceffu wallet are then sent to Binance, one of the largest cryptocurrency exchanges, to open positions in a carefully managed strategy. Binance is chosen due to its liquidity, efficiency, and support for various trading strategies. The goal is to use these funds for low-risk trading or other revenue-generating opportunities that can provide consistent returns.

**Step 4: Weekly profit distribution**

The profits generated from the trades and strategies employed on Binance are accumulated over a week. Each week, the yield generated is calculated and then distributed to the asUSDF contract. asUSDF is the staked version of USDF, and holders can lock their USDF to receive yield over time. This staking mechanism lets holders earn passive income in addition to the stability USDF provides.

Here’s a simplified flowchart illustrating the process:

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXejq4yVs9TGiY32B9Qia-PWSC07YJXhUubV3-OMQAxLGyEGc3kFSrX3_jhaspC9FCGndAkWPC5LBkL6Qd2ffRFO9Yb7gVUTXFnTfSwQIXjrsFrljqy3K579xtCLP9TMJiCJ6myK%3Fkey%3DYBw161GYKNkAByDTZqA_i60J&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d845ca68&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/how-usdf-works#id-2.-delta-neutral-strategy-for-fee-generation)

2\. Delta-neutral strategy for fee generation

One of the core strategies employed by USDF to generate returns is the delta-neutral strategy. This strategy helps maintain stability and minimize exposure to market volatility, while still allowing holders to earn rewards.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/how-usdf-works#what-is-a-delta-neutral-strategy)

**What is a delta-neutral strategy?**

A delta-neutral strategy involves holding both long and short positions. The goal is to neutralize or balance out the effect of price changes so that no matter which direction the market moves, the overall position remains relatively unchanged in terms of value.

For example, funds could be used in perpetual trading on platforms like Binance. By carefully balancing long and short positions, the strategy ensures that profits are made through the fee generation and the cost of trades, rather than relying solely on price appreciation.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/how-usdf-works#how-does-the-usdf-delta-neutral-strategy-generate-revenue)

**How does the USDF delta-neutral strategy generate revenue?**

The key revenue sources come from:

1.  Trading Fees: Binance, like many exchanges, charges a fee for opening and closing positions. By using a delta-neutral strategy, USDF generates revenue from these fees while reducing risk exposure.
    
2.  Interest Rate Differentials: In cases where leverage is used in trading, USDF can benefit from interest rate differences between various crypto assets or trading pairs, allowing it to generate more income while maintaining a neutral market stance.
    
3.  Stability of Returns: Since the strategy aims to mitigate market volatility, it offers a more stable return profile. Unlike other strategies that are heavily reliant on directional market moves (either up or down), the delta-neutral approach ensures that even in uncertain or bearish market conditions, the system can continue to generate returns for holders.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/how-usdf-works#how-the-delta-neutral-strategy-works-for-usdf)

**How the delta-neutral strategy works for USDF:**

USDF funds deposited into Binance are used to buy spot and short perpetual positions on a specific asset, such as Bitcoin (BTC) or Ether (ETH). Buying spot is effectively ‘long-ing’, and it profits when the price of assets increases. On the other hand, the short position profits when the price decreases. Because these counterbalance each other, the overall net position remains neutral (or close to neutral) in terms of market exposure.

This means that USDF can generate consistent fee income, regardless of asset price movements, making the strategy less sensitive to market volatility. The value of USDF stays consistent, with any gains or losses being offset by the balanced positions.

[PreviousSituating USDF in the stablecoin landscape](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/situating-usdf-in-the-stablecoin-landscape)

Binomial supports asBNB restaking for base yield + Binomial points.

# Situating USDF in the stablecoin landscape | Aster

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/situating-usdf-in-the-stablecoin-landscape#comparisons-with-usdt-usdc-ethena)

Comparisons with USDT, USDC, Ethena


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Stablecoins play a pivotal role in the blockchain ecosystem, offering stability and bridging the gap between volatile cryptocurrencies and stable fiat currencies like the US Dollar. In 2025, the stablecoin market is set to mature and become a mainstream asset class. This growth will be spurred by clearer regulations, more cryptocurrency-friendly legislation and broader adoption. As decentralized finance (DeFi) gain momentum, the stablecoin market is evolving with both centralized and decentralized solutions to meet diverse user needs. Below, we’ll look into major stablecoins like USDT, USDC, and Ethena’s USDe—to see how they compare to USDF. We’ll highlight their differences, potential, and the broader implications for holders especially in market downturns.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/situating-usdf-in-the-stablecoin-landscape#id-1.-centralized-custodial-stablecoins-usdt-usdc)

1\. Centralized custodial stablecoins: USDT/USDC

Centralized stablecoins like USDT (Tether) and USDC (USD Coin) have become the backbone of the stablecoin market due to their high liquidity, transparency, and widespread adoption. Both are pegged to the US Dollar and backed by fiat reserves managed by centralized entities.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/situating-usdf-in-the-stablecoin-landscape#usdt-tether)

**USDT (Tether)**

USDT, issued by Tether Ltd., is the largest stablecoin and the fourth largest cryptocurrency by market capitalization, with over $80 billion in circulation. Its extensive use in cryptocurrency exchanges, DeFi protocols and as a bridge currency in trading pairs makes it a highly liquid asset. Tether generated $13 billion group-wide net profits in 2024 and disclosed $143.7 billion of assets in reserve against $136.6 billion in liabilities, adding up to $7 billion of excess reserves backing its stablecoins. As stablecoins become a mainstream asset class, Tether usage is set to exponentially increase.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/situating-usdf-in-the-stablecoin-landscape#usdc-usd-coin)

**USDC (USD Coin)**

USDC, issued by Circle, is another widely adopted stablecoin in the market with a market cap exceeding $30 billion. USDC is backed by reserve assets held in regulated financial institutions. USDC positions itself as a regulated and transparent option to attract institutional investors. Circle’s monthly transaction volume in November 2024 alone reached $1 trillion, pushing its all-time volume past $18 trillion. According to data from DeFiLlama, stablecoin issuers like Circle and Tether also took the lion’s share for on-chain revenue in December 2024. Circle generated $132.7 million in revenue, only second to Tether’s $532.1 million.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/situating-usdf-in-the-stablecoin-landscape#revenue-and-growth-of-centralized-stablecoins)

**Revenue and growth of centralized stablecoins**

Revenue for centralized stablecoins like USDT and USDC is derived from several sources:

*   Interest on reserves: Both stablecoins hold large amounts of fiat reserves, which are invested in low-risk, interest-generating assets like government bonds. These investments generate income for the issuers.
    
*   Transaction fees: USDT and USDC also generate revenue through fees related to transactions on exchanges and their integration into DeFi protocols.
    

However, their centralized nature introduces several risks: Counterparty risk as they are controlled by a single entity whose solvency and integrity are critical; Transparency issues regarding whether these stablecoins are fully backed by reserves; Regulatory risk as being centralized means they are vulnerable to changes in the regulatory environment which may affect value and legality.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/situating-usdf-in-the-stablecoin-landscape#id-2.-decentralized-stablecoins-ethena-and-dai)

2\. Decentralized stablecoins: Ethena and DAI

Decentralized stablecoins like Ethena’s USDe and DAI operate using smart contracts and thus are not reliant on any central authority. These stablecoins aim to offer greater autonomy, transparency, and decentralization.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/situating-usdf-in-the-stablecoin-landscape#ethena-and-usde)

**Ethena and USDe**

USDe, issued by Ethena, is a synthetic stablecoin designed to provide stability through a delta-neutral hedging mechanism. USDe is backed by synthetic assets and composable with DeFi protocols, helping it to maintain its peg to the US Dollar. The platform also offers high yield opportunities of up to 18% APY by converting USDe into sUSDe.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/situating-usdf-in-the-stablecoin-landscape#dai)

**DAI**

DAI, issued by MakerDAO, is a decentralized stablecoin that is collateralized by a mix of cryptocurrencies such as Ethereum. DAI maintains its peg to the US Dollar through a decentralized system powered by smart contracts on the Ethereum blockchain. Collateral is stored in Collateralized Debt Positions (CDPs), or vaults, and DAI is over-collateralized to account for volatility. MakerDAO also enables users to earn yield by participating in governance and utilizing DAI in various DeFi applications.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/situating-usdf-in-the-stablecoin-landscape#revenue-and-growth-of-decentralized-stablecoins)

**Revenue and growth of decentralized stablecoins**

*   Ethena (USDe): The main revenue for Ethena comes from its DeFi ecosystem, where holders participate in liquidity provision, staking, and yield generation.
    
*   DAI: The MakerDAO ecosystem enables holders to lock collateral into smart contracts to mint DAI. MakerDAO also generates revenue through fees and governance tokens, allowing holders to participate in the protocol's decision-making and share in its growth. DAI is widely used across DeFi protocols, contributing to its growth and adoption.
    

Both Ethena and DAI have seen considerable growth due to increasing demand for DeFi. As DeFi matures, decentralized stablecoins will continue to play a crucial role in providing liquidity and stability to the ecosystem.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/situating-usdf-in-the-stablecoin-landscape#id-3.-ethenas-model-and-its-limitations-during-bear-markets)

3\. Ethena's model and its limitations during bear markets

USDF’s model is most similar to Ethena’s USDe in offering high yield opportunities. However, USDe’s model has certain limitations during market downturns, especially when negative fee rates become prevalent in a bear market.

**Challenges during bear markets**

Ethena’s reliance on high-risk strategies like synthetic assets may expose it to more volatility, making yield generation unsustainable in prolonged market downturns or during periods of long-term negative fee rates. This can result in yield losses, as the synthetic asset positions become more vulnerable. Additionally, the high yield offered during bull markets can significantly reverse during bear market conditions, leading to reduced returns.

**USDF’s bear market resilience**

Aster’ USDF addresses this issue by integrating decentralized stablecoin strategies while incorporating advanced risk management to deal with market volatility. During negative fee periods or bear markets, USDF will look to diversify its revenue streams such as integrating DAI lending strategies. This could look like leveraging DAI’s collateralized lending platform, allowing for a more stable return during market stagnation or downturn.

A multi-strategy approach including DeFi lending and synthetic asset exposure ensures that holders can continue to earn rewards and remain resilient against market downturns. This diversified strategy helps hedge against negative fee periods, ensuring that USDF holders don’t face significant losses.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/situating-usdf-in-the-stablecoin-landscape#id-4.-usdf-vs-other-stablecoins-key-comparisons-and-the-road-ahead)

4\. USDF vs other stablecoins: Key comparisons and the road ahead

USDF combines the benefits of decentralized ownership and high yields, giving it a distinct edge over centralized competitors like USDT and USDC. When compared to other decentralized stablecoins like USDe and DAI, USDF stands out for its robust risk management features and its ability to diversify income sources during adverse market conditions.

*   Decentralized nature vs centralized custodianship: While USDT and USDC are centralized, offering stability and scalability, USDF introduces a decentralized mechanism for greater security and transparency.
    
*   Bear market resilience: Unlike USDe, which is vulnerable to negative fee rates and prolonged market downturns, USDF can adapt by utilizing DeFi strategies like DAI lending to generate consistent returns, providing better stability for holders.
    
*   Potential for institutional adoption: USDF's focus on decentralized mechanisms and the regulatory compliance of underlying USDT funds makes it an attractive option for institutional investors—who need both stability and regulatory assurance, setting it apart from other decentralized alternatives.
    

[PreviousUSDF Stablecoin](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin)
[NextHow USDF works](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/how-usdf-works)

Last updated 5 months ago

It features MEV-free, one-click execution in Simple Mode. Pro Mode adds 24/7 stock perpetuals, Hidden Orders, and grid trading, available across BNB Chain, Ethereum, Solana, and Arbitrum.

# Overview | Aster

Aster is a next-generation decentralized exchange offering both Perpetual and Spot trading, designed as a one-stop onchain venue for global crypto traders. It features MEV-free, one-click execution in Simple Mode. Pro Mode adds 24/7 stock perpetuals, Hidden Orders, and grid trading, available across BNB Chain, Ethereum, Solana, and Arbitrum.

Its unique edge lies in the ability to offer liquid-staking tokens (asBNB) or yield-generating stablecoins (USDF) as collateral, unlocking unparalleled capital efficiency. Powered by Aster Chain, a high-performance and privacy-focused L1, and backed by YZi Labs, Aster is building the future of DeFi: fast, flexible, and community-first.

At the heart of this ecosystem is the $ASTER token, a core asset that decentralizes governance, drives growth, rewards participation, and supports long-term sustainability.

*   Ticker: $ASTER
    
*   Maximum supply: 8,000,000,000
    
*   Token format: BEP-20 on Binance Smart Chain
    
*   Token address: 0x000Ae314E2A2172a039B26378814C252734f556A

# FAQs | Aster

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-4-harvest/faqs#q-what-are-the-points)

Q: What are the points?

Points are [Aster Stage 4](https://www.asterdex.com/en/stage4/statistics)
 airdrop points for trading on Aster Perpetual and Spot (1001x is not included).

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-4-harvest/faqs#q-how-are-points-calculated)

Q: How are points calculated?

Points = (Trade points +Position points + **Aster Assets points** + Liquidation points +Profit points + Loss points) × Team boost + Referral points

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-4-harvest/faqs#q-does-a-higher-score-always-mean-a-bigger-airdrop)

Q: Does a higher score always mean a bigger airdrop?

Aster does not encourage hedging or wash trading to farm points. To ensure fairness, adjustments are applied to farmed points; points shown may not reflect final allocation.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-4-harvest/faqs#q-how-are-trade-points-calculated)

Q: How are trade points calculated?

In [Stage 4](https://www.asterdex.com/en/stage4/statistics)
, both spot and perpetual trading are counted.

**Trade Points** are now calculated based on your trading fee contribution, liquidity (maker order) contribution and symbol boost factor.Updated hourly.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-4-harvest/faqs#q-what-is-symbol-boost-on-trade-points)

Q:What is Symbol Boost on Trade Points?

It’s a limited-time boost on Trade Points for ASTER-designated symbols. Trade the eligible symbols to receive an extra multiplier on your Trade Points

Your final Trade Points will be equal to your previous Trade Points multiplied by the symbol’s boost factor.

Only the Trade Points generated from trading the boosted symbol will receive this multiplier — others will remain unchanged.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-4-harvest/faqs#q-how-are-position-points-calculated)

Q: How are position points calculated?

Based on both the duration and size of your positions. Aster does not encourage long-term hedging positions to farm points. To ensure fairness, adjustments are applied to farmed points; points shown may not reflect final allocation.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-4-harvest/faqs#q-how-are-aster-assets-points-calculated)

Q: How are Aster Assets points calculated?

Based on the margin size (only in cross-margin mode) when opening positions each day, and on the proportion of Aster/asBNB/USDF in your portfolio. The larger your margin and the higher your share of Aster assets, the more points you earn.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-4-harvest/faqs#q-how-are-liquidation-points-calculated)

Q: How are Liquidation points calculated?

Liquidation Points are calculated from the liquidation fees incurred at the time of liquidation. The more liquidation fees a user generates, the more Liquidation Points they receive.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-4-harvest/faqs#q-how-are-profit-and-loss-points-calculated)

Q: How are profit and loss points calculated?

Points are based on your net profit or loss each hour. The timing follows the schedule shown on this page. Do not attempt to game the system by closing offsetting positions right before and after the hourly cutoff to double-count profit and loss points. Doing so may delay your points from being added.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-4-harvest/faqs#q-how-does-the-referral-bonus-work)

Q: How does the referral bonus work?

Earn a share of your invitees’ based on the total points of your invitees and their invitees. Points earned from first-level invitees are higher than those from second-level invitees. Updated daily.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-4-harvest/faqs#q-how-does-team-boost-work)

Q: How does team boost work?

When a team’s cumulative points reach a certain threshold, the team unlocks a boost multiplier. The boost takes effect a few hours after joining a team. In Stage 4, team boosts accumulate throughout the campaign and do not reset.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-4-harvest/faqs#q-why-my-point-is-lower-than-others-with-similar-trades)

Q:Why my point is lower than others with similar trades?

Aster encourage the user get points via normal trade, any abnormal operations include but not limited to brush trade will lead to a decrease of your point weight.

[PreviousTeam boosts](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-4-harvest/team-boosts)
[NextOverview](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdaster/overview)

Last updated 7 days ago

# How to claim your Airdrop | Aster

How to claim $ASTER Airdrop

Users will have up to 30 days to claim the airdrop via [Aster’s website](https://www.asterdex.com/en/airdrop)
. After Oct 17 2025, all unclaimed tokens will be redirected to support the ecosystem’s development initiatives.

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdaster/tge/how-to-claim-your-airdrop#check-your-eligibility)

Check Your Eligibility


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Users can check their token eligibility for the airdrop and claim their tokens by following these steps:

1\. Navigate to [](http://list.org/)
Aster, and open the “$ASTER Airdrop” Tab in the header navigation bar at the top and click "Claim Airdrop”. You can also access the Aster official Airdrop page [here](https://www.asterdex.com/en/airdrop)

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FNFX6dcZsOzWXIkNvCXl1%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-17%252017.03.54.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9e7d2a13-6b2a-450a-9102-afde26f6b689&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3295cae9&sv=2)

2\. Once eligibility checks are available on 11 September 07:00 UTC+0, check your airdrop amount by connecting your wallet and click on “check your eligibility”:

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FNUKUQuRaehWNT5FZwVKx%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-17%252017.05.02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2a2aa177-dc67-4c78-8294-ffb7d6c2cd74&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=38664fc6&sv=2)

1.  After you click the button of Click eligibility, you will be able to see the amount of Aster airdrop tokens on your Aster account.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FtB3dneN2F9JNH6PRDLLX%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-17%252017.06.53.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dde479a4b-75d3-4a78-80cd-981da75f3117&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a1d739df&sv=2)

4\. You should be able to claim your Aster Airdrop once the Airdrop claim goes live on 17 September, 09:00 UTC+0. Click on “Claim” and confirm the transaction.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FTci77n5MNvK3qpU0xIwY%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-17%252017.05.53.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D691fc324-3b71-45a0-b35c-aedcec7cbd45&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6939c699&sv=2)

_Note\* Claiming airdrops does not require any authorization, or in other words, “approve” transactions. Please be vigilant and verify that any page requesting “approval” is an official page to avoid potential phishing scams._

5\. Please check check balance to see your Aster token balance. You will be notified and the tokens will be in your [Aster Spot account](https://www.asterdex.com/en/spot/ASTERUSDT)
 after the claim.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F5knWECopQTNwd0fpv2Ne%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-17%252017.11.52.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7e7d4dee-c45d-427d-b7de-53d72e8dfed3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=822954db&sv=2)

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FSclzAxfysMOCqRWGYi9k%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-17%252017.15.09.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1bd50e1d-5a9d-465f-bc40-dec608bd194d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8a2680ce&sv=2)

1.  Be aware of phishing scams and make sure that you click on the official airdrop link: https://www.asterdex.com/en/airdrop

# Yield strategies | Aster

👉 [**Visit Ecosystem**](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn/ecosystem)

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/yield-strategies#yield-strategies-yieldnest)

Y**ield strategies** - YieldNest


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[YieldNest](https://app.yieldnest.finance/)
 is a next-generation liquid restaking protocol that offers simple, high-yielding, risk-adjusted restaking and DeFi strategies. It merges DeFi's best strategies into single, unified, high-powered assets with L1 settlement assurances. Powered & Secured by DeFAI.

YieldNest utilizes asBNB restaking as one underlying strategy to generate yields for its ynBNBx multi-asset vault.

_Please note that_ _**you do not receive asBNB tokens**_ _when you stake wBNB into the ynBNBx vault on YieldNest. Check with YieldNest about ynBNBx yield._

[PreviousRestaking](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/restaking)
[NextUSDF Stablecoin](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin)

# Unlock APX tokens in APX DAO | Aster

You can unlock your veNFT and retrieve all your $APX tokens without penalties on September 16. Kindly please follow the step-to-step instructions to unlock the APX tokens without penalties.

First Step: Go to [APX DAO staking page](https://www.apollox.finance/en/governance/vault)
 and connect your wallet.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FSni01okDx5NNDhRjLxJ0%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-16%252010.13.31.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D22f0f695-d530-4a78-b123-e0a252036ac8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=931b9cab&sv=2)

Second Step: Claim all your rewards first before unlocking the current veNFT.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FFuukAkTIl2MhyVK2ojbz%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-10%252012.52.08.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfc482c46-fef4-4ece-8a25-b835022d2050&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b577f93b&sv=2)

Third Step: Click the button of “Instant unlock” to withdraw your $APX tokens without penalties.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FytozPwFgEjsyb06zFSkC%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-10%252012.51.03.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df3493a78-e2d7-4072-bbf1-8408860e5101&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3a8b68d&sv=2)

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FK4DlKc6orWPjn7nrq6xX%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-16%252010.56.05.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1553eb11-c75e-4d52-ab5c-d9813db88835&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fa6c8e3c&sv=2)

Last Step: Click the button of "Unlock Now", then you will receive APX tokens in your wallet.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FMRRGH5jfY1G6QVPA4naV%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-16%252010.56.45.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D22fb14ef-a651-4df7-835a-1d2920fb2a55&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9722fb44&sv=2)

Once you have unlocked all veNFT and receive all APX tokens. You could deposit all APX tokens to Aster dex and exchange all APX tokens into ASTER tokens.

# Pendle | Aster

👉 [**Visit Ecosystem**](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn/ecosystem)

**Note:**

*   **Those who split Aster Earn assets into PT and YT without further activity on Pendle are exploiting the Au points reward system. Aster prioritizes real activity like providing liquidity or trading PT and YT on Pendle. To protect the interests of genuine DeFi holders and encourage healthy activity, exploiters may lose all Au points.**
    
*   **The Au Points Program will officially sunset and a snapshot of Au Points balances will be taken at 00:00:00 UTC on Friday, June 13, 2025. No further Au Points will be granted after this point.** [**Read more**](https://x.com/Aster_DEX/status/1932367398872760416)
    **.** _**Last updated: June 10, 2025**_
    

* * *

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle#basic-concepts)

Basic concepts


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfe1WOOqTr9fmA9qX4_ZxxBoEafXn_8ffRVuAuWoPI32JHcAHoO3jgWcPuxlvL0NEJSTt9wciLnFzlQ7YcinQsCyM_fsTSVLezux8S6e33h3H0FcYLVgDcD8c_XH1692ewqPm1l_Q%3Fkey%3DJ3kbZi7pcl1auuw3TlOIrsy5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7b273caf&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle#sy)

SY:

*   A token standard on Pendle for wrapping yield-bearing tokens.
    
*   SY is then split into PT and YT.
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle#pt)

PT:

*   Represents the principal of the underlying yield-bearing token.
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle#yt)

YT:

*   Represents all the yield of the asset.
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle#lp)

LP:

*   The LP token you get after adding liquidity.
    

[PreviousLP on PancakeSwap](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pancakeswap/lp-on-pancakeswap)
[NextasUSDF on Pendle](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/asusdf-on-pendle)

# LP on PancakeSwap | Aster

**The Au Points Program will officially sunset and a snapshot of Au Points balances will be taken at 00:00:00 UTC on Friday, June 13, 2025. No further Au Points will be granted after this point.** [**Read more**](https://x.com/Aster_DEX/status/1932367398872760416)
**.** _**Last updated: June 10, 2025**_

* * *

**Page Summary**

[1\. Mint & Hold asToken StableSwap LPs](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pancakeswap/lp-on-pancakeswap#id-1.-mint-and-hold-astoken-stableswap-lps)

[2\. Stake StableSwap LPs](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pancakeswap/lp-on-pancakeswap#c05a)

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pancakeswap/lp-on-pancakeswap#id-1.-mint-and-hold-astoken-stableswap-lps)

1\. Mint & Hold asToken StableSwap LPs


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Earn Au points for minting & holding [**StableSwap LP**](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn/ecosystem)
 **tokens**.

*   **If you mint V3 LP tokens, you do not get Au points.**
    
*   **Minting StableSwap LP is NOT the same as LP staking.**
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252Fu9r8XjE4zgXb2G9I0dTz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8d5dbf52-ddd5-4d5c-8b9d-9d0670c29be9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dfc010c0&sv=2)

*   USDF/USDT StableSwap LP: 35x Au
    
*   asUSDF/USDF StableSwap LP: 30x Au
    
*   asUSDF/USDT StableSwap LP: 25x Au
    
*   asCAKE/CAKE StableSwap LP: 2x Au
    

**How is Au calculated?**

Au points are accrued based on the USD value of the StableSwap LP tokens minted. For example, if you add liquidity to the asUSDF/USDT stable LP on PancakeSwap, which has a 25x Au multiplier, and minted 20 USD worth of stable LP tokens, you should get 20 x 25 = 500 Au. You will continue earning 500 Au/hour.

* * *

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pancakeswap/lp-on-pancakeswap#c05a)

2\. Stake StableSwap LPs


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Please note that LP Staking is NOT the same as minting & holding** [**StableSwap LPs**](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn/ecosystem)
**. LP Staking is only available for the following StableSwap pairs:**

*   USDF/USDT StableSwap LP: 35x Au + APR
    
*   asUSDF/USDT StableSwap LP: 25x Au + APR
    

**How do I stake my StableSwap LP?**

Please connect your wallet to PancakeSwap and go to \[My Positions\]. If you already hold StableSwap LPs, click \[Stake LP\] and confirm.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FUTCxjGjjcyaHzeRWwOO6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9bda713-081b-4ed5-a8c9-7107deb21989&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6a5ceec4&sv=2)

**How is Au calculated?**

Au multiplier for staking a StableSwap LP is the same as the multiplier for minting and holding. For example, minting and holding asUSDF/USDT stable LP has a 25x Au multiplier. Staking asUSDF/USDT stable LP thus also has a 25x Au multiplier.

Scenario:

*   If you have 20 USD worth of asUSDF/USDT stable LP and staked all of it, you continue earning 20 x 25 = 500 Au/hour.
    
*   If you stake 10 USD worth of asUSDF/USDT stable LP and continue holding 10 USD worth of asUSDF/USDT stable LP, you will earn 10 x 25 = 250 Au/hour from staking and 10 x 25 = 250 Au/hour from holding.
    

**What does APR consist of?**

When you stake StableSwap LPs on PancakeSwap, you also earn Combined APR in the form of CAKE tokens. Combined APR consists of Farm APR and LP fee APR. Please read this for more details about Farm APR: [https://docs.pancakeswap.finance/products/yield-farming](https://docs.pancakeswap.finance/products/yield-farming)

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FMQOVMQCcaSvGufc8sGRH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df6e0cc3d-75df-42af-af00-b876b2640643&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c7e5b5bf&sv=2)

**How do I collect CAKE token rewards?**

Go to your staked positions and click \[Harvest\] to collect CAKE rewards.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FYeN7pXcf7t2e1mmqJbKO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd6000a0b-2966-4f04-9de4-6713234361bd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=545bad27&sv=2)

[PreviousPancakeSwap](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pancakeswap)
[NextPendle](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle)

Last updated 5 months ago
