# Tranchess | Aster

**The Au Points Program will officially sunset and a snapshot of Au Points balances will be taken at 00:00:00 UTC on Friday, June 13, 2025. No further Au Points will be granted after this point.** [**Read more**](https://x.com/Aster_DEX/status/1932367398872760416)
**.** _**Last updated: June 10, 2025**_

* * *

👉 [**Visit Ecosystem**](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn/ecosystem)

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/tranchess#basic-concepts)

Basic Concepts


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/tranchess#asbnbqueen)

asBNBQUEEN:

*   Swap asBNBQUEEN 1:1 with asBNB. Every asBNBQUEEN can be split into 0.1 turPasBNB and 0.9 staYasBNB. Similarly, every 1 turPasBNB and 9 staYasBNB can be merged into 10 asBNBQUEEN. The ratio is always 1⇌0.1+0.9.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FeNWx474TEqpnZ6qi6fnv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ded77a961-26e1-485e-8e6e-ea803acadedf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=21f157c3&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/tranchess#turpasbnb)

turPasBNB:

*   Short for "Turbo Point asBNB", turPasBNB turbocharges your speed of earning asBNB points.
    
*   turPasBNB earns you Au points, HODLer airdrops, and Megadrops. Tranchess will distribute HODLer airdrops and Megadrops.
    
*   You can swap turPasBNB back to asBNB anytime via Tranchess’ Swap function or hold it until the fund ends, when turPasBNB will be converted back to asBNB based on their fair value.
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/tranchess#stayasbnb)

staYasBNB:

*   Short for "Stable Yield asBNB", staYasBNB earns a fixed interest of 20%.
    
*   You do not earn Au points, HODLer airdrops or Megadrops.
    
*   You can swap staYasBNB back to asBNB anytime via Tranchess’ Swap function or hold it until the fund ends, when staYasBNB will be converted back to asBNB based on their fair values.
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/tranchess#stayasbnb-asbnb-lp)

staYasBNB-asBNB LP:

*   You receive LP tokens by providing liquidity to the LP pool. You can add or withdraw liquidity anytime in pairs or single assets.
    
*   LP holders collect a basket of yield: Au points, CHESS rewards, Trading fee, Partial interest from staYasBNB.
    
*   LP holders earn HODLer airdrops and Megadrops. Tranchess will distribute HODLer airdrops and Megadrops.
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/tranchess#faq)

FAQ

**How do I get Au points?**

Tranchess will record your Au points allocation in their system and will distribute Aster token airdrop to you after Aster TGE. Note that you will not be able to see your Au points on Aster' airdrop dashboard. Please check with Tranchess' support team.

**How do I get HODLer airdrops and Megadrops?**

Tranchess will distribute these rewards to eligible holders. Please check with Tranchess' support team directly.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/tranchess#read-tranchess-asbnb-wiki-to-learn-more)

[Read **Tranchess' asBNB wiki to learn more.**](https://tranchess.notion.site/Tranchess-asBNB-Fund-User-Guide-1b2ce8b3d9e3806ba639f21fa0a83744)

[PreviousHow to transfer liquidity to new pool](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/how-to-transfer-liquidity-to-new-pool)
[NextRestaking](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/restaking)

Last updated 5 months ago

# Exchange APX to Aster | Aster

If you have $APX tokens in a decentralized wallet, please follow the step-to-step tutorial to exchange $APX tokens to $ASTER tokens.

First step: Connect your wallet on [Aster token exchange page](https://www.asterdex.com/en/apx-upgrade)
, sign the confirmation request to complete the process.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FmUZANvY4KRi5AaNt3Yqn%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-16%252017.55.51.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D179e5b5e-4046-413d-bc1b-9e43f8c9b6d8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=109b777e&sv=2)

Second step: Click the button of deposit, deposit $APX tokens to your Aster Spot account.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FfKo2Uynpxr8Q5AeJXQFK%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-16%252017.57.45.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8171cc01-375e-4ccf-afd3-1e02cba3d676&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=61751b6b&sv=2)

Third step: Input the $APX amount and click the button of “exchange” to complete the transaction based on the current exchange ratio. Kindly please note that the exchange ratio will decrease over time.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FbV5l19WIpWu0CBkmfc87%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-17%252018.02.45.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8930898c-ddf8-48c3-bf60-f6b16ae254d1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=591f6146&sv=2)

Last step: After this, you could see $ASTER token balance in your [Spot account](https://www.asterdex.com/en/spot/CDLUSD1)
. You can trade the $ASTER tokens on the Spot trading page when trading opens or withdraw the $ASTER tokens to your crypto wallet when withdrawals are live.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FwcNyY5nFUV8HOFEXsCvJ%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-17%252018.04.11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D366ca87f-d30a-4bd8-96a8-d080e612a614&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e3c4f7c&sv=2)

# asBNB on Pendle | Aster

**Note:**

*   **Those who split asUSDF into PT and YT without further activity on Pendle are exploiting the Au points reward system. Aster prioritizes real activity like providing liquidity or trading PT and YT on Pendle. To protect the interests of genuine DeFi holders and encourage healthy activity, exploiters may lose all Au points.**
    
*   **The Au Points Program will officially sunset and a snapshot of Au Points balances will be taken at 00:00:00 UTC on Friday, June 13, 2025. No further Au Points will be granted after this point.** [**Read more**](https://x.com/Aster_DEX/status/1932367398872760416)
    **.** _**Last updated: June 10, 2025**_
    

* * *

asBNB is a liquid staking token of BNB. It brings BNB yields that are traditionally restricted to CeFi users and CeFi applications onchain. On Aster, you will stake slisBNB or BNB to mint asBNB. You will earn Binance launchpool rewards, HODLer airdrops and Megadrops. You also earn 5x Au points when you mint asBNB on Aster. Read more about asBNB:

[Mint asBNB](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asbnb)

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/asbnb-on-pendle#basic-concepts)

Basic concepts


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfe1WOOqTr9fmA9qX4_ZxxBoEafXn_8ffRVuAuWoPI32JHcAHoO3jgWcPuxlvL0NEJSTt9wciLnFzlQ7YcinQsCyM_fsTSVLezux8S6e33h3H0FcYLVgDcD8c_XH1692ewqPm1l_Q%3Fkey%3DJ3kbZi7pcl1auuw3TlOIrsy5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7b273caf&sv=2)

SY:

*   A token standard on Pendle for wrapping yield-bearing tokens. For example, when you deposit asBNB, asBNB is automatically wrapped into SY-asBNB. This happens on the backend, so you don’t have to deal with conversion between SY and asBNB.
    
*   SY is then split into PT and YT.
    

PT:

*   Represents the principal of the underlying yield-bearing token. For example, PT-asBNB represents the principal of asBNB (i.e. does not include asBNB yield or Au points)
    

YT:

*   Represents all the yield of the asset. For example, YT-asBNB represents the yield and Au points you can get from asBNB.
    

LP:

*   The LP token you get after adding liquidity. For example, you get LP-asBNB after adding asBNB liquidity.
    

* * *

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/asbnb-on-pendle#provide-liquidity)

Provide liquidity


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you provide asBNB liquidity, you get LP-asBNB. LP-asBNB is perfect for those who want to earn Aster yield, Pendle yield and Au points.

LP yield includes 10x Au points, Underlying Yield, PT fixed yield, $PENDLE incentives and Pendle swap fees.

LP holders also earn HODLer airdrops and Megadrops. Claim them on the Aster website.

* * *

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/asbnb-on-pendle#pt-asbnb)

PT-asBNB


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PT-asBNB represents the principal portion of asBNB. Thus, 1 PT-asBNB is equivalent to the value of 1 asBNB excluding asBNB yields and Au points.

If you're bullish on asBNB, PT-asBNB lets you buy in at a fixed rate discount as it is traded at a discount to asBNB.

*   **Fixed APY**: The value of PT-asBNB will gradually increase and become equal to the value of the asBNB at maturity. This process creates a fixed guaranteed return ('fixed APY'). For example, let's say PT-asBNB offers a fixed APY of 23% with maturity on 24 July 2025. This means that PT-asBNB holders get a guaranteed return of 23% APY if held till maturity. You DO NOT earn asBNB underlying yield or Au points.
    
*   **What you can do**: Hold till maturity OR trade PT-asBNB on Pendle anytime.
    

* * *

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/asbnb-on-pendle#yt-asbnb)

YT-asBNB


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

YT-asBNB represents the yield portion of the underlying asset asBNB. Thus, 1 YT-asBNB represents the yield and Au points you can earn from 1 asBNB.

If you are a yield-maxi, YT-asBNB helps to leverage your yield exposure. Buying YT-asBNB means that you are 'longing the yield' of asBNB.

*   **YT yield**:
    
    *   YT-asBNB lets you earn asBNB yield and 10x Au points till maturity. asBNB yield from launchpool rewards is reflected in NAV. Au points accumulate hourly and you can check Au points on the Aster Airdrop dashboard.
        
    *   YT-asBNB holders also earn HODLer airdrops and Megadrops. Claim them on the Aster website.
        
    *   The value of YT-asBNB will naturally trend towards $0 as there is less remaining yield the closer we get to maturity. Holders profit when the total yield collected up to that point ends up being higher than their cost of buying YT-asBNB.
        
    
*   **What you can do**: Hold till maturity OR trade YT-asBNB on Pendle anytime.
    

[PreviousasUSDF on Pendle](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/asusdf-on-pendle)
[NextUSDF on Pendle](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/usdf-on-pendle)

Last updated 5 months ago

# USDF on Pendle | Aster

**Note:**

*   **Those who split asUSDF into PT and YT without further activity on Pendle are exploiting the Au points reward system. Aster prioritizes real activity like providing liquidity or trading PT and YT on Pendle. To protect the interests of genuine DeFi holders and encourage healthy activity, exploiters may lose all Au points.**
    
*   **The Au Points Program will officially sunset and a snapshot of Au Points balances will be taken at 00:00:00 UTC on Friday, June 13, 2025. No further Au Points will be granted after this point.** [**Read more**](https://x.com/Aster_DEX/status/1932367398872760416)
    **.** _**Last updated: June 10, 2025**_
    

* * *

USDF is a yield-bearing stablecoin. On Aster, you will stake USDT to mint USDF. You earn 35x Au points when you mint USDF on Aster. Read more about USDF:

[USDF Stablecoin](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin)

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/usdf-on-pendle#basic-concepts)

Basic concepts


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfe1WOOqTr9fmA9qX4_ZxxBoEafXn_8ffRVuAuWoPI32JHcAHoO3jgWcPuxlvL0NEJSTt9wciLnFzlQ7YcinQsCyM_fsTSVLezux8S6e33h3H0FcYLVgDcD8c_XH1692ewqPm1l_Q%3Fkey%3DJ3kbZi7pcl1auuw3TlOIrsy5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7b273caf&sv=2)

SY:

*   A token standard on Pendle for wrapping yield-bearing tokens. For example, when you deposit USDF, USDF is automatically wrapped into SY-USDF. This happens on the backend, so you don’t have to deal with conversion between SY and USDF.
    
*   SY is then split into PT and YT.
    

PT:

*   Represents the principal of the underlying yield-bearing token. For example, PT-USDF represents the principal of USDF (i.e. does not include Au points).

*   Represents all the yield of the asset. For example, YT-USDF represents the Au points you can get from USDF.

*   The LP token you get after adding liquidity. For example, you get LP-USDF after adding USDF liquidity.

LP yield includes 35x Au points, PT fixed yield, $PENDLE incentives, and Pendle swap fees.

* * *

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/usdf-on-pendle#pt-usdf)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PT-USDF represents the principal portion of USDF. Thus, 1 PT-USDF is equivalent to the value of 1 USDF excluding Au points.

For example, let's say PT-USDF offers a fixed APY of 15% with maturity on 24 July 2025. This means that PT-USDF holders get a guaranteed return of 15% APY if held till maturity. The value of YT-USDF will naturally trend towards $0 as there is less remaining yield the closer we get to maturity. Holders profit when the total yield collected up to that point ends up being higher than their cost of buying YT-USDF.

# Mint asCAKE | Aster

**Note:**

*   **Due to the new CAKE Tokenomics 3.0 Proposal taking into effect, the veCAKE and Gauges Voting System have been retired. asCAKE minting has been stopped.** _**Last updated: Apr. 23, 2025**_
    
*   **asCAKE redemptions to CAKE are now available on Aster.** _**Last updated: Apr. 27, 2025**_
    
*   **The Au Points Program will officially sunset and a snapshot of Au Points balances will be taken at 00:00:00 UTC on Friday, June 13, 2025. No further Au Points will be granted after this point.** [**Read more**](https://x.com/Aster_DEX/status/1932367398872760416)
    **.** _**Last updated: June 10, 2025**_
    

* * *

**Page summary**

[How to mint asCAKE](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-ascake#how-to-mint-ascake)

[How to redeem asCAKE](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-ascake#how-to-redeem-ascake)

[asCAKE FAQ](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-ascake#ascake-faq)

Aster presents asCAKE, an innovative liquid staking derivative where you can stake your CAKE to mint asCAKE. asCAKE maximizes your CAKE utility and real yields:

*   APY from veCAKE yield (veCAKE Pool yield + Revenue Sharing yield), reflected in the net asset value of asCAKE.
    
*   APY from voting rewards (Bribes), reflected in the net asset value of asCAKE.
    
*   1x Au Points Multiplier for Aster airdrop
    

Stringent risk control measures ensure safety. Smart contracts are fully audited to guarantee their reliability. Please read asCAKE FAQs below.

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-ascake#how-to-mint-ascake)

How to mint asCAKE


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Once you have CAKE, go to [AsterEarn](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn)
    . Select asCAKE from the dropdown menu. Click \[Connect Wallet\] and sign the message.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F9EtIhSIy0m3Qp24vTOPf%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-23%252019.07.19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d9e371a-0c49-4c4e-8b38-b2021024922b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1b4d29c8&sv=2)

1.  Select \[Deposit\]. Click \[Approve CAKE\]. Currently, you can only stake CAKE using the BSC chain.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FgYPoNZuWxt9EEj4nhD3o%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De524713f-149e-4019-b437-67be6cff50c3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fecf348f&sv=2)

1.  Enter your CAKE value. Click \[Smart Mint asCAKE\]. Smart Mint is a mechanism to optimize CAKE to asCAKE rates so you get the best conversion rate. Using Smart Mint, Aster will select between the conversion rate on AsterEarn or the conversion rate on the CAKE/asCAKE liquidity pool on PancakeSwap. Click the confirm button to proceed. Do note that minting asCAKE is irreversible.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FUYWPabwwSVBUI59c9ODH%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-23%252019.10.19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1b7f6d23-ccf6-4359-938b-c3dfe32049be&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a6d6a4b8&sv=2)

1.  Once confirmed, you have minted asCAKE successfully.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FpFNzcjtBdLuN6O9maMwn%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-23%252019.11.16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4fda8958-d6cd-41b8-bee0-5a1fb1b48337&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a5a7e33a&sv=2)

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-ascake#how-to-obtain-cake)

How to obtain CAKE


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You need CAKE to mint asCAKE. If you don’t already hold CAKE, you can [buy CAKE on PancakeSwap](https://pancakeswap.finance/)
. If you had previously deposited CAKE on Aster, you can stake it on AsterEarn.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-ascake#method-1-swap-cake-on-pancakeswap)

Method 1: Swap CAKE on PancakeSwap

Read [PancakeSwap’s tutorial on how to trade](https://docs.pancakeswap.finance/products/pancakeswap-exchange/trade-guide)
.

1.  Go to the PancakeSwap [Swap page.](https://docs.google.com/document/d/1fNJREb_QJ42gnYDdfhahhBhvKIOzDdLmwnJEzTJmBRg/edit?tab=t.0)
    
2.  Connect Wallet to PancakeSwap.
    
3.  Choose the token you want to trade from the dropdown menu in the upper section. Make sure you have a sufficient amount of them in your wallet to trade with. Your balance is shown above the token dropdown menu.
    
4.  Choose CAKE in the lower section.
    
5.  Next, either type an amount in the upper section to input the number of tokens you want to swap (spending amount). Or, type an amount in the lower section to input the number of tokens you want to swap to (receiving amount).
    
6.  Whichever section you input your amount, the amount in the other section will be estimated automatically.
    
7.  Check all the details, and click the Swap button.
    
8.  If you are trading a token for the first time, you may first need to click "Enable XXX (your token)" to approve.
    
9.  A window with more details will appear. Check the details are correct. When you are ready, click the Confirm Swap button. Your wallet will ask you to confirm the action.
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-ascake#method-2-stake-cake-from-aster-deposit-account)

Method 2: Stake CAKE from Aster Deposit Account

If you had previously deposited CAKE on Aster, you can stake it on AsterEarn.

Step 1: Withdraw your CAKE from Aster to your personal wallet.

Step 2: Go to the AsterEarn page. Select asCAKE from the dropdown menu, then click \[Approve CAKE\].

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-ascake#how-to-redeem-ascake)

How to redeem asCAKE


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Redeem asCAKE for CAKE directly on Aster. Go to the asCAKE page and click \[Withdraw\]. Connect your wallet and complete the steps to get back CAKE.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FOflt0XNSKb3TyrDCsPpz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D13ff7d61-9e44-4152-8b36-1e26a17fcaef&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3edfc08d&sv=2)

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-ascake#ascake-faq)

asCAKE FAQ


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Note:**

*   **Due to the new CAKE Tokenomics 3.0 Proposal taking into effect, the veCAKE and Gauges Voting System have been retired. asCAKE minting has been stopped.** _**Last updated: Apr. 23, 2025**_
    
*   **asCAKE redemptions to CAKE are now available on Aster.** _**Last updated: Apr. 27, 2025**_
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-ascake#what-is-ascake)

What is asCAKE?

asCAKE is an asToken minted by staking CAKE on AsterEarn. The token contract address is: 0x9817F4c9f968a553fF6caEf1a2ef6cF1386F16F7.

**How is APY from veCAKE yield generated?**

Your staked CAKE on AsterEarn will be staked on PancakeSwap to get veCAKE and earn yield. veCAKE yield consists of veCAKE Pool yield + Revenue Sharing yield. Aster will collect veCAKE yield weekly and update these returns in asCAKE net asset value (NAV) within 7 days.

**How is APY from voting rewards (bribes) generated?**

Through veCAKE, Aster obtains voting rights. We partner with projects to generate returns from Bribes (such as, voting for gauges on PancakeSwap in return for bribes from the projects).

Aster collects rewards from Bribes every 2 weeks, and updates these returns in asCAKE’s NAV within 14 days.

**How do I get the Au Multiplier?**

By minting asCAKE, you automatically earn Au points. Au points give you an allocation of $AST airdrop. Connect your wallet to check your Au points here: [https://www.asterdex.com/en/stage1/leaderboard](https://www.asterdex.com/en/stage1/leaderboard)
.

**How is Au calculated?**

This depends on your CAKE investment and the market price of CAKE. For example, if you stake 100 CAKE when CAKE price is $2.5, and asCAKE Au multiplier is 1x, your mint earns 100 x 2.5 x 1 = 250 Au.

If there is no change in CAKE price, you will continue earning (100 x 2.5 x 1) Au per hour.

If CAKE price later drops to $2, you will earn (100 x 2 x 1) Au per hour.

**What is Smart Mint?**

Smart Mint is a mechanism to optimize CAKE to asCAKE rates so that you get the best conversion rate. Using Smart Mint, Aster will select between the conversion rate on AsterEarn or the conversion rate on the CAKE/asCAKE liquidity pool on PancakeSwap.

**Can I redeem my CAKE at any time?**

Yes, you can redeem asCAKE for CAKE on Aster directly with no waiting time.

**What are the risks involved?**

We have conducted thorough smart contract audits to ensure the security and reliability of the platform. In addition, we implement robust risk management protocols to protect your funds at all times.

**Are there any fees involved?**

There is no fee to mint or redeem asCAKE.

[PreviousMint asBNB](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asbnb)
[NextMint asUSDF](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asusdf)

Last updated 5 months ago

# Aster – Privacy Policy | Aster

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-privacy-policy#id-1.-introduction)

1\. Introduction

At Aster, we recognize the importance of your right to privacy and the protection of your information. As a provider of a decentralized cryptocurrency exchange platform, we are committed to best practices in privacy and transparency. We collect data only when it is strictly necessary to provide our Services.

Given the decentralized nature of our platform, we strive to process the minimum amount of data required. This Privacy Policy outlines our practices regarding the collection, use, and protection of your information when you use Aster, including accessing our website, decentralized applications, APIs, and related services (collectively, the “Services”).

By using our Services, you acknowledge that you have read, understood, and agree to the practices described in this Privacy Policy.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-privacy-policy#id-2.-data-controller-and-contact-information)

2\. Data Controller and Contact Information

Aster is the data controller responsible for processing your information. If you have any questions about this Privacy Policy or our data practices, please contact us at: [\[email protected\]](https://docs.asterdex.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-privacy-policy#id-3.-information-we-collect-and-how-we-use-it)

3\. Information We Collect and How We Use It

Following the principle of data minimization, we collect only the information necessary to provide and improve our Services. We collect and process only IP addresses for the following purposes:

*   Monitoring and preventing abuse of our Services
    
*   Ensuring network security
    
*   Facilitating traffic redirection in compliance with regulatory requirements based on the user’s country
    
*   Conducting statistical analysis to improve our Services
    

The processing of this information is based on our legitimate interests in maintaining the security, functionality, and regulatory compliance of our platform and protecting our users.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-privacy-policy#id-3.1-anonymized-data-usage)

3.1 Anonymized Data Usage

We use aggregated or anonymized data to enhance our Services. This includes:

*   Analyzing general usage patterns
    
*   Gathering feedback
    
*   Conducting research
    

All these activities are performed while ensuring individual users remain unidentified. For instance, we may generate usage reports that do not contain any information that could identify you.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-privacy-policy#id-4.-data-retention)

4\. Data Retention

We retain your IP address only for as long as necessary to provide our Services, fulfill the purposes stated in this Privacy Policy, and comply with legal requirements. We may also keep your data for an extended period if required by applicable laws or if it is needed for legal disputes or regulatory matters. We regularly review our retention practices to ensure that data is not kept longer than necessary.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-privacy-policy#id-5.-data-sharing-and-disclosure)

5\. Data Sharing and Disclosure

We may transfer your IP address to our service providers or third parties in connection with Aster’s operation of its business, as certain features on Aster rely on various third-party products and services (collectively “Third Party Services”), such as cloud storage, analytics and improvement of website-related services and features, and performance of maintenance services.

Third party services providers only have access to your IP address, to perform their functions, provide services and may not use it for other purposes. Furthermore, they must process the IP address in accordance with our contractual agreements and only as permitted by applicable data protections laws.

We may also share your IP address with the following persons or in the following circumstances:

Business transfers. As we continue to develop our business, we might sell or buy other businesses or services. In such transactions, your IP address generally is one of the transferred business assets but remains subject to the promises made in any pre-existing Privacy notice (unless, of course, you consent otherwise). Also, in the unlikely event that Aster or substantially all of its assets are acquired, your IP address will be one of the transferred assets.

Protection of Us and Others. We will share your IP address outside of Aster if we have a reasonable belief that access, use, preservation, or disclosure of the IP address is reasonably necessary to comply with any applicable law, regulation, legal process, or enforceable governmental request; to cooperate with law enforcement; to enforce or apply our Terms of Use and other agreements; or to protect the rights, property, or safety of Aster, our employees, our users, or others.

Our services may enable you to connect with various third-party services, decentralized applications, and other external platforms (referred to as “Third Party Platforms”).

These Third Party Platforms acts as independent data controller and processing of your IP address will be subject to their privacy notice and policy. This Privacy Notice does not cover the privacy practices of these Third Party Platforms, including any websites linked through our services. A link to a third-party site does not imply endorsement by us or our affiliates.

Your use of these Third Party Platforms and their handling of your IP address will be governed by their respective terms and privacy policies, and not by this Privacy Notice.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-privacy-policy#id-6.-international-transfers-of-personal-data)

6\. International Transfers of Personal Data

We may transfer your IP address to our Affiliates, third-party partners, and service providers based throughout the world. In cases where we intend to transfer your IP address to third countries or international organisations outside of your country of residence, Aster puts in place suitable technical, organizational and contractual safeguards (including Standard Contractual Clauses), to ensure that such transfer is carried out in compliance with applicable data protection rules.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-privacy-policy#id-7.-data-security)

7\. Data Security

We recognize that information security is a crucial component of data privacy. We are committed to making sure your IP address is protected in accordance with applicable laws and our data privacy policies.

Although no data transmission, including over the Internet or through any website, can be guaranteed to be entirely secure, we employ a range of commercially reasonable physical, technical, and procedural measures to protect your IP address from unauthorized access, use, disclosure, alteration, or destruction.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-privacy-policy#id-8.-your-privacy-rights)

8\. Your Privacy Rights

Subject to applicable law, as outlined below, you have a number of rights in relation to your privacy and the protection of your IP address. If you want to exercise any of your rights please contact us at privacy at \[insert the email address\].

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-privacy-policy#id-9.-children)

9\. Children

We are especially sensitive about children’s information. Our Services are not targeted towards children, and our users must be at least eighteen (18) years old to use our services. We don’t knowingly collect information from children under the age of 13. If you are a parent or legal guardian of a minor child, we will treat any information that you provide us while using Aster on behalf of your minor child as Personal Information as otherwise provided in this Privacy Policy. If you have questions concerning our information practices with respect to children, or if you learn that a child under the age of 13 has used Aster, created a user account, or provided us with personal information, please email us at privacy\[at\]asterdex.com or contact us through our online form.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-privacy-policy#id-10.-revisions-to-our-privacy-notice)

10\. Revisions to Our Privacy Notice

If you choose to use Aster’s products and services, your use and any dispute over privacy is subject to this Notice and our Terms of Use. If you have any concerns about privacy at Aster, please contact us with a complete description, and we will try to resolve it. You also have the right to contact your local Data Protection Authority.

Our business changes regularly, and our Privacy Notice may change also. We reserve the right to update and revise this Privacy Notice at any time.

We occasionally review this Privacy Notice to make sure it complies with applicable laws and conforms to changes in our business. If we do revise this Privacy Notice, we will update the “Last Updated” date at the beginning of this notice so that you can tell if it has changed since your last visit and will do our best to notify you.

Please review this Privacy Notice regularly to ensure that you are aware of its terms. Your continued use of Aster after an amendment to our Privacy Notice constitutes your acceptance to the revised or amended terms.

11\. Governing Law and Jurisdiction

Any dispute arising under these Terms shall be subject to the exclusive jurisdiction of the courts of Hong Kong. # Mint asBNB | Aster

**The Au Points Program will officially sunset and a snapshot of Au Points balances will be taken at 00:00:00 UTC on Friday, June 13, 2025. No further Au Points will be granted after this point.** [**Read more**](https://x.com/Aster_DEX/status/1932367398872760416)
**.** _**Last updated: June 10, 2025**_

* * *

**What's in this article**

[How to mint asBNB](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asbnb#how-to-mint-asbnb)

[How to withdraw asBNB](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asbnb#how-to-withdraw-asbnb)

[asBNB on Aster FAQs](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asbnb#asbnb-on-aster-faqs)

[asBNB Restaking FAQs](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asbnb#asbnb-restaking-faqs)

**Aster presents asBNB**, a liquid staking product that allows you to stake BNB or slisBNB to mint asBNB — offering flexible utility and strong yield potential.

**Key benefits**:

*   **Up to 30% APY** from BNB ecosystem rewards:
    
    *   **Binance Launchpool rewards** are reflected in the net asset value of asBNB.
        
    *   **Binance Hodler Airdrops** are distributed as asBNB and claimable on the asBNB page.
        
    *   **Megadrop rewards** are also distributed as asBNB and claimable on the same page.
        
    
*   **5× Au Points multiplier** for Aster airdrop eligibility.
    
*   **Lista DAO CAC S3**: If you earned Lista stardust before the event ended, check your eligibility on Lista DAO’s airdrop portal.
    

**Minting and withdrawal**:

*   You can mint asBNB with **BNB or slisBNB**. If you use BNB, it will be automatically converted to slisBNB.
    
*   **Withdrawals always return slisBNB**, even if you minted with BNB or cancel a pending mint.
    

**Security**:

Smart contracts are fully audited, with strong risk controls in place. See the asBNB FAQ for full details.

* * *

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asbnb#how-to-mint-asbnb)

How to mint asBNB


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1\. Once you have slisBNB or BNB, go to [Aster Earn](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn)
. Select asBNB, click \[Connect wallet\], and sign the message.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FnSGokX4J0t0lMnCqTXmQ%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-03-31%252016.04.03.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db3ca6f5e-0b2a-4d65-b545-e70f4cf1c452&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=40284677&sv=2)

1.  Enter the amount of slisBNB or BNB you want to mint and click \[Approve BNB\]. After that, confirm the transaction.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FFNdlGCDSVeqNHhGCgfxV%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-03-31%252016.05.13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D325043a6-3740-431c-874e-927fad28783f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e064227d&sv=2)

3\. Now you can click on \[Mint asBNB\].

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FmEtSAG0cRQNWohFzdTqf%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-10%252016.50.25.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc087ed3c-f91c-4ca3-b7cd-0486408a9a4b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5adf650c&sv=2)

1.  If a launchpool is active at the time of your request, it will be queued and processed only after the launchpool ends and the asBNB net asset value is updated. If there’s no active launchpool, your asBNB will be minted immediately.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F4mlFMWR5YjCuI9PMGrzw%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2024-12-26%252010.20.59.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94a2169b-59db-47ab-b4df-9855f34e86b8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cf2f5cd0&sv=2)

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asbnb#how-to-get-slisbnb)

How to get slisBNB


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You’ll need slisBNB to mint asBNB. If you don’t already have any, check out [this tutorial by Lista DAO](https://docs.bsc.lista.org/user-guide/liquid-staking-slisbnb)
 to learn how to obtain it.

If you previously deposited slisBNB on Aster, you can stake it directly on Aster Earn.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asbnb#method-1-stake-bnb-to-mint-slisbnb-on-lista-dao)

Method 1: Stake BNB to mint slisBNB on Lista DAO

**Step 1:**

*   Go to [Lista’s BNB liquid staking page](https://lista.org/liquid-staking/BNB)
     and connect your wallet.
    

**Step 2:**

*   Enter the amount of BNB you want to stake, click “Stake,” and confirm the transaction.
    
*   After the transaction is confirmed, slisBNB will be sent to your wallet.
    

**Step 3:**

*   To view your slisBNB balance, open your MetaMask wallet extension and select your account.
    
*   Scroll to the bottom of your Tokens tab and click “Import tokens”.
    

**Step 4:**

*   Paste the slisBNB contract address into the “Token Contract Address” field, then click “Add Custom Token”.
    
    *   slisBNB’s contract address: 0xB0b84D294e0C75A6abe60171b70edEb2EFd14A1B
        
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asbnb#method-2-swap-bnb-to-slisbnb-on-binance-wallet)

Method 2: Swap BNB to slisBNB on Binance Wallet

**Step 1: Open Binance Wallet**

*   Launch Binance Wallet on your device.
    
*   Ensure you are logged in and have BNB in your wallet.
    

**Step 2: Navigate to Swap**

*   After logging in, click the "Swap" tab at the bottom of the screen.
    

**Step 3: Select BNB to slisBNB**

*   Choose BNB from the dropdown as the token you want to swap.
    
*   Enter the amount of BNB you wish to swap. For example, 0.1 BNB as shown in the image.
    
*   In the “To” section, select slisBNB from the dropdown as the token to receive.
    

**Step 4: Review the swap details**

*   Check the details carefully to make sure everything is correct.
    

**Step 5: Execute the swap**

*   Click the Swap button to initiate the transaction.
    
*   Confirm any prompts that appear to complete the swap.
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asbnb#method-3-stake-slisbnb-from-aster-account)

Method 3: Stake slisBNB from Aster account

If you had previously deposited slisBNB on Aster, you can directly stake it.

**Step 1:**

*   Withdraw your slisBNB from Aster to your personal wallet.
    

**Step 2:**

*   Go to the [Aster Earn](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn)
     page. Select asBNB from the dropdown menu, then click \[Approve slisBNB\].
    

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asbnb#how-to-withdraw-asbnb)

How to withdraw asBNB


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Go to Aster Earn and select asBNB. Click \[Connect wallet\] and sign the message. Then select \[Withdraw\] and click \[Approve asBNB\].
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FZ8XgfSfVYJCrc9HZiTQJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D423dc6b6-176c-4799-a92c-bf1725c3e085&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e771b611&sv=2)

3\. Enter the amount of asBNB you want to withdraw, then click \[Withdraw\] to receive slisBNB. If there are no active Binance Launchpools, your withdrawal will be processed immediately. If a launchpool is active, your request will be queued and processed once the launchpool ends and the asBNB net asset value is updated. Launchpool rewards typically take 3–5 business days to be reflected in the asBNB net asset value.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F3ykUKLFr3BWLFMl0bYeG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0eac8e3c-befb-4611-b2e4-3e04cbea41e6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ba7fd9c1&sv=2)

Note: Regardless of whether you used BNB to mint asBNB, withdrawing asBNB will return slisBNB. If your mint request is still in the queue, canceling it will also return slisBNB.

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asbnb#asbnb-on-aster-faqs)

asBNB on Aster FAQs


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**What is asBNB?**

asBNB is a liquid staking token minted by staking slisBNB through Aster Earn.

Token contract address: 0x77734e70b6E88b4d82fE632a168EDf6e700912b6.

**How is asBNB APY generated?**

When you stake slisBNB on Aster Earn, it’s converted into clisBNB by Lista DAO and used to participate in Binance Launchpools. The rewards earned are converted to BNB by Lista DAO and returned to Aster, increasing the net asset value of asBNB. You can view the current asBNB APY [here](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn/astoken?token=slisBNB)
.

**How do I get the Au Multiplier?**

When you mint asBNB, you automatically earn Au points—your key to unlocking an allocation of the $AST airdrop. Connect your wallet to view your Au points [here](https://www.asterdex.com/en/stage1/leaderboard)
.

**How is Au calculated?**

Your Au rewards depend on how much BNB/slisBNB you stake and the current BNB price.

Example: Stake 0.5 BNB at $670 with a 5× multiplier → earn 1,675 Au/hour.

If BNB drops to $650 → earn 1,625 Au/hour.

**How do I get Lista stardust?**

Lista DAO's CAC S3 has ended. Check your reward eligibility on the [Lista DAO airdrop portal](https://lista.org/airdrop)
.

**Do I get Binance Hodler Airdrops?**

asBNB minters are eligible for Binance Hodler Airdrops, distributed as asBNB. Tokens will be sent to Lista DAO, converted to BNB, then to asBNB by Aster. Rewards will be claimable 3–5 business days after the airdrop ends.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FtKnECfT2f6gS2UeGGklt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0e1304d1-d1d7-4e0c-8074-a7bcf9f215d0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5738f162&sv=2)

**Do I get Megadrop rewards?**

asBNB minters are eligible for Megadrop rewards, distributed as asBNB. Like Hodler Airdrops, rewards will be converted to asBNB and claimable on the asBNB page within 3–5 business days after the Megadrop ends.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FlEEhD23KQchVQXpbaggA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da6cd2f71-8981-42f1-9a09-bfbcfbadbcec&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f07235a3&sv=2)

**What is the conversion ratio of slisBNB to asBNB, BNB to slisBNB, etc.?**

You can view the current conversion ratios on the [asBNB webpage](https://astherus.finance/en/earn/cedefi)
. Adjust the “From” and “To” assets to see different conversion rates.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FAHB5egJtdhkhA6sSUt8l%252FConversion.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daaac97d7-82ff-4869-b0e2-091028273d64&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3752f1c6&sv=2)

**Can I mint or withdraw asBNB at any time?**

You can withdraw asBNB instantly when no Binance Launchpool is active. If a Launchpool is active, your request will be queued and processed after the pool ends and the asBNB net asset value is updated—typically within 3–5 business days.

Note: You’ll always receive slisBNB when withdrawing, even if you originally minted asBNB with BNB. This also applies if you cancel a queued mint request.

**What are the risks involved?**

We’ve conducted comprehensive smart contract audits and implemented strict risk controls to keep your funds secure and the platform reliable.

**Are there any fees involved?**

Minting and withdrawing asBNB is completely fee-free, giving you full flexibility to manage your assets without extra costs.

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asbnb#asbnb-restaking-faqs)

asBNB Restaking FAQs


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**What is asBNB restaking?**

After minting asBNB on Aster, you can restake it on supported protocols such as Binomial or Kernel DAO.

**How do I claim Binance Launchpool rewards, Lista stardust, and Aster Au points?**

Binance Launchpool rewards are automatically reflected in asBNB’s net asset value. Lista DAO’s CAC S3 has ended—check your eligibility on their [airdrop portal](https://lista.org/airdrop)
. To view your Au points, head to Aster’s [airdrop dashboard](https://www.asterdex.com/en/stage1/team)
.

**How do I claim HOLDer airdrop rewards and Megadrop rewards when I restake asBNB on other protocols?**

HOLDer and Megadrop rewards will be converted to asBNB and claimed by the restaking protocol on your behalf before being distributed to you. Please refer to the respective projects for exact distribution timelines.

**Do I earn additional rewards for restaking asBNB?**

You may earn additional rewards from the restaking protocol—for example, restaking asBNB on Binomial or Kernel DAO can earn you their native points.

**Can I mint asBNB on Binomial or Kernel DAO?**

No, you can only mint asBNB on Aster.

[PreviousAster Earn](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn)
[NextMint asCAKE](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-ascake)

# Deposit APX to Aster Spot | Aster

If you have $APX tokens in a decentralized wallet, please follow the step-to-step tutorial to exchange $APX tokens to $ASTER tokens.

First Step: Connect your wallet on [Aster Spot trading page](https://www.asterdex.com/en/spot/CDLUSD1)
.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FAM4LcTZOLxMiZsvYvpaG%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-16%252012.30.44.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8c4feb66-c78b-43e2-8162-693843d6bb5d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b4e57b9b&sv=2)

Second Step: Click the button of deposit, deposit $APX tokens to your Aster Spot account. Click the button of Approve APX.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252Frnz4kdVOElcR2rA1YXzT%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-16%252012.33.53.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D21ebacec-1612-4b23-9642-8fd82d41679b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cf5e42f&sv=2)

Third Step: Input the APX amount and click the button of Deposit. Please confirm the deposit transaction in your wallet.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FATKrt6IbeXQdg8S8DmUu%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-16%252012.35.57.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9728d784-2753-4130-aee7-8bfd37bca584&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=102b903a&sv=2)

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252Fw4hTJcX7EzjlB3V1tr6h%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-16%252012.37.12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc20abb47-3e22-45a1-8efb-43c6daed112b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b9a71cd5&sv=2)

Last Step: Then you could see the APX tokens under Assets.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FAZaDGZ02E5grPuCbj7vR%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-16%252012.45.39.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5409234b-d7e0-4318-a579-05d3e1122575&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4d0353d0&sv=2)

When Aster exchange page launched, you could exchange APX tokens to ASTER tokens.

# Unstake the APX-BNB LP | Aster

If you hold the APX LP like APX-BNB LP, please follow the instructions to unlock the $APX tokens.

First step: Please go to the [APX LP staking page](https://www.apollox.finance/en/staking/lp)
 and connect your wallet.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FHIHQKd7B8EIOdQ1NRvaD%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-10%252013.08.31.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De4666812-4339-4e0d-b980-a32cc84de4c3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=679bfd4a&sv=2)

Second step: Please enter the amount of ALP, click the button of “Unstake” to unlock the LP.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F53mEDC5WRHNnvyeUqFlc%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-10%252013.06.50.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6f33714b-a180-45db-9a0b-8f848d88418c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7a21f5d8&sv=2)

Third step: Go to the PancakeSwap page and check your holding positions, click the button of “remove”, then you could receive the responded tokens in return.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FsLGzPP0w4S1XBkhBuBxd%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-10%252013.12.39.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D132d8a0e-e1b9-4e07-8517-9d74a2237355&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=66165a28&sv=2)

Last step: Since you remove the LP successfully and receive the $APX tokens, you could follow the above instructions to exchange your $APX tokens into $ASTER tokens.

[PreviousClaim ALP staking rewards](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdaster/apx-token-exchange/claim-alp-staking-rewards)
[NextClaim Binance Wallet Exclusive Reward](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdaster/claim-binance-wallet-exclusive-reward)

# Aster Media Kit | Aster

**Shorter description**

*   Decentralized perpetual contracts. Multi-chain, liquid, secure.
    

**Longer description**

*   Trade perpetuals on Aster, the top DEX with low fees, deep liquidity, multi-chain support, high leverage, and yield. Use Simple or Pro mode. Secure and non-custodial.
    

**Please follow these guidelines when using Aster brand assets:**

✨ All Aster brand assets are copyrighted materials. Please get approval from Aster before using them.

✨ Where possible, hyperlink our brand assets to Aster’s official website and social media channels like [X (Twitter)](https://x.com/Aster_DEX)
 and [Telegram](https://t.me/AsterDEX)
.

✨ Use our brand assets when announcing official partnerships.

**Avoid the following:**

❌ Don’t use Aster brand assets for promoting your own project — especially without our consent.

❌ Don’t repurpose any Aster brand elements (logos, visuals, colors, etc.) for other uses.

**Get in touch**

# Withdraw APX from APX perpetual account | Aster

If you have $APX tokens in the APX perpetual account, please follow the instructions to withdraw all $APX tokens to your wallet.

First step: Please go to the [APX V1 page](https://www.apollox.finance/en/futures/BTCUSDT)
 and connect your wallet as below:

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FArQNRnyvVk4OcKKJN8Pp%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-10%252012.56.40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D43062f77-b2f5-4de5-8e30-f3982d2ac5bb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d41e1fc7&sv=2)

Second step: Kindly please check the APX tokens under the “Assets”:

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F2BDrJSyk3HRfP7aPh1es%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-10%252013.02.28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D80f92181-54c5-49dd-ae09-edf117a70e93&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7ac56f96&sv=2)

Third step: Please click the button of withdraw to proceed the transaction on the blockchain.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F2dSlEf1zpULTLpnzeUUX%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-10%252013.04.17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd0ecf443-25ee-4939-b14a-2b02eaa39696&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7d4caf12&sv=2)

Last step: After you withdraw all $APX tokens from the APX perpetual account to your wallet, you could follow the above instructions to exchange your $APX tokens into $ASTER tokens.

[PreviousUnlock APX tokens in APX DAO](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdaster/apx-token-exchange/unlock-apx-tokens-in-apx-dao)

# Aster – Terms & Conditions | Aster

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-terms-and-conditions#id-1.-introduction-and-acceptance)

1\. Introduction and Acceptance

By accessing or using the Aster platform (“Aster”), you agree to be bound by these Terms and Conditions (“Terms”), and to comply with all applicable laws and regulations. If you do not agree with any of these Terms, do not access or use Aster.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-terms-and-conditions#id-2.-eligibility-and-wallet-access)

2\. Eligibility and Wallet Access

You must be at least 18 years old and have the legal capacity to enter into a binding agreement. Aster may restrict or deny access based on jurisdiction, regulatory requirements, or other internal policies.

Aster does not custody user assets. You are solely responsible for connecting your own compatible digital wallet and maintaining control of its credentials. Aster cannot recover lost wallet access.

You may be required to verify your identity or complete certain onboarding steps to access specific features or services on Aster.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-terms-and-conditions#id-3.-services-and-trading-rules)

3\. Services and Trading Rules

Aster provides access to decentralized financial protocols, including perpetual contracts and other trading products. You understand and accept that:

*   Trading may be subject to limitations, fees, slippage, and partial fills.
    
*   Orders may not execute immediately or at all, depending on market conditions.
    
*   You must not engage in abusive behavior, wash trading, market manipulation, front-running, or other prohibited conduct.
    

Aster reserves the right to limit or suspend access to services at its sole discretion.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-terms-and-conditions#id-4.-fees-and-payments)

4\. Fees and Payments

Aster may charge transaction or protocol fees, which will be disclosed at the time of execution. You are responsible for all applicable network fees (gas fees) and for complying with any tax obligations resulting from your activity.

Aster may modify fee structures or introduce new fees at any time, with or without notice.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-terms-and-conditions#id-5.-swaps-and-transfers)

5\. Swaps and Transfers

Once a transaction is submitted and confirmed on-chain, it cannot be reversed. You are solely responsible for verifying all transaction details, including wallet addresses, assets, and amounts, before confirming.

Transfers into and out of Aster-supported smart contracts may be subject to limits, delays, or security checks.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-terms-and-conditions#id-6.-intellectual-property-and-prohibited-uses)

6\. Intellectual Property and Prohibited Uses

All content, trademarks, code, and intellectual property related to Aster belong to the project or its licensors.

You may not:

*   Copy, modify, reverse engineer, or decompile any part of Aster.
    
*   Use Aster for illegal activity or to facilitate unauthorized access to other systems.
    
*   Interfere with or disrupt the platform or related services.
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-terms-and-conditions#id-7.-risk-disclosure)

7\. Risk Disclosure

By using Aster, you acknowledge and accept the significant risks associated with digital assets and decentralized protocols, including:

*   Price volatility and loss of value
    
*   Smart contract bugs or exploits
    
*   Regulatory uncertainty
    
*   Permanent loss of assets due to user error
    

You agree that Aster does not provide financial, investment, legal, or tax advice. All use is at your own risk.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-terms-and-conditions#id-8.-limitation-of-liability)

8\. Limitation of Liability

To the maximum extent permitted by law, Aster shall not be liable for any indirect, incidental, special, or consequential damages arising out of or in connection with your use of the platform.

This includes, without limitation, loss of profits, data, assets, or access.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-terms-and-conditions#id-9.-indemnification)

9\. Indemnification

You agree to indemnify and hold harmless Aster, its team members, contributors, partners, and affiliates from and against any claims, damages, liabilities, and expenses (including legal fees) arising from:

*   Your use or misuse of Aster
    
*   Your violation of these Terms
    
*   Your violation of any applicable law or rights of any third party
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-terms-and-conditions#id-10.-modifications)

10\. Modifications

Aster may update or modify the platform or these Terms at any time. Updates may be communicated via the platform or associated channels. Continued use of Aster after any changes constitutes acceptance of the new Terms.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-terms-and-conditions#id-11.-termination-and-suspension)

11\. Termination and Suspension

Aster may suspend or terminate your access to the platform at any time, with or without cause or notice. You may stop using Aster at any time.

Provisions that, by their nature, should survive termination (such as disclaimers and limitations of liability) will continue to apply.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-terms-and-conditions#id-12.-governing-law-and-dispute-resolution)

12\. Governing Law and Dispute Resolution

These Terms shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of Hong Kong, without regard to its conflict of law principles.

You agree to resolve any dispute arising out of these Terms on an individual basis. You waive the right to participate in class actions or jury trials.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-terms-and-conditions#id-13.-force-majeure)

13\. Force Majeure

Aster shall not be held liable for any delay or failure in performance resulting from events beyond its reasonable control, including but not limited to natural disasters, internet outages, regulatory actions, or third-party service interruptions.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-terms-and-conditions#id-14.-assignment)

14\. Assignment

You may not assign or transfer your rights or obligations under these Terms without Aster’s prior written consent. Aster may assign these Terms at its discretion.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/about-us/aster-terms-and-conditions#id-15.-entire-agreement)

15\. Entire Agreement

These Terms constitute the entire agreement between you and Aster regarding use of the platform and supersede any prior or contemporaneous communications.

###

16\. Contact

If you have any questions about these Terms, please contact us at: [\[email protected\]](https://docs.asterdex.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)

# How to transfer liquidity to new pool | Aster

**Using the asUSDF May 2025 and asUSDF Nov 2025 pools as an example:**

1.  Head to the [asUSDF May 2025 pool webpage](https://app.pendle.finance/trade/pools/0x9e515a7115c86d7314159dbdab41e555d5330dfe/zap/in?chain=bnbchain)
     and connect your wallet.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252Fyvs4UboG5RYs2uR5ruOA%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-20%2520at%252011.16.39%25E2%2580%25AFAM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D18231b86-cdb4-4593-b48c-615f0bff343c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=68b810ce&sv=2)

1.  Click \[Transfer Liquidity\], select all existing positions, tick \[Claim All Pool Rewards\] and \[Keep YT Mode\]. In the \[Target Pool\], enter 0x2ac20c37b5577e04bb68e239a45f4fb3b4edb184.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FK9ZxzL7OcuTWnN5PFzOp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb7ac977-f06c-4828-8fc1-fdb2188cd48e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fabfd5a5&sv=2)

1.  0x2ac20c37b5577e04bb68e239a45f4fb3b4edb184 is the pool address of the new asUSDF Nov 2025 pool. You will be asked to select a new market to rollover. Select \[LP\].
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252Ff9UiL7S2eHEOQJxm59zO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6922f5b8-0792-4fd5-b764-a9f504a897f8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=40b61432&sv=2)

1.  Then, click \[Approve Tokens\]. After approving, click \[Roll Over\] to transfer your liquidity.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FIqGO6u3P1cBYUBf7RqKU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8bce694f-7506-42c9-8525-a22022c9b9f0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c3583852&sv=2)

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FjXtKavMzlolPNC5eXAyr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D59c79c43-5cef-43e7-a587-9b029f617606&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e1d9be44&sv=2)

Once completed, you should see your liquidity in the new asUSDF pool.

# Tutorials | Aster

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/tutorials#how-to-mint-usdf)

How to mint USDF?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1\. Go to the \[[USDF](https://www.asterdex.com/en/usdf)\
\] tab on the Aster website. Click \[Connect wallet\] and sign the message.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXc36dQgR8R_3wVqT1U5zYBXlmyTbGUKEl5NF5xHebgaOX4nVU-yJpTDOafFRGnAVN41lhBd2kzvtWBJRNOQq2I2l4zgx8VQ5s82HzZFDYhhYWRqzOK0k8gjYYJv362DQ85DaIElkg%3Fkey%3DYBw161GYKNkAByDTZqA_i60J&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=789a5fbc&sv=2)

2\. Input a USDT value to get the estimated amount of USDF you would receive.

3\. Click \[Smart Mint USDF\] and confirm. Once confirmed, you have minted USDF successfully.

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/tutorials#how-to-redeem-usdf)

How to redeem USDF?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1\. Go to the \[[USDF](https://www.asterdex.com/en/usdf)\
\] tab on the Aster website. Click \[Connect Wallet\] and sign the message. Click \[Redeem\] and \[Approve USDF\].

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcfxciqfoioI2qaoF9DaL1cl0w2QsXfMsibtehvcl5yn0boVR8rnlcJCEn7PALDK55WLPhVnudIPe6lcBm6mKl-mv09vbxza1EM_dSGa-XxwpD_NODD11Vcm-6izlF0HvYk8r-9OA%3Fkey%3DYBw161GYKNkAByDTZqA_i60J&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4c0400bf&sv=2)

2\. Input a USDF value to get the estimated amount of USDT you would receive. You can choose to redeem USDF on Aster, or swap USDF for USDT on PancakeSwap.

3\. If you redeem USDF on Aster, your request will be processed and will appear under the Claim section. For most redemptions, it takes 1 to 2 days to redeem USDF for USDT. For large amounts, it may take up to 7 days. During the waiting period, you will not earn Au points. After the waiting period, remember to click \[Claim\] to claim your USDT tokens.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfIQnZULTIel0-ufIndXHaRZbP3PhPSF3Rnv6n2PgOY0kx74MR1S-VD4OeYwxV06tRSw-XzjeGJzTeYvGcIi9-epuvGTHCKdeJ6BH-Zm0_n1zOwDS_56qKWOLBuh1Yw9pt9E6VBfg%3Fkey%3DYBw161GYKNkAByDTZqA_i60J&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7377d631&sv=2)

4\. Alternatively, you can click \[Swap\]. You will be redirected to the PancakeSwap page with the quoted USDT amount.

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/tutorials#how-to-mint-asusdf)

How to mint asUSDF:


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1\. Go to [Aster Earn](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn)
. Click \[Connect wallet\] and sign the message.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcKmKp_HZr8Ufb9-JX-y0GwI_bSgOsnrlmt8JEsFbLFa8d_IylXnRqq6llwo0MMw9fl8732SPH_2KaXMzFUTnc6TOEFHB9jgwIYkmxnOo6P3R-1wZECGcNS4cyHES7Iy6FdUD5Mng%3Fkey%3DYBw161GYKNkAByDTZqA_i60J&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1bb65a89&sv=2)

2\. Select USDF from the dropdown menu. Click \[Approve USDF\].

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfQtFAX0MEh6Gookbutas1VQbUh356AnJJssg9fDfWIVf1eQIRZXE4tRElAGCrA9XzFtBR1FjqYCUMz1AKuFjybITK0KtCM7KVkTIgoyRy4c47Bu79xIjrqrJjz874nHqig8uKd7g%3Fkey%3DYBw161GYKNkAByDTZqA_i60J&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6e8aa1ab&sv=2)

3\. Enter your desired USDF value. Click \[Mint asUSDF\]. Then click the confirm button to proceed.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXez3ot_Wk8tklVGMpLDV8qkbLv6cIfLMYMmDjyHOww1NP29vM6nh_Jgi7kLvsP60Ewcn48ulCs2D-cE0SqxglZFODhc1LuMIsqIxfYesjAa5yL5kyiQCyZAe_erAOZEFnRmMQP_5Q%3Fkey%3DYBw161GYKNkAByDTZqA_i60J&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3e2406f4&sv=2)

4\. Once confirmed, you have minted asUSDF successfully.

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/tutorials#how-to-withdraw-asusdf)

How to withdraw asUSDF:


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1\. Go to [Aster Earn](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn)
. Click \[Connect wallet\] and sign the message.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdi7KYKK7K5UJWjXZixm6RH-M9QoUtNPr60_JyBmlq7EtnoiC2M9BdcDm-7xALiFtjlvJUvGHe0DutiYtEMUrknYlB3x18-Np-4hsky8codRqkxBlLz099USuceaMxi_sysPn1h%3Fkey%3DYBw161GYKNkAByDTZqA_i60J&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3ea8de73&sv=2)

2\. Select asUSDF from the dropdown menu. Select \[Withdraw\]. Enter your desired withdrawal value and click \[Request withdraw\].

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXc2FnDpi6FScsPEqYoZ89U1Gr_WQq-cS88KzssO0gjd_NFZDNBCjxgA5RHH0upTpSQ6aapwhH_lZ7oU4ySIw5pqiHz8Mci-kpBk69SvXjnPUCZ2J0DbN8Mn66oUMRY7p9aWiNpwag%3Fkey%3DYBw161GYKNkAByDTZqA_i60J&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4e7ad888&sv=2)

3\. Once confirmed, your request to withdraw asUSDF is in the queue. Withdrawals of asUSDF to USDF take around T+1 hour (2 hours). You can see the request status in \[Claim\]. Please make sure that BNB Chain is selected as the network so that you can view the claim status. Please also note that you will not continue earning Au points and yield during the waiting period.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXedkB2XYSJ31d_VapR4xunLa9AQ4_PPWvN8MdvgYzAnv0MaqXJq-cS_VuXaDP7U4DIYx9TMO_rMI32s3z0aTAFKypMVhCISOYdFJMWi9HLcYgcvtr8NmntuKMEnSjZUyY1-ugSghg%3Fkey%3DYBw161GYKNkAByDTZqA_i60J&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=88eca724&sv=2)

Remember to claim your USDF by clicking \[Claim\]. Once claimed, the status will reflect as Claimed.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXd76fqE9Rf3KGRamWr2pHPVWCxzY2ABrpHm96bzXsyyJUcoK8X0rGBZgY4IUjDlOqjIMMug_MA0V6GwQ_w89tFfaEdQwLop_RBj8HNm4Mdrek4nZ50KpXFnUwi3YarywDIR8QWXAA%3Fkey%3DYBw161GYKNkAByDTZqA_i60J&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=31342a4f&sv=2)

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/usdf-stablecoin/tutorials#how-to-mint-usdf-lp-or-asusdf-lp)

How to mint USDF LP or asUSDF LP


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# How to calculate Au points for LP and YT | Aster

**The Au Points Program will officially sunset and a snapshot of Au Points balances will be taken at 00:00:00 UTC on Friday, June 13, 2025. No further Au Points will be granted after this point.** [**Read more**](https://x.com/Aster_DEX/status/1932367398872760416)
**.** _**Last updated: June 10, 2025**_

* * *

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/how-to-calculate-au-points-for-lp-and-yt#au-multipliers-for-lp-and-yt)

Au Multipliers for LP & YT


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   asUSDF: 25x Au
    
*   asBNB: 10x Au
    
*   USDF: 35x Au
    

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/how-to-calculate-au-points-for-lp-and-yt#contracts)

Contracts


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   SY-asUSDF: 0x9E515a7115C86d7314159DbdAb41E555d5330Dfe
    
*   YT-asUSDF: 0x5e4Ea9538E8ae4C22f3897e85C7AB51672Bb3a62
    
*   SY-asBNB: 0xe954c3b53b2cd8b9056737193780f0a541815bb2
    
*   YT-asBNB: 0x89c625c475f33a78a8c60250137a3d51aa12b357
    
*   SY-USDF: 0x0f47aee96fae2558b0081c8d2dffbb8512397e23
    
*   YT-USDF: 0x5e9d14e48c7a35c77caf83bd15ae2f73d411e523
    

* * *

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/how-to-calculate-au-points-for-lp-and-yt#how-to-calculate-au-points-for-lp)

How to calculate Au points for LP?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/how-to-calculate-au-points-for-lp-and-yt#using-lp-asusdf-as-an-example)

Using LP-asUSDF as an example:

Formula: **Au multiplier\*(SY held in LP\*User LP/Total LP)**

*   **Au multiplier** refers to the Au points for that asset. For LP-asUSDF, it is 25x.
    
*   **SY held in LP\*User LP/Total LP** refers to the SY attributable to you in the pool
    

**Scenario using wallet 0xd6…995b:**

1\. First, query the activeBalance and the pool’s totalActiveSupply.

Go to the SY-asUSDF contract > Read Contract > Query the wallet address in [2\. activeBalance](https://bscscan.com/address/0x9e515a7115c86d7314159dbdab41e555d5330dfe#readContract#F2)
 and [19\. totalActiveSupply](https://bscscan.com/address/0x9e515a7115c86d7314159dbdab41e555d5330dfe#readContract#F19)
. Use [https://bscscan.com/unitconverter](https://bscscan.com/unitconverter)
 if you need help converting units.

For the wallet 0xd6…995b, the activeBalance is 209.11 and the totalActiveSupply is 2,488,522.

Hence, this user’s percentage proportion of the LP pool = (209.11/2,488,522)\*100 = 0.0084%.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeCZdkZ7RK-0jIKRuTXSc2vnfMw4hvYOK5BDZ7k2igstig2rsedSMG5ut95QtSBgvB2G0EqO7kj5S35J4DjCov2PfyYUQg_RmXBqADbDfSO4FRyfQQsfThtj-ZpqUuJYeD8P6OeAA%3Fkey%3DJ3kbZi7pcl1auuw3TlOIrsy5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c58801d&sv=2)

Wallet 0xd6…995b's activeBalance at time of query

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FDVSthfuoWRQK17l2cw9V%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De714d70f-b570-4f11-9a9f-c1ca78ae65f2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=89988917&sv=2)

Wallet 0xd6…995b's totalActiveSupply at time of query

2\. Next, derive the SY attributable to the wallet. Go to the [SY-asUSDF contract](https://bscscan.com/address/0x9e515a7115c86d7314159dbdab41e555d5330dfe)
 and look at the total SY sitting in the LP contract.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdwq78c8NWRC4U3xDCD4yftuWG66mqZm_LJ4Ws1zjj1jRR4i_NBJnxwlvee8cdT5mkPk0evgCmTC5MonzmrW9cvUlH6rR_6rmC_q7WUoxn3byNE-1hM8il-gVr8XOJDpRU2b0ooWQ%3Fkey%3DJ3kbZi7pcl1auuw3TlOIrsy5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8a63efac&sv=2)

Total SY in the LP contract at time of query

The total SY in the LP-asUSDF contract is 4,052,238. Thus, for the wallet 0xd6…995b, the SY attributable to the user is 4,052,238\*0.0084% = 340.38 SY.

Putting it all together, this user earns 25\*340.38 = 8,509 Au points/hour.

* * *

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/how-to-calculate-au-points-for-lp-and-yt#how-to-calculate-au-points-for-yt)

How to calculate Au points for YT?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/how-to-calculate-au-points-for-lp-and-yt#using-yt-asusdf-as-an-example)

Using YT-asUSDF as an example:

Formula = **Au multiplier\*(SY\*YT/Total YT)**

*   **Au multiplier** refers to the Au points for that asset. For LP-asUSDF, it is 25x.
    
*   **SY\*YT/Total YT** refers to your proportion of SY (which earns you Au points)
    

**Scenario using wallet 0xd6…995b:**

1\. First, get the [total SY amount sitting in the YT-asUSDF contract](https://bscscan.com/address/0x5e4ea9538e8ae4c22f3897e85c7ab51672bb3a62)
. In the example below, it is 15,199,750.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfkYU-2_nRcs-zfb5UW3JPUGGSnMbHKng19Qrf-dkxG_jQHuavH4EdVEa6P9zNZoKmIxAgzvQjxRpSH0Ioh3rwOcN6yWbAx2FgmAKQ-KR7kwLFeuWr2D_iJuZhWvEsauYBBjBLACw%3Fkey%3DJ3kbZi7pcl1auuw3TlOIrsy5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a02181bd&sv=2)

Total SY in the YT-asUSDF contract at time of query

Then, look at how many YT-asUSDF the wallet 0xd6…995b has. After checking token holdings, this user has 4,514 YT-asUSDF.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfdYbxZSlzDe0bv740S83HJXoFEf0XxGb1M-RvMy3qoXLaqgbrqC97G3H5DoF0X6lyjqYr1sJA7YH7zpgt3LUn2cmiO3B71kDoZ2d7FkAQfG1c1xmHDvrfIWI_Z5K4tVpZrYTD8%3Fkey%3DJ3kbZi7pcl1auuw3TlOIrsy5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=82bacaf9&sv=2)

Wallet 0xd6…995b YT-asUSDF holding at time of query

Thus, the user wallet 0xd6…995b’s percentage proportion of YT is (4,514/15,199,750)\*100 = 0.03%

2\. Next, calculate the user’s proportion of SY.

It is 0.03%\*15,199,750 = 4,559 SY. However, remember that there is a 3% fee. Hence, the user’s proportion of SY is 4,559\*97% = 4,422 SY.

Putting it all together, this user earns 25\*4,422 = 110,550 Au points/hour

[PreviousUSDF on Pendle](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/usdf-on-pendle)
[NextHow to transfer liquidity to new pool](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/how-to-transfer-liquidity-to-new-pool)

Last updated 5 months ago
