# APX Token Exchange | Aster

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FjpcZQVW4uI9RpwoCayRO%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-09-05%252015.32.03.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29b582a7-a7db-4e37-b68f-3c7554cd3086&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e602fd8a&sv=2)

With the [reveal of $ASTER token](https://medium.com/asterdex/all-need-to-know-about-aster-airdrop-24b2e914b025)
 by Aster, APX holders will soon be able to upgrade their $APX tokens to $ASTER. This article explains everything you need to know before exchanging your APX holdings for $ASTER.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdaster/apx-token-exchange#apx-to-aster-exchange-info)

APX to ASTER Exchange Info

APX Token Exchange page will be live on September 17 2025. All exact timestamps for time sensitive activities will be revealed closer during the day - please watch out for announcements from [Aster’s X account](https://x.com/Aster_DEX)
.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdaster/apx-token-exchange#apx-token-holders)

APX token holders:

You can immediately exchange APX spot tokens for $ASTER. The exchange ratio decreases over time on a first-come, first-served basis. See the exchange ratios below across five time periods.

**Rewards from APX DAO will end on September 11.**

**APX DAO stakers:**

You can unlock your veNFT and retrieve all your $APX tokens without penalties on September 16, before exchanging APX spot tokens for $ASTER based on the same exchange ratios below.

**APX to ASTER Exchange Ratio:**

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FXHkWmKwd45suUSf28J8m%252FTGE_APX%2520to%2520ASTER_table.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2b87d5e9-30a4-4ab3-b921-d38cd6829860&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d85edc5b&sv=2)

_**Tip:**_ _There are no restrictions on the amount you can swap during each cycle._

**APX to ASTER Exchange Process**

**APX token holders:**

1.  Once APX Token Upgrade page is live, visit the page and connect your wallet
    
2.  Deposit $APX to your Aster spot account
    
3.  Enter the amount of $APX you wish to exchange, and complete the exchange to receive your $ASTER tokens instantly in your Aster spot account
    
4.  After that, you can trade the $ASTER tokens on the Spot trading page when trading opens or withdraw the $ASTER tokens to your crypto wallet when withdrawals are live
    

**APX DAO stakers:**

1.  Access the [APX DAO page](https://www.apollox.finance/en/governance)
     to unlock your current veNFT and retrieve all your $APX tokens without penalties
    
2.  Once unlocked, proceed to the Aster exchange page to swap for $ASTER tokens based on the steps shared above for APX token holders.
    

💡 Tip: Please claim all your rewards before unlocking the current veNFT on APX DAO.

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/usdaster/apx-token-exchange#faqs)

FAQs

**How do I exchange $APX for $ASTER tokens?**

*   Go to the Aster exchange page, connect your wallet, and deposit your $APX tokens into your spot account. Enter the amount you want to convert, then confirm the exchange. Your $ASTER tokens will be added instantly to your Spot account.
    

**How do I exchange $APX from APX DAO for $ASTER tokens?**

*   On the [APX DAO page](https://www.apollox.finance/en/governance)
    , use the immediate unlock feature to retrieve your staked $APX. After unlocking, return to the Aster exchange page to complete the swap. Please note that the exchange rate decreases over time.
    

**How do I check the $ASTER token balance after the exchange?**

*   You will see your $ASTER token balance in the Aster spot account directly after the exchange. You may trade $ASTER tokens on the spot market directly or withdraw $ASTER to another wallet.
    
*   Your $ASTER balance will appear directly in your Spot account after the exchange. You can trade $ASTER on the spot market or withdraw it to another wallet.
    

**When can I unlock the veNFT on the APX DAO page?**

*   The instant unlock feature with no penalties will be available on September 16.
    

**When can I deposit $APX tokens to my Aster Spot account?**

*   Aster will enable $APX token deposits on September 16. Please follow [our Twitter](https://x.com/Aster_DEX)
     for the exact timestamps for the instant veNFT unlock and $APX deposit functions on Aster.
    

_**Tip:**_ _Exchange early to get the best rate and maximize your $ASTER tokens._

More detailed tutorials will come soon.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252Fq7n6IzuaOu93zZ80URa5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D35b335ea-d4ce-4293-9644-f31b3ba26868&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=86c6207b&sv=2)

[**Human vs AI: The Ultimate Trading Battle**](https://www.asterdex.com/en/campaigns/human-vs-ai)

**$200,000 Prize pool. 100 funded traders. Zero downside. Team Human vs AI.**

For decades, humans dominated trading. Intuition. Experience. The ability to read what data fails to capture.

Then came the AI models. GPT-5. Gemini. Deepseek. Grok and more. Running 24/7, processing millions of signals in seconds, executing without fear.

Now it’s time to let **Team Human** and **Team AI** settle this on-chain.

* * *

**The Most Asymmetric Bet in Crypto**

Aster is funding **up to 100 human traders** with **10,000 USDT each** to fight the world’s leading AI models in a live, real-size Perpetual competition.

If you are selected:

*   You keep every dollar of profit
    
*   Aster absorbs every dollar of loss
    

On top of that, you’re not just trading for yourself. You’re playing for **Team Human.**

*   Total prize pool: $200,000
    
*   $100,000 for the top Human PnL champion
    
    *   Prize goes unclaimed if AI takes #1.
        
    
*   Human team base prize pool: $50,000.
    
    *   If humans beat AI, the prize pool DOUBLES to $100,000.
        
    *   Every profitable human trader shares the prize pool.
        
    

Apply now to represent Team Human: [Register Now](https://forms.gle/yrKzPgMHZ8ynMkVF6)

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/trading-campaign/human-vs-ai-battle-for-the-futures-usd200-000-reward-pool#usd200-000-prize-pool-overview)

$200,000 Prize Pool Overview

1.  **Individual Prize**
    
    *   Top PnL Champion: $100,000
        
    *   The $100,000 prize is awarded only if the top PnL trader is Human.
        
    *   If an AI trader takes the #1 PnL spot, this individual prize is not awarded.
        
    
2.  **Human Team Prizes**
    
    *   Base Prize: $50,000
        
    *   If **Team Human** beats **Team AI**, the Human Team prize pool **doubles to $100,000**.
        
    *   Human team rewards are distributed **proportionally based on each trader’s positive PnL** (human champion excluded).
        
    *   **Reward for each eligible Human trader** = (Individual Positive PnL ÷ Total Positive PnL of all eligible Human team members) × Human Team Prize Pool.
        
    
    Notes:
    
    1.  PNL calculation: PNL = Total balance (including unrealized PNL + wallet balance) - Initial Trading Funds
        
    2.  Team ROI = Sum of all team members’ PNL / Total Initial Trading Funds of all team members
        
    3.  Only traders with positive PNL (PNL > 0) are eligible to share the team rewards. Rewards are distributed strictly according to each trader’s share of total **positive** Human team PNL.
        
    4.  **Rewards are paid in USDF**, Aster’s yield-bearing stablecoin.

*   After the event ends, Aster will conduct a full audit of all participant accounts to verify trading behavior, rule compliance, and data accuracy. The official final rankings will be announced separately once the review is complete.
    
*   After the audit, Aster will distribute the rewards (Final balance - the initial 10,000 USDT + the prize amount) to the participant’s personal Aster Spot account provided during registration.
    
*   The ‘Final balance’ will be determined based on the snapshot taken at the end of the competition. Any profits generated from trades executed after the competition ends will not be counted, and any remaining USDT will be reclaimed by Aster.

# asUSDF on Pendle | Aster

**Note:**

*   **Those who split asUSDF into PT and YT without further activity on Pendle are exploiting the Au points reward system. Aster prioritizes real activity like providing liquidity or trading PT and YT on Pendle. To protect the interests of genuine DeFi holders and encourage healthy activity, exploiters may lose all Au points.**
    
*   **The Au Points Program will officially sunset and a snapshot of Au Points balances will be taken at 00:00:00 UTC on Friday, June 13, 2025. No further Au Points will be granted after this point.** [**Read more**](https://x.com/Aster_DEX/status/1932367398872760416)
    **.** _**Last updated: June 10, 2025**_
    

* * *

asUSDF is the innovative yield-bearing token of stablecoin USDF. On Aster, you will stake USDF to mint asUSDF. The delta neutral positions that back USDF also generate asUSDF yields (neutral arbitrage APY and funding rates reflected in asUSDF’s net asset value). You also earn 10x Au points when you mint asUSDF on Aster. Read more about asUSDF and USDF:

[Mint asUSDF](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/mint-asusdf)

* * *

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/asusdf-on-pendle#basic-concepts)

Basic concepts


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfe1WOOqTr9fmA9qX4_ZxxBoEafXn_8ffRVuAuWoPI32JHcAHoO3jgWcPuxlvL0NEJSTt9wciLnFzlQ7YcinQsCyM_fsTSVLezux8S6e33h3H0FcYLVgDcD8c_XH1692ewqPm1l_Q%3Fkey%3DJ3kbZi7pcl1auuw3TlOIrsy5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7b273caf&sv=2)

SY:

*   A token standard on Pendle for wrapping yield-bearing tokens. For example, when you deposit asUSDF, asUSDF is automatically wrapped into SY-asUSDF. This happens on the backend, so you don’t have to deal with conversion between SY and asUSDF.
    
*   SY is then split into PT and YT.
    

PT:

*   Represents the principal of the underlying yield-bearing token. For example, PT-asUSDF represents the principal of asUSDF (i.e. does not include asUSDF yield or Au points)
    

YT:

*   Represents all the yield of the asset. For example, YT-asUSDF represents the yield and Au points you can get from asUSDF.
    

LP:

*   The LP token you get after adding liquidity. For example, you get LP-asUSDF after adding asUSDF liquidity.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/asusdf-on-pendle#there-are-a-few-ways-to-engage-with-asusdf-on-pendle)

There are a few ways to engage with asUSDF on Pendle.

* * *

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/asusdf-on-pendle#provide-liquidity)

Provide liquidity


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you provide asUSDF liquidity, you get LP-asUSDF. LP-asUSDF is perfect for those who want to earn both yield and Au points.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F1z51GAEQpXGstIFIi5CC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4111e4e6-2ddd-4716-aafe-b6ab291cfb91&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=302d093e&sv=2)

Adding asUSDF liquidity

LP yield includes 25x Au points, Underlying Yield, PT fixed yield, $PENDLE incentives, and Pendle swap fees. Note: Pendle states Underlying Yield from USDF because USDF is the underlying stablecoin of yield-bearing token asUSDF.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcfFSR4v5q9eIWdxF4s4TCnNhmOqhxeJDunkBas_AXl0x93LfCXzulGxNY0m1QzRqr2ANDRV4L_-q4oO4sefatSKn5bXRychNYp0jRcR9d-k2oCxDSQREhrwXuE2PMXcCP5mGoztQ%3Fkey%3DJ3kbZi7pcl1auuw3TlOIrsy5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6a21995d&sv=2)

LP-asUSDF Yield

* * *

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/asusdf-on-pendle#pt-asusdf)

PT-asUSDF


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PT-asUSDF represents the principal portion of asUSDF. Thus, 1 PT-asUSDF is equivalent to the value of 1 asUSDF excluding asUSDF yields and Au points.

If you're bullish on asUSDF, PT-asUSDF lets you buy in at a fixed rate discount as it is traded at a discount to asUSDF.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfWP7ArNfWRthwNgA7uljBgrdUJUHrM1JsvzXFXbTXNzJFNKwno9tykQ-0e7sV3CB7cwnNziVOu7eA5ccc17gI2g51OsnH0J5gv56uQoWwlBMUWk1KcQqgRrLOdD3DG4cQKAUIr%3Fkey%3DJ3kbZi7pcl1auuw3TlOIrsy5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b315ac3&sv=2)

Buying PT-asUSDF

*   **Fixed APY**: The value of PT-asUSDF will gradually increase and become equal to the value of the asUSDF at maturity. This process creates a fixed guaranteed return ("fixed APY"). For example, let's say PT-asUSDF offers a fixed APY of 18.39% with maturity on 29 May 2025. This means that PT-asUSDF holders get a guaranteed return of 18.39% APY if held till maturity. You DO NOT earn asUSDF underlying yield or Au points.
    
*   **What you can do**: Hold till maturity OR trade PT-asUSDF on Pendle anytime.
    
*   Note: Pendle states that 1 PT-asUSDF is equal to 1 USDF deposited in Aster. This is a nod to USDF as the underlying stablecoin of yield-bearing token asUSDF. At maturity, you can redeem PT-asUSDF for asUSDF at a 1:1 ratio.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcxWKx37YLjbx_VGhEsUF1xZpENNTcOztAwhJaG28oatYgwL0fapayTsRpSqu_GsPMpSckm6-1zqDQlvFS9vwuaLJFRxfQKT3SA7rYrHioZ8qvh7eV6DC_i1iJ9mH262etIjlmFAA%3Fkey%3DJ3kbZi7pcl1auuw3TlOIrsy5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2d7819a8&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/asusdf-on-pendle#yt-asusdf)

YT-asUSDF


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

YT-asUSDF represents the yield portion of the underlying asset asUSDF. Thus, 1 YT-asUSDF represents the yield and Au points you can earn from 1 asUSDF.

If you are a yield-maxi, YT-asUSDF helps to leverage your yield exposure. Buying YT-asUSDF means that you are 'longing the yield' of asUSDF.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcVCFbHD_Qz8S3hoGI7upzsykLNn26OkmsSemXdyaQYNFJfplWiJHItZq7cxOyRTgsdU6caKgxbtns7mGwS5c-iyEZDwNSnmkQqeEyb_5UtNnpFTGb5-TpS_n0xSEBAWDw2kpj4%3Fkey%3DJ3kbZi7pcl1auuw3TlOIrsy5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fe5d3043&sv=2)

Buying YT-asUSDF

*   **YT yield**: YT-asUSDF lets you earn asUSDF yield and 25x Au points till maturity. asUSDF yield is reflected in NAV. Au points accumulate hourly and you can check Au points on the [Aster Airdrop dashboard](https://www.asterdex.com/en/stage1/team)
    . The value of YT-asUSDF will naturally trend towards $0 as there is less remaining yield the closer we get to maturity. Holders profit when the total yield collected up to that point ends up being higher than their cost of buying YT-asUSDF.
    
*   **What you can do**: Hold till maturity or trade YT-asUSDF on Pendle anytime.
    

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeQ-apJ_YoUTDZGiufwNisdUacQO6HIMyX0GlPE4G6skspDfDc_k6KqlTBuEZUlzhoSu1zMO-kmVF7DzBTkLOCYTU7_HCQh9u-V0pF-oZmbDJ-8iKjN9qz45G2hyiwa6t0lfKQvOw%3Fkey%3DJ3kbZi7pcl1auuw3TlOIrsy5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=896a662&sv=2)

[PreviousPendle](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle)
[NextasBNB on Pendle](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/aster-earn/ecosystem/pendle/asbnb-on-pendle)

# Market Maker Program | Aster

Overview

To strengthen liquidity and reward market makers, Aster is introducing MM Preferential Fees and a monthly MM Reward Pool. Each month, 300,000 USDT worth of $ASTER will be distributed to qualifying market makers based on their effective maker volume.

1\. Program Objective

*   Incentivize Liquidity: Strengthen liquidity across supported pairs on Aster Pro Mode by rewarding active and effective market makers.
    
*   Aligning Long-Term Value Creation: Distribute Aster token rewards as part of a sustainable and performance-based program, aligned with on-chain activity and trading contributions.
    
*   Support Fair Market Structure: Encourage tight spreads, deep books, and active quoting through quantifiable, rule-based incentives.
    

2\. MM Preferential Fees

Tier

Criteria (Rolling 14 days)

Taker Fee (bps)

Maker Fee Rebate (bps)

MM 1

\>= $500M or Maker Vol >= 1.5%

2.7

\-0.25

MM 2

\>= $1B or Maker Vol >= 3%

2.3

\-0.50

For market maker rebates, the trading interface will display your applicable Taker fee rate (determined by your volume tier or marker volume percentage) and a Maker fee of "0". Please note that our system calculates and disburses Maker rebates every hour based on the published fee schedule. These rebates can be tracked in the transaction history under Aster Perpetual.

3\. MM Reward Pool

*   Monthly Allocation: **300,000 USDT worth of the $ASTER** token supply.
    
*   Distribution Basis: Proportional to each MM’s altcoin pair effective maker volume contribution in a given calendar month.
    

Note: Aster reserves the right to evaluate the effect of the MM rewards pool program on a monthly basis and take appropriate actions such as adjusting or suspending the rewards pool.

4\. Calculation Methodology

Effective Maker Volume Weighting

MM’s Weighted Effective Volume = MM’s qualified Hot Pair maker volume \* Hot pair Weighted Index + MM’s qualified Normal Pair maker volume \* Normal Pair Weighted Index

Each MM’s Reward Share = MM’s Weighted Effective Volume / Total Weighted Effective Volume x Reward Pool

Type

Weighted Index

Hot Pair (H)

10

Normal Pair (N)

1

A maker’s volume for a given trading pair is counted as effective only if the following two conditions are met:

A. Quoting Standards:

*   Bid and Offer sizes meet or exceed the minimum size requirement for the pairs
    
*   Bid-Offer Spread is within the allowed limit (e.g., ≤0.1% for BTC/ETH/SOL, ≤0.25% for other pairs).
    
*   Orders remain live in the orderbook for at least 0.5 seconds at a time.
    

B. Qualifying Percentage for that Pair on the Day (from 00:00 to 23:59 UTC):

*   The pair is only counted if the MM maintains these standards for ≥70% of that trading day.
    
*   If \[Qualifying %\] < 70%, that pair's volume is excluded from the MM’s effective maker volume.
    

Kindly refer to 5. Quoting Qualification Details for supported pairs.

5\. Quoting Qualification Details and Pair Type

Note: If a pair’s \[Qualifying Percentage\] < 70%, this pair does not qualify for preferential fees on the next day. Preferential fees will only be awarded to qualified pairs.

In order to qualify for a particular pair in a day, MMs must satisfy the following conditions simultaneously at least 70% of the day (0:00 UTC to 23:59 UTC) :

*   Total Bids shown > Cumulative Minimum Size;
    
*   Total Offers shown > Cumulative Minimum Size;
    
*   Orders must be outstanding in the order book for at least 0.5 seconds;
    
*   The Bid/Offer spread is calculated as( \[Offer price at Minimum Size\] - \[Bid price at Minimum Size\]) / { (\[Offer price at Minimum Size\] + \[Bid price at Minimum Size\]) /2 } < \[Required Bid/Offer spread\].

     mode (orderbook trading) to earn Rh points and qualify for the $AST airdrop. Additional rewards include potential Rh point boosts and BONUSUSD. _Last updated: April 10, 2025_

# Au Trader Boost | Aster

**Important Notice: The Au Points Program is ending with a final snapshot of Au points balance taken at 00:00 UTC, June 13 2025.**

**Page Summary:**

[A. What is Au Trader Boost?](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/au-trader-boost#a.-what-is-au-trader-boost)

[Au Trader Boost](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/au-trader-boost#b.-au-trader-boost-tiers)

[C. Au Points Calculation](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/au-trader-boost#c.-au-points-calculation)

* * *

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/au-trader-boost#a.-what-is-au-trader-boost)

A. What is Au Trader Boost?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Recap: Au = Airdrop points you earn by minting and holding eligible assets. Rh = Airdrop points you earn by trading perps on Aster Pro mode.

**Au Trader Boost** is an incentive to encourage minters to trade on Aster Pro mode. Aside from earning Rh points, you may get an Au Trader Boost for your asset holdings if you hit certain trading volume criteria!

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/au-trader-boost#b.-au-trader-boost-tiers-new-adjustment-on-21-may)

B. Au Trader Boost Tiers (New adjustment on 21 May)


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Total Trading Vol on Aster Pro in a day

Au Trader Boost (Adjust on 12 May)

New adjustment on 21 May

≥ 10k

2x

+1x

≥ 50k

2.4x

+2x

≥ 200k

2.6x

+2.5x

≥ 500k

3x

+3x

To calculate your Pro mode trading volume, use this formula: **Pro taker volume + (Pro maker volume\*0.5)**

For example, Alice conducted trades on Aster Pro on Monday, reaching a total trading volume of 50k. On Tuesday 00:00 UTC+0, the system calculates Alice's Pro mode trading volume and verifies that it corresponds to an Au Trader Boost of 2x. This boost will be reflected in Alice's airdrop dashboard and Alice receives an additional 2x boost on her Au points at 00:05 UTC+0 on Tuesday.

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/au-trader-boost#c.-au-points-calculation)

C. Au Points Calculation


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The formula for calculating Au points is:

**Au = SUM( holding\_token\_USD\_value \* token\_AU\_multiplier ) \* (team boost + Trader boost) + ref bonus**

*   **Au** is the total airdrop points you get from minting and holding assets
    
*   **holding\_token\_USD\_value** refers to the USD investment of your underlying asset. For example, if you stake 0.5 BNB when BNB price is $670, your holding\_token\_USD\_value is 0.5 x 670.
    
*   **token\_AU\_multiplier** is the Au multiplier of the asset. For example, asBNB has a 5x Au multiplier.
    
*   **team boost** is the boost leverage of your team.
    
*   **Trader Boost** is the additional Au boost you earn from trading on Aster Pro mode.
    
*   **ref bonus** is the total Au points you have earned from your Tier 1 and 2 referrals.
    

Check your Au Trader Boost on the airdrop dashboard:

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F3XKi4rjOzpsZYx4QonOq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6815f177-179b-4f06-bd43-f6fc462ee141&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3b2cca67&sv=2)

# Trade like a Pro, Earn like a Pro | Aster

**Important Notice:**

*   The Stage 1 Rh Points Program has ended with Epoch 21 on June 22, 2025, 23:59 UTC+0, and distribution of Stage 1 Rh points has stopped. Stage 2 incentives will be announced in due time. [Read more](https://x.com/Aster_DEX/status/1935669044600082686)
    . _Last updated: June 23, 2025_
    

* * *

**Page Summary:** [1\. Why Pro Mode?](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/trade-like-a-pro-earn-like-a-pro#id-1.-why-pro-mode)
 [2\. Rh Points Calculation](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/trade-like-a-pro-earn-like-a-pro#id-2.-rh-points-calculation)
 [3\. FAQ](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/trade-like-a-pro-earn-like-a-pro#id-3.-faq)
 [4\. Terms & Conditions](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/trade-like-a-pro-earn-like-a-pro#id-4.-terms-and-conditions)

In the **Trade like a Pro, Earn like a Pro** program, earn Rh points in each Aster Stage 1 weekly epoch when you trade perpetuals on Aster Pro Mode. Refer friends, form teams and boost Rh!

Currently, **there is no fixed $ASTER token allocation percentage for each weekly epoch** in the Trade Like a Pro, Earn like a Pro program**.** This is termed 'blind mining' and each epoch's allocation will be determined at Aster's discretion.

*   Only trades on Aster Pro Mode via the Aster website earn Rh points.
    
*   You may qualify for extra rewards: 1.1x Rh points boost AND/OR 100 BonusUSD trading bonus. Remember to claim them before trading.
    

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/trade-like-a-pro-earn-like-a-pro#id-1.-why-pro-mode)

1\. Why Pro Mode?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Pro mode introduces an advanced order book interface with deep liquidity, up to 100x leverage and advanced trading tools. It doesn’t just provide a CEX-like experience; Pro mode’s fees are even lower than CEXs!

*   Fees: Maker 0.01%, Taker 0.035%
    
*   Multi-assets mode: Trade perps using different cryptocurrency assets as collateral
    
*   Referral program: 20% commission, with a tiered system in the works
    
*   Airdrop points: Trading on Pro mode earn you Rh points for the upcoming $AST airdrop
    

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/trade-like-a-pro-earn-like-a-pro#id-2.-rh-points-calculation)

2\. Rh Points Calculation


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

An epoch lasts one week, from Monday 00:00 UTC+0 to Sunday 23:59 UTC+0. Only the first epoch differs: Wednesday, 10 Apr. to Sunday, 13 Apr. 23:59 UTC+0.

Only trades on Aster Pro mode via the Aster website earn Rh points. Trades on Aster Simple mode (on-chain trading) and Dumb Mode do not earn Rh points. Your Rh balance updates every hour.

**Formula: Rh = \[Pro taker\_vol + (Pro maker\_vol\*0.5)\]\*(team boost + user\_Rh\_boost) + ref bonus**

For example:

*   If Alice’s taker\_vol is $100, maker\_vol is $200, and Alice has no team boost, Alice’s Rh = \[100 + (200\*0.5)\] = 200 Rh
    
*   If Alice’s taker\_vol is $100, maker\_vol is $200, and Alice has a team boost of 1.1x, Alice’s Rh = \[100 + (200\*0.5)\]\*(1.1) = 220 Rh
    

Note: Each trading pair has a minimum trading order size. Depending on the leverage selected, you will need a corresponding minimum principal. Please choose your leverage accordingly.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdIlC-HmJnFOM138P9gkEm_UkOVhAE56QZM1yUyxNhEUY_5jS_9vwaS0t-6xu6gMGZRXwtvP0xdC8NNK93lGd6pwHPdBtlWa8tSnmVsOWOaqJazjADgfgoVQ78kaGBQkBcIPzBQ%3Fkey%3Dxma8o7QrK4dbPiaixZMZQ3rV&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7d587328&sv=2)

Your airdrop allocation from Rh points is determined by your Rh weightage in each epoch: **Your Rh weightage = sum(your total Rh in this epoch / all Rh in this epoch)**

[![Logo](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstatic.asterindex.com%2Fcloud-futures%2Fstatic%2Fimages%2Fdex%2Faster%2Faster-favicon.png&width=20&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cd2929c9&sv=2)92,481.8 | BTCUSDT | Trade | AsterAstherus](https://www.asterdex.com/en/futures/v1/BTCUSDT)

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/trade-like-a-pro-earn-like-a-pro#id-3.-faq)

3\. FAQ


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**What are Au points?**

Au points are Aster airdrop points for minting and holding eligible assets. Enjoy up to 20x Au multiplier when you mint and hold asTokens, USDF, ALP and eligible LP tokens. To see individual asset multipliers, please refer to [https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn](https://www.asterdex.com/en/earn)
.

Your USD asset value is verified hourly and Au points stack hourly. For example, if you earned 100 Au points in the first hour, you would have 2400 Au points after 24 hours. Check your Au balance on the Aster airdrop dashboard.

**What are Rh points?**

Rh points are Aster airdrop points for trading on Aster Pro mode (Aster Simple mode and Dumb mode do not earn Rh points). To calculate your Rh points for each trade, refer to section 2. Rh Points Calculation.

Your Pro mode trading volume is verified hourly. However, unlike Au points, Rh points do not stack hourly. Check your Rh balance on the Aster airdrop dashboard.

**How can I boost my Au and Rh points?**

Boost your airdrop points when your friends bind your invite code before their first mint or trade. By forming a team, you and your friends can earn up to 1.2x points boost.

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/trade-like-a-pro-earn-like-a-pro#id-4.-terms-and-conditions)

4\. Terms & Conditions


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Market makers cannot earn Rh points.
    
*   After the end of each epoch, Aster may adjust Trade like a Pro, Earn like a Pro (the 'Activity') rules according to trader feedback and market conditions. Rh points will be released non-linearly.
    
*   Only traders who meet all the requirements are considered qualified.
    
*   The 1.1x Rh points boost and BonusUSD reward are limited to one entry per trader. Bot registered accounts will not be eligible for rewards.
    
*   Aster reserves the right to disqualify trades that are deemed to be wash trades, displaying attributes of market manipulation, bulk-account registrations to farm additional bonuses or any other attempts at fraud.
    
*   Aster reserves the right to cancel or amend any Activity or Activity Rules at our sole discretion.
    
*   Aster reserves the right of final interpretation of this Activity.
    

Risk Warning: Perpetual trading carries a substantial risk. All trading activities are done at your discretion and at your own risk. The information here should not be regarded as financial or investment advice from Aster. Aster will not be liable for any loss that might arise from your use of Aster.

E. Au Points Calculation


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We take hourly snapshots to calculate Au points. Check your Au points on the [S1 Landing Page](https://www.asterdex.com/en/stage1/team)
. There is an hourly cap of 100M Au points per address in Stage 1 (Does not include team boost and ref bonus).

**The formula for calculating Au points is:**

**Au = SUM( holding\_token\_USD\_value \* token\_AU\_multiplier ) \* (team boost + Trader boost) + ref bonus**

*   **Au** is the total airdrop points you get from minting and holding assets
    
*   **holding\_token\_USD\_value** refers to the USD investment of your underlying asset. For example, if you stake 0.5 BNB when BNB price is $670, your holding\_token\_USD\_value is 0.5 x 670.
    
*   **token\_AU\_multiplier** is the Au multiplier of the asset. For example, asBNB has a 5x Au multiplier.
    
*   **team boost** is the boost leverage of your team.
    
*   **Trader Boost** is the additional Au boost you earn from trading on Aster Pro mode.
    
*   **ref bonus** is the total Au points you have earned from your Tier 1 and 2 referrals.
    

Scenario:

If you stake 0.5 BNB when BNB price is $670, and asBNB Au multiplier is 5x, your mint earns (0.5 x 670 x 5) = 1,675 Au.

If there is no change in BNB price, you will continue earning (0.5 x 670 x 5) Au per hour.

If BNB price later drops to $650, you will earn (0.5 x 650 x 5) Au per hour.

# Mark Price (Oracle) | Aster

**What is Mark Price?**

Mark Price is a reference price applied to calculate traders' unrealized profit and loss (PnL), to reduce unnecessary forced liquidations in an abnormally volatile market, and improve the stability of the contracts market. The Mark Price ensures fair and accurate pricing of perpetual contracts.

Ensuring the accurate calculation of unrealized PnL is crucial to avoid unnecessary liquidations. The Mark Price, a key component in determining liquidations, is heavily influenced by the Price Index.

**What is Price Index?**

The Price Index is a weighted average price calculated by considering prices from major spot markets like Binance, Huobi, and Kraken. This weighting system ensures that markets with higher trading volumes have a greater impact on the final index value.

As the Price Index is a representation of the fair value of the asset's spot price, we use this to calculate the Mark Price, which plays a crucial role in determining your unrealized PnL (profit or loss on open positions). It's important to note that your realized PnL (profit or loss on closed positions) is based on the actual market price at the time you close your position.

This formula calculates the Mark Price for a contract:

Mark Price = Median × (Price 1 , Price 2 , Contract Price)

whereby

*   _Price 1 = Price Index × (1 + Funding Rate × (Time to Next Funding Rate (h)/8 ))_
    
*   _Price 2 = Price Index + Moving Average (5-min basis)_
    
*   _Median: The middle price out of Price 1, Price 2, and the Contract Price is taken as the median. For example, if Price 1 < Price 2 < Contract Price, then Price 2 is taken as the Mark Price._
    
*   _Moving Average (5-min basis) = Moving Average (( Bid 1 + Ask 1) / 2 — Price Index), sampled every minute in 5-minute intervals._
    

When there is huge deviation in price sources or abnormal market conditions causing large differences between the Spot Price and the Mark Price, AstheEx may implement additional precautionary actions. For example, Price 2 may be taken directly as the Mark Price.

**Ensuring Price Stability**

Here are some safeguards AstherusEX employs against potential issues with spot market data.

*   Single Price Source Deviation: When the Last Price of a particular exchange deviates more than 5% from the Median Price of all price sources, the price weight of that exchange will be set to zero.
    
*   Multi Price Source Deviation: If the Last Price of more than one exchange shows a deviation greater than 5%, the Median Price of all price sources will be used as the index value instead of the weighted average.
    
*   Exchange Connectivity Problems: If we can’t access the data feed for an exchange that has had trades updated in the last 5 minutes, we can use price data from the last result to calculate the Price Index. If the trade data for an exchange has not been updated for 10 seconds, the weight of this exchange will be set to zero when calculating the weighted average.
    
*   Last Trade Price Protection: If the system encounters issues obtaining reliable data for the Price Index, it might affect contracts that solely rely on this index (single Price Index contracts). To prevent this from impacting your positions, we utilize the "Last Trade Price Protection" mechanism. This mechanism temporarily sets the Mark Price based on the last executed trade price for the specific contract. This ensures the system can still calculate your unrealized PnL and liquidation level, ultimately preventing unnecessary position closures.
    

Last updated 1 year ago

. A screen will pop up to prompt you to enter your invite code. Click \[Redeem invite code\]. Click \[Skip\] if you don’t have one.

3a. Au referral bonus


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Important notice: The Au Points Program is ending with a final snapshot of Au points balance taken at 00:00 UTC, June 13 2025.**

*   Tier 1 referral: Get 10% of your invitees’ Au points when they mint asTokens, USDF and/or ALP. **Your invitees must bind your invite code before their first mint**.
    
*   Tier 2 referral: Get 5% when your invitees refer their friends to mint asTokens, USDF and/or ALP. **Your invitee’s friends must bind your invitee’s code before their first mint**.
    

**Scenario:**

Alice invites Ben. Ben binds Alice’s invite code.

*   Ben earns 5,000 Au from his first mint.
    
*   Alice earns 10% of Ben’s points. Thus, she gets 5,000\*0.1 = 500 Au.
    

Ben invites Charlie to Aster. Charlie binds Ben’s invite code.

*   Charlie earns 2,500 Au from his first mint.
    
*   Ben earns 10% of Charlie’s points. Thus, he gets 2,500\*0.1 = 250 Au.
    
*   Alice earns 5% of Charlie’s points. Thus, she gets 2,500\*0.05 = 125 Au.

3b. Au team boost


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Important notice: The Au Points Program is ending with a final snapshot of Au points balance taken at 00:00 UTC, June 13 2025.**

Everyone in a referral family is a Team. Teams can enjoy team boosts. A team is composed of the following members:

*   **The person who invited you (A)**
    
*   **Other invitees of the person who invited you (B)**
    
*   **Yourself (C)**
    
*   **Your invitees (D)**
    

For example, Alice invited you and Don to Aster. You invited Charlie. Charlie invited Evan. Hence, Alice is A. Don is B. You are C. Charlie is D. Evan is not included in your Team.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/referral-bonus-and-team-boosts#eabd)

Team boost scenario:

Team boosts are applied to the **team’s cumulative Au from minting asTokens, USDF and ALP only in the previous hour**. Hourly snapshots are taken to calculate Team Au points. Au earned from referral bonuses or previous team boosts are not included in the total Au amount.

For example:

Alice, Ben and Don are a team. In the previous hour, Alice earned 500,000 Au, Ben earned 300,000 Au and Don earned 200,000 Au. These Au points are earned from minting asTokens, USDF and ALP only. Au earned from their referral bonuses or previous team boosts are not counted.

Team Au in the previous hour = 500,000 + 300,000 + 200,000 = 1,000,000 Au

According to the table below, all members benefit from a 1.05x team boost.

Alice gets 500,000\*1.05 = 525,000 Au. Ben gets 300,000\*1.05 = 315,000 Au. Dion gets 200,000\*1.05 = 210,000 Au.

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/referral-bonus-and-team-boosts#id-6511)

Wyn invites Yuki to trade on Aster Pro Mode. Yuki binds Wyn’s invite code.

4b. Rh team boost


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Everyone in a referral family is a team. Teams can enjoy team boosts. A team is composed of the following members:

*   **The person who invited you (A)**
    
*   **Other invitees of the person who invited you (B)**
    
*   **Yourself (C )**
    
*   **Your invitees (D)**
    

For example: Yuki invited you and Wyn to Aster. You invited Zen, and Zen invited Ben.

*   Yuki = A
    
*   Wyn = B
    
*   You = C
    
*   Zen = D
    
*   Ben is not part of your team because he is a referral of your referral (second level).
    

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/referral-bonus-and-team-boosts#how-team-boosts-work)

How team boosts work

*   Team boosts are based on the team’s cumulative Rh earned from trading on Aster Pro in the previous day.
    
*   Daily snapshots are taken to calculate team Rh points.
    
*   Rh from referral bonuses or previous team boosts are not included.
    

**Example**

Wyn, Yuki, and Zen are a team. On the previous day, they earned:

*   Wyn: 600,000 Rh
    
*   Yuki: 300,000 Rh
    
*   Zen: 100,000 Rh
    

Team Rh = 600,000 + 300,000 + 100,000 = 1,000,000 Rh

According to the boost table, the team qualifies for a 1.05x boost, applied equally to each member’s Rh:

*   Wyn: 600,000 × 1.05 = 630,000 Rh
    
*   Yuki: 300,000 × 1.05 = 315,000 Rh
    
*   Zen: 100,000 × 1.05 = 105,000 Rh

# Treasure Boost Campaign | Aster

We've launched the Treasure Boost campaign for Hyperliquid, GMX, and Drift users. Eligible users can receive either a 1.1x Rh boost **AND/OR** 100 BonusUSD.

**👉** [**Check your eligibility here**](https://www.asterdex.com/en/rewards)

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/treasure-boost-campaign#id-1.-do-you-qualify-for-extra-1.1x-rh-points-boost-and-or-bonususd)

1\. Do you qualify for extra 1.1x Rh points boost and/or BONUSUSD?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FCNPMAR8bXMBFVefYkBxg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9ebceb66-a782-4ce1-adaf-157a43b09685&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3b513683&sv=2)

**1.1x Rh points boost**:

*   The points boost is applicable for 30 days after claiming. It will apply to all Aster Pro mode trades made by your wallet.
    
*   For example, if you earned 1000 Rh points from your Pro mode trades, you will get 1000\*1.1 = 1100 Rh points after the boost.
    
*   If you also join a team with e.g. a 1.2x Rh boost, you will get 1000\*（1.2+0.1）= 1300 Rh points after the boost.
    

(If you don't qualify for the extra 1.1x Rh points boost, you can still get up to 1.2x Rh boost by joining a team. See [Referral Bonus & Team Boosts](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/referral-bonus-and-team-boosts)
)

**100 BonusUSD**:

*   _**BonusUSD is a unique bonus token on Aster which can be used as collateral when trading perpetuals on Aster Pro mode (BNB Chain).**_
    
*   _**Multi-assets mode has to be activated to use BonusUSD as collateral.**_
    
*   _**BonusUSD can only be used on Aster. It cannot be withdrawn.**_
    
*   _**Profits generated from trades using BonusUSD as collateral can be withdrawn.**_
    

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/treasure-boost-campaign#id-2.-how-to-claim-extra-1.1x-rh-points-boost-and-or-bonususd)

2\. How to claim extra 1.1x Rh points boost and/or BONUSUSD?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Go to the rewards claim page (coming soon) and connect your wallet. Click \[Claim Reward\] to check your eligibility and claim rewards.

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/stage-1-spectra/treasure-boost-campaign#id-3.-how-to-use-the-bonususd)

3\. How to use the BONUSUSD?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Aster has launched a futures bonus token (BONUSUSD) for users who trade on [Aster Pro Mode](https://www.asterdex.com/en/futures/v1/BTCUSDT)
. BONUSUSD is a futures bonus token issued by Aster. BONUSUSD is a unique USD-pegged token which traders can use as collateral to trade crypto futures on [Aster Pro Mode](https://www.asterdex.com/en/futures/v1/BTCUSDT)
!

_Note: BONUSUSD is a futures bonus token and cannot be withdrawn._ [_Multi-assets mode_](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/asterex-pro-mode/muti-single-asset-margin)
 _has to be activated to use BONUSUSD as collateral._

**How-to Guide**

Step 1: Go to Campaign page and connect your wallet. Click \[Claim Reward\] to check your eligibility and claim rewards.

Your BONUSUSD tokens will have been automatically credited to your balance after you claim the BONUSUSD manually.

Step 2: Go to the [Portfolio](https://www.asterdex.com/en/portfolio)
 and check your BONUSUSD balance.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252Fi175RG0UBR1bCafwt1hQ%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-04-09%252011.49.19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D61b87967-22b8-4b0d-aeb5-f1d7691a2f28&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a842c9f4&sv=2)

Step 3: (Skip this step if multi-asset mode is already enabled.) Enable [Multi-Assets Mode](https://docs.asterdex.com/product/asterex-pro-mode/muti-single-asset-margin)
 to use BONUSUSD as collateral. On the Aster Pro mode scroll down to ‘Margin Ratio’ & select \[Multi-Assets Mode\].

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252F2fQMS9hmvmRtLiiXf9bl%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-04-09%252011.51.26.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0620aff9-2fca-4b37-98b8-08a4c256818a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a5c646fc&sv=2)

Step 4: Choose the preferred perpetual contract from the dropdown list. Set your preferred leverage.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FD3GYGsEh9ZYasJu8gku7%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-04-09%252011.54.16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Debe03192-3d26-4fc2-8d84-ed6edc2fc335&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=74993da8&sv=2)

Step 5: Set your preferred order type. Aster Pro Mode offers Limit, Market, Stop Limit orders and Trailing Stop order.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FW78kc6RAOagPkg7DiWD8%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-04-09%252011.57.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4ff1b893-f5a7-48e9-9850-61b43c175368&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=352e713f&sv=2)

Step 6: Monitor your position(s) and close them based on your exit strategy. All your positions are listed in the \[Positions\] tab.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4068247257-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWhSHuKmgnGREbVb12PK2%252Fuploads%252FRj7efFgOK66LTiR9SAm5%252F%25E6%2588%25AA%25E5%25B1%258F2025-04-09%252011.59.07.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1bed715e-bc6e-4532-acf1-3d2bd3cc2ca9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=87c00e79&sv=2)

Last updated 7 months ago

# Trading Guide | Aster

Head over to [https://astherus.finance/en](https://astherus.finance/en)
 and select \[Trade Now\] to access our DEX trading landing page.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfWRfMRQmbyP8mP2SqtNzWEy_6OiqKZZ6fTes0H7Psa7QrQQZLREZvOaACcvB229Kl8TLBt4_RkBnZWeQZrpET4-kGn2IRecc2eJ2myAWfq-duie8_x81QAkzmPGKpTDIBnTAjk4n-95co-tfAT5F3OjWe_%3Fkey%3D6Kpdn8TohC6DnxRsU4h2fw&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d709346c&sv=2)

Below is the trading interface for AstherusEX.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXd9vmdTXreELDqfnXZjQ9wGDTpyS4_XW3V9RvpLne63Xgf8S-VWgA8Cm2_u3q8kHRXBuSNGFXrmRQPaAY3JrDwWCVB8dFCJaixXZiCkdpeHjT5BnY_Dsy7b-R00S9FxWD73Go8KxgY9cVRWtN0vcnACChVL%3Fkey%3D6Kpdn8TohC6DnxRsU4h2fw&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fb68e5e1&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/astherusex-orderbook-perp-guide/trading-guide#price-chart)

Price Chart

The Astherus candlestick price chart offers a dynamic way to track price trends. Whether you’re looking at intraday movements or longer-term data, you can easily switch between daily, weekly, or monthly views to suit your strategy.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXc8ylYiyxN3P7kvMc4lCHgWEb9SwDPd3HRZzpF1HYBeN-j8g__UQZ_b9iTSo2vF_0t2v6R-ayHKnTUUcbfFhe6WncDb1rOaE9yPy4Q0lKLROhAIi3n9j8jWwJ2Q7zoZl-6wNavADR53zmx1ylbUy-fOVyi_%3Fkey%3D6Kpdn8TohC6DnxRsU4h2fw&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eace32b&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/astherusex-orderbook-perp-guide/trading-guide#trade-sidebar)

Trade Sidebar

In the trade sidebar, you have full control over your trade settings. Here, you can select your preferred Asset mode and position mode from the dropdowns, and select your preferred order types to open a trade.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcjTmIDGbeLNkgaabfhunw_jo4dGmGxjxJ8dKUkz5ZjHYlKuBMCd4TFxvUk9kLBXk1gj1zvQscjYkVvkPz0Q5Mzrll4J6KlZ1DcNaq3Fc5eyybHmxxkyAt6SXNtXaPhte-vSQ1hiAsBAHxa6T0Sg-abyr4G%3Fkey%3D6Kpdn8TohC6DnxRsU4h2fw&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dd978f9d&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/astherusex-orderbook-perp-guide/trading-guide#order-book)

Order Book

The order book provides a snapshot of live market activity, showing the latest bids and asks. You can track prices, order sizes, and the total volume available at any given moment, helping you stay on top of the market.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcFKQXUrlG0NfgtF7CBphdvByMd04xqXmEsy9loAgdngpYVY6bfjwSm34OdlhI5LYsbOKMfxeacBI6W2APkV7pUuomXJUm3PZZL5GC4V33zjyv_65kPzTCRlBLOAqJA6_Aj2C6Ro2VSZwaAec-93cpYpKM%3Fkey%3D6Kpdn8TohC6DnxRsU4h2fw&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c0226e9c&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/astherusex-orderbook-perp-guide/trading-guide#position-overview)

Position Overview

This section keeps all your trading data front and center. Here, you can check your current positions, monitor active orders, and dive into your trade, order, and transaction history. You’ll also see detailed metrics like unrealized PnL, estimated liquidation price, and margin ratio. Need to close a position? You can do that right from this section with either a market or limit order.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcSizFJWwxFEMquCOisl4BRN6kgEONtC21Qyo0Mdiozodb7_6xKIbqs9L7SOYmR0qTzlvhA9TFB_KpsucPhdIUHgy9P0f3vEfHZgXRUccJD5KzMdlW6GFMUrtBnrH0ML5Ti0NK5z7IvyosjNwV1N06Z4uFa%3Fkey%3D6Kpdn8TohC6DnxRsU4h2fw&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=95559324&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.asterdex.com/astherusex-orderbook-perp-guide/trading-guide#margin-ratio-panel)

Margin Ratio Panel

The margin ratio panel helps you keep tabs on your account health. It shows your current margin ratio, maintenance margin, and account equity, calculated as Account equity + Unrealized PnL. If your margin ratio hits 100%, your positions will be liquidated—so it’s important to keep an eye on this panel.

![](https://docs.asterdex.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXc-Hnl7ddPoHx8PMKtIXGIZAL0sGbKVVpZ1vm92zMNmU-LdIbn2VBRZbkBUuioORyLHKfrrZwADgjq-_HdUp88QpesLopwqu7raLcMSZWdIFuKpdbGa42XLzdxZUAB1dwGL_iQHeV_LKG2LDo15lq6m9k-b%3Fkey%3D6Kpdn8TohC6DnxRsU4h2fw&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=81baba6&sv=2)
